===== FILE: app\api\save-profile\route.ts =====

    1| import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
    2| 
    3| import { createSupabaseClientWithAccessToken } from "@/lib/supabase";
    4| 
    5| type SaveProfileBody = {
    6|   currentSavings?: unknown;
    7|   monthlySavings?: unknown;
    8|   expectedReturn?: unknown;
    9|   targetAmount?: unknown;
   10|   timeHorizon?: unknown;
   11| 
   12|   // Also accept snake_case keys to match the DB schema.
   13|   current_savings?: unknown;
   14|   monthly_savings?: unknown;
   15|   expected_return?: unknown;
   16|   target_amount?: unknown;
   17|   time_horizon?: unknown;
   18| };
   19| 
   20| function asFiniteNumber(name: string, value: unknown): number {
   21|   if (typeof value !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(value)) {
   22|     throw new TypeError(`${name} must be a finite number`);
   23|   }
   24|   return value;
   25| }
   26| 
   27| export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
   28|   try {
   29|     const authHeader = req.headers.get("authorization") ?? "";
   30|     const match = authHeader.match(/^Bearer\s+(.+)$/i);
   31|     if (!match) {
   32|       return NextResponse.json(
   33|         { error: "Missing Authorization Bearer token" },
   34|         { status: 401 },
   35|       );
   36|     }
   37| 
   38|     const accessToken = match[1];
   39|     const supabase = createSupabaseClientWithAccessToken(accessToken);
   40|     if (!supabase) {
   41|       return NextResponse.json(
   42|         { error: "Supabase is not configured on the server" },
   43|         { status: 500 },
   44|       );
   45|     }
   46| 
   47|     const { data: userData, error: userError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
   48|     if (userError || !userData.user) {
   49|       return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 });
   50|     }
   51| 
   52|     let body: SaveProfileBody;
   53|     try {
   54|       body = (await req.json()) as SaveProfileBody;
   55|     } catch {
   56|       return NextResponse.json({ error: "Invalid JSON body" }, { status: 400 });
   57|     }
   58| 
   59|     const currentSavings = asFiniteNumber(
   60|       "currentSavings",
   61|       body.currentSavings ?? body.current_savings,
   62|     );
   63|     const monthlySavings = asFiniteNumber(
   64|       "monthlySavings",
   65|       body.monthlySavings ?? body.monthly_savings,
   66|     );
   67|     const expectedReturn = asFiniteNumber(
   68|       "expectedReturn",
   69|       body.expectedReturn ?? body.expected_return,
   70|     );
   71|     const targetAmount = asFiniteNumber(
   72|       "targetAmount",
   73|       body.targetAmount ?? body.target_amount,
   74|     );
   75|     const timeHorizon = asFiniteNumber(
   76|       "timeHorizon",
   77|       body.timeHorizon ?? body.time_horizon,
   78|     );
   79| 
   80|     const userId = userData.user.id;
   81| 
   82|     const { data, error } = await supabase
   83|       .from("financial_profiles")
   84|       .upsert(
   85|         {
   86|           user_id: userId,
   87|           current_savings: currentSavings,
   88|           monthly_savings: monthlySavings,
   89|           expected_return: expectedReturn,
   90|           target_amount: targetAmount,
   91|           time_horizon: timeHorizon,
   92|         },
   93|         { onConflict: "user_id" },
   94|       )
   95|       .select()
   96|       .single();
   97| 
   98|     if (error) {
   99|       return NextResponse.json(
  100|         { error: error.message },
  101|         { status: 500 },
  102|       );
  103|     }
  104| 
  105|     return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, profile: data }, { status: 200 });
  106|   } catch (e) {
  107|     const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Unexpected error";
  108|     const status = e instanceof TypeError ? 400 : 500;
  109|     return NextResponse.json({ error: message }, { status });
  110|   }
  111| }

===== FILE: app\auth\login\page.tsx =====

    1| "use client";
    2| 
    3| import { useState } from "react";
    4| import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
    5| 
    6| import { createSupabaseClient } from "@/lib/supabase";
    7| 
    8| export default function LoginPage() {
    9|   const router = useRouter();
   10| 
   11|   const [email, setEmail] = useState<string>("");
   12|   const [password, setPassword] = useState<string>("");
   13|   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
   14|   const [isSubmitting, setIsSubmitting] = useState<boolean>(false);
   15| 
   16|   async function onSubmit(e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) {
   17|     e.preventDefault();
   18|     setError(null);
   19| 
   20|     const supabase = createSupabaseClient();
   21|     if (!supabase) {
   22|       setError(
   23|         "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
   24|       );
   25|       return;
   26|     }
   27| 
   28|     setIsSubmitting(true);
   29|     try {
   30|       const { error: signInError } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
   31|         email,
   32|         password,
   33|       });
   34| 
   35|       if (signInError) {
   36|         setError(signInError.message);
   37|         return;
   38|       }
   39| 
   40|       router.replace("/");
   41|     } finally {
   42|       setIsSubmitting(false);
   43|     }
   44|   }
   45| 
   46|   const inputClassName =
   47|     "mt-1 w-full rounded-md border border-foreground/20 bg-background px-3 py-2 text-foreground outline-none focus:border-foreground/40";
   48| 
   49|   return (
   50|     <div className="min-h-screen bg-background text-foreground">
   51|       <main className="mx-auto w-full max-w-md px-6 py-12">
   52|         <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold">Log in</h1>
   53| 
   54|         <form onSubmit={onSubmit} className="mt-8 space-y-4">
   55|           <div>
   56|             <label htmlFor="email" className="block text-sm font-medium">
   57|               Email
   58|             </label>
   59|             <input
   60|               id="email"
   61|               name="email"
   62|               type="email"
   63|               autoComplete="email"
   64|               value={email}
   65|               onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
   66|               className={inputClassName}
   67|               required
   68|             />
   69|           </div>
   70| 
   71|           <div>
   72|             <label htmlFor="password" className="block text-sm font-medium">
   73|               Password
   74|             </label>
   75|             <input
   76|               id="password"
   77|               name="password"
   78|               type="password"
   79|               autoComplete="current-password"
   80|               value={password}
   81|               onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
   82|               className={inputClassName}
   83|               required
   84|             />
   85|           </div>
   86| 
   87|           {error ? (
   88|             <div className="rounded-md border border-foreground/15 p-3">
   89|               <p className="text-sm">{error}</p>
   90|             </div>
   91|           ) : null}
   92| 
   93|           <button
   94|             type="submit"
   95|             disabled={isSubmitting}
   96|             className="w-full rounded-md border border-foreground/20 bg-background px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-foreground hover:border-foreground/40 disabled:opacity-60"
   97|           >
   98|             {isSubmitting ? "Logging in…" : "Login"}
   99|           </button>
  100|         </form>
  101| 
  102|         <p className="mt-6 text-sm text-foreground/70">
  103|           Don&apos;t have an account?{" "}
  104|           <a href="/auth/signup" className="text-foreground underline">
  105|             Sign up
  106|           </a>
  107|         </p>
  108|       </main>
  109|     </div>
  110|   );
  111| }

===== FILE: app\page.tsx =====

    1| "use client";
    2| 
    3| import { useCallback, useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
    4| import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
    5| 
    6| import InputForm, { type FinancialInputs } from "@/components/InputForm";
    7| import DebugPanel from "@/components/DebugPanel";
    8| import CauseCard from "@/components/CauseCard";
    9| import InsightCard from "@/components/InsightCard";
   10| import ImprovementSuggestions from "@/components/ImprovementSuggestions";
   11| import LeverSuggestion from "@/components/LeverSuggestion";
   12| import ProjectionGraph from "@/components/ProjectionGraph";
   13| import ScenarioSimulator from "@/components/ScenarioSimulator";
   14| import TrajectoryStatus from "@/components/TrajectoryStatus";
   15| import ReturnInsight from "@/components/ReturnInsight";
   16| import MarketScenarios from "@/components/MarketScenarios";
   17| import { analyzeTrajectory, type TrajectoryAnalysis } from "@/services/trajectoryService";
   18| import {
   19|   createSupabaseClient,
   20|   getFinancialProfile,
   21|   saveFinancialProfile,
   22| } from "@/lib/supabase";
   23| 
   24| type ResultState = TrajectoryAnalysis | null;
   25| 
   26| function formatNumber(value: number): string {
   27|   return new Intl.NumberFormat(undefined, { maximumFractionDigits: 2 }).format(
   28|     value,
   29|   );
   30| }
   31| 
   32| export default function Home() {
   33|   const router = useRouter();
   34| 
   35|   const SHOW_DEBUG_PANEL = true;
   36| 
   37|   const [result, setResult] = useState<ResultState>(null);
   38|   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
   39|   const [inputs, setInputs] = useState<FinancialInputs | null>(null);
   40|   const [isAuthChecked, setIsAuthChecked] = useState<boolean>(false);
   41|   const didAutoRunFromProfile = useRef<boolean>(false);
   42| 
   43|   useEffect(() => {
   44|     let cancelled = false;
   45| 
   46|     void (async () => {
   47|       const supabase = createSupabaseClient();
   48|       if (!supabase) {
   49|         if (!cancelled) {
   50|           setError(
   51|             "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
   52|           );
   53|         }
   54|         return;
   55|       }
   56| 
   57|       const { data, error: sessionError } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
   58|       if (cancelled) return;
   59| 
   60|       if (sessionError || !data.session) {
   61|         router.replace("/auth/login");
   62|         return;
   63|       }
   64| 
   65|       setIsAuthChecked(true);
   66|     })();
   67| 
   68|     return () => {
   69|       cancelled = true;
   70|     };
   71|   }, [router]);
   72| 
   73|   async function handleLogout() {
   74|     const supabase = createSupabaseClient();
   75|     if (!supabase) {
   76|       setError(
   77|         "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
   78|       );
   79|       return;
   80|     }
   81| 
   82|     const { error: signOutError } = await supabase.auth.signOut();
   83|     if (signOutError) {
   84|       setError(signOutError.message);
   85|       return;
   86|     }
   87| 
   88|     router.replace("/auth/login");
   89|   }
   90| 
   91|   const handleSubmit = useCallback((values: FinancialInputs) => {
   92|     try {
   93|       setError(null);
   94| 
   95|       // UI inputs are percent; analysis service expects decimal.
   96|       const engineInputs = {
   97|         currentSavings: values.currentSavings,
   98|         monthlySavings: values.monthlySavings,
   99|         expectedReturn: values.expectedReturn / 100,
  100|         targetAmount: values.targetAmount,
  101|         timeHorizon: values.timeHorizon,
  102|       };
  103| 
  104|       const analysis = analyzeTrajectory(engineInputs);
  105|       setResult(analysis);
  106| 
  107|       setInputs(values);
  108| 
  109|       // Persist inputs for the authenticated user.
  110|       // Store expected_return as a decimal rate (engine format).
  111|       void saveFinancialProfile({
  112|         current_savings: values.currentSavings,
  113|         monthly_savings: values.monthlySavings,
  114|         expected_return: engineInputs.expectedReturn,
  115|         target_amount: values.targetAmount,
  116|         time_horizon: values.timeHorizon,
  117|       }).catch((err: unknown) => {
  118|         setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : "Failed to save profile");
  119|       });
  120|     } catch (e) {
  121|       setResult(null);
  122|       setInputs(null);
  123|       setError(e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Calculation failed");
  124|     }
  125|   }, []);
  126| 
  127|   useEffect(() => {
  128|     if (!isAuthChecked) return;
  129|     if (didAutoRunFromProfile.current) return;
  130| 
  131|     let cancelled = false;
  132| 
  133|     void (async () => {
  134|       try {
  135|         const profile = await getFinancialProfile();
  136|         if (!profile || cancelled) return;
  137| 
  138|         // expected_return is stored as a decimal, but the form takes % input.
  139|         const loadedInputs: FinancialInputs = {
  140|           currentSavings: Number(profile.current_savings),
  141|           monthlySavings: Number(profile.monthly_savings),
  142|           expectedReturn: Number(profile.expected_return) * 100,
  143|           targetAmount: Number(profile.target_amount),
  144|           timeHorizon: Number(profile.time_horizon),
  145|         };
  146| 
  147|         // Ensure inputs state reflects the loaded profile immediately.
  148|         setInputs(loadedInputs);
  149| 
  150|         // Immediately run the same calculation pipeline as manual submit.
  151|         didAutoRunFromProfile.current = true;
  152|         handleSubmit(loadedInputs);
  153|       } catch {
  154|         // Silently ignore load errors for now; the user can still use the form.
  155|       }
  156|     })();
  157| 
  158|     return () => {
  159|       cancelled = true;
  160|     };
  161|   }, [handleSubmit, isAuthChecked]);
  162| 
  163|   if (!isAuthChecked) {
  164|     return (
  165|       <div className="min-h-screen bg-background text-foreground">
  166|         <main className="mx-auto w-full max-w-2xl px-6 py-10">
  167|           <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold">Trajectos</h1>
  168|           <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-foreground/70">Loading…</p>
  169|           {error ? (
  170|             <div className="mt-6 rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-4">
  171|               <p className="text-sm">{error}</p>
  172|             </div>
  173|           ) : null}
  174|         </main>
  175|       </div>
  176|     );
  177|   }
  178| 
  179|   return (
  180|     <div className="min-h-screen bg-background text-foreground">
  181|       <main className="mx-auto w-full max-w-2xl px-6 py-10">
  182|         <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-4">
  183|           <div>
  184|             <h1 className="text-2xl font-semibold">Trajectos</h1>
  185|             <p className="text-xs text-foreground/50 mt-1">
  186|               Version 0.1 — Experimental
  187|             </p>
  188|           </div>
  189|           <button
  190|             type="button"
  191|             onClick={handleLogout}
  192|             className="rounded-md border border-foreground/20 bg-background px-3 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-foreground hover:border-foreground/40"
  193|           >
  194|             Logout
  195|           </button>
  196|         </div>
  197|         <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-foreground/70">
  198|           Enter inputs to project value and schedule.
  199|         </p>
  200| 
  201|         <section className="mt-8">
  202|           <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Financial Profile</h2>
  203|           <div className="mt-3 rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-5">
  204|             <InputForm
  205|               onSubmit={handleSubmit}
  206|               initialValues={inputs ?? undefined}
  207|             />
  208|           </div>
  209|         </section>
  210| 
  211|         {error ? (
  212|           <div className="mt-6 rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-4">
  213|             <p className="text-sm">{error}</p>
  214|           </div>
  215|         ) : null}
  216| 
  217| 
  218|         {result ? (
  219|           <section className="mt-8">
  220|             <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Trajectory Analysis</h2>
  221|             <div className="mt-3 rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-4">
  222|               <div className="text-sm">
  223|                 <p>
  224|                   Projected future value: {formatNumber(result.projectedFutureValue)}
  225|                 </p>
  226|                 <p>Years to reach target: {formatNumber(result.nActual)}</p>
  227|                 <p>
  228|                   {result.compression === 0
  229|                     ? "You are on track for your target"
  230|                     : (() => {
  231|                         const months = Math.round(
  232|                           Math.abs(result.compression * 12),
  233|                         );
  234|                         return result.compression < 0
  235|                           ? `You are ${months} months behind your target`
  236|                           : `You are ${months} months ahead of your target`;
  237|                       })()}
  238|                 </p>
  239|                 <p className="mt-2">
  240|                   Inflation shock adds {formatNumber(result.shock.monthsAdded)}
  241|                   months to your timeline.
  242|                 </p>
  243|               </div>
  244|             </div>
  245| 
  246|             <ReturnInsight message={result.returnInsight.message} />
  247|           </section>
  248|         ) : null}
  249| 
  250|         {result && inputs ? (
  251|           <section className="mt-8">
  252|             <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Trajectory Diagnosis</h2>
  253| 
  254|             <div className="mt-3">
  255|               <TrajectoryStatus accelerationScore={result.accelerationScore} />
  256|             </div>
  257| 
  258|             <InsightCard title={result.insight.title} message={result.insight.message} />
  259| 
  260|             <CauseCard primary={result.cause.primary} secondary={result.cause.secondary} />
  261| 
  262|             <div className="rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-4 mt-6">
  263|               <p className="text-sm font-medium">
  264|                 Acceleration Score: {formatNumber(result.accelerationScore)}
  265|               </p>
  266|               <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-foreground/70">
  267|                 {result.accelerationScore > 1
  268|                   ? "You are accelerating ahead of your target"
  269|                   : result.accelerationScore === 1
  270|                     ? "You are exactly on track"
  271|                     : "You are below the required pace"}
  272|               </p>
  273|             </div>
  274|           </section>
  275|         ) : null}
  276| 
  277|         {result ? (
  278|           <section className="mt-8">
  279|             <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Improvement Plan</h2>
  280| 
  281|             {result.compression < 0 ? (
  282|               <ImprovementSuggestions suggestions={result.improvements} />
  283|             ) : null}
  284| 
  285|             <div className="mt-4">
  286|               <LeverSuggestion
  287|                 isBehind={result.compression < 0}
  288|                 increaseMonthlySavings={result.increaseMonthlySavings ?? undefined}
  289|               />
  290|             </div>
  291|           </section>
  292|         ) : null}
  293| 
  294|         {result && inputs ? (
  295|           <ScenarioSimulator scenarios={result.scenarios} />
  296|         ) : null}
  297| 
  298|         {result && inputs ? (
  299|           <MarketScenarios
  300|             marketScenarios={result.marketScenarios}
  301|             timeHorizon={inputs.timeHorizon}
  302|           />
  303|         ) : null}
  304| 
  305|         {result && inputs ? (
  306|           <section className="mt-8">
  307|             <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Projection</h2>
  308|             <div className="mt-3">
  309|               <ProjectionGraph
  310|                 PV={inputs.currentSavings}
  311|                 PMT={inputs.monthlySavings}
  312|                 r={inputs.expectedReturn / 100}
  313|                 n={inputs.timeHorizon}
  314|               />
  315|             </div>
  316| 
  317|             <div className="mt-4 rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-4">
  318|               <div className="text-xs font-semibold text-foreground/60">
  319|                 Assumptions
  320|               </div>
  321|               <p className="mt-2 text-xs text-foreground/60">
  322|                 This projection assumes an average annual return equal to the
  323|                 expected return entered above. Actual investment performance may
  324|                 vary depending on market conditions and investment choices.
  325|               </p>
  326|             </div>
  327|           </section>
  328|         ) : null}
  329| 
  330|         {SHOW_DEBUG_PANEL && result && inputs ? (
  331|           <DebugPanel
  332|             inputs={{
  333|               currentSavings: inputs.currentSavings,
  334|               monthlySavings: inputs.monthlySavings,
  335|               expectedReturn: inputs.expectedReturn / 100,
  336|               targetAmount: inputs.targetAmount,
  337|               timeHorizon: inputs.timeHorizon,
  338|             }}
  339|             result={{
  340|               projectedFutureValue: result.projectedFutureValue,
  341|               nActual: result.nActual,
  342|               compression: result.compression,
  343|               accelerationScore: result.accelerationScore,
  344|             }}
  345|           />
  346|         ) : null}
  347|       </main>
  348|     </div>
  349|   );
  350| }

   35|     1| import { NextResponse, type NextRequest } from "next/server";
   36|     2| 
   37|     3| import { createSupabaseClientWithAccessToken } from "@/lib/supabase";
   38|     4| 
   39|     5| type SaveProfileBody = {
   40|     6|   currentSavings?: unknown;
   41|     7|   monthlySavings?: unknown;
   42|     8|   expectedReturn?: unknown;
   43|     9|   targetAmount?: unknown;
   44|    10|   timeHorizon?: unknown;
   45|    11| 
   46|    12|   // Also accept snake_case keys to match the DB schema.
   47|    13|   current_savings?: unknown;
   48|    14|   monthly_savings?: unknown;
   49|    15|   expected_return?: unknown;
   50|    16|   target_amount?: unknown;
   51|    17|   time_horizon?: unknown;
   52|    18| };
   53|    19| 
   54|    20| function asFiniteNumber(name: string, value: unknown): number {
   55|    21|   if (typeof value !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(value)) {
   56|    22|     throw new TypeError(`${name} must be a finite number`);
   57|    23|   }
   58|    24|   return value;
   59|    25| }
   60|    26| 
   61|    27| export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
   62|    28|   try {
   63|    29|     const authHeader = req.headers.get("authorization") ?? "";
   64|    30|     const match = authHeader.match(/^Bearer\s+(.+)$/i);
   65|    31|     if (!match) {
   66|    32|       return NextResponse.json(
   67|    33|         { error: "Missing Authorization Bearer token" },
   68|    34|         { status: 401 },
   69|    35|       );
   70|    36|     }
   71|    37| 
   72|    38|     const accessToken = match[1];
   73|    39|     const supabase = createSupabaseClientWithAccessToken(accessToken);
   74|    40|     if (!supabase) {
   75|    41|       return NextResponse.json(
   76|    42|         { error: "Supabase is not configured on the server" },
   77|    43|         { status: 500 },
   78|    44|       );
   79|    45|     }
   80|    46| 
   81|    47|     const { data: userData, error: userError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
   82|    48|     if (userError || !userData.user) {
   83|    49|       return NextResponse.json({ error: "Unauthorized" }, { status: 401 });
   84|    50|     }
   85|    51| 
   86|    52|     let body: SaveProfileBody;
   87|    53|     try {
   88|    54|       body = (await req.json()) as SaveProfileBody;
   89|    55|     } catch {
   90|    56|       return NextResponse.json({ error: "Invalid JSON body" }, { status: 400 });
   91|    57|     }
   92|    58| 
   93|    59|     const currentSavings = asFiniteNumber(
   94|    60|       "currentSavings",
   95|    61|       body.currentSavings ?? body.current_savings,
   96|    62|     );
   97|    63|     const monthlySavings = asFiniteNumber(
   98|    64|       "monthlySavings",
   99|    65|       body.monthlySavings ?? body.monthly_savings,
  100|    66|     );
  101|    67|     const expectedReturn = asFiniteNumber(
  102|    68|       "expectedReturn",
  103|    69|       body.expectedReturn ?? body.expected_return,
  104|    70|     );
  105|    71|     const targetAmount = asFiniteNumber(
  106|    72|       "targetAmount",
  107|    73|       body.targetAmount ?? body.target_amount,
  108|    74|     );
  109|    75|     const timeHorizon = asFiniteNumber(
  110|    76|       "timeHorizon",
  111|    77|       body.timeHorizon ?? body.time_horizon,
  112|    78|     );
  113|    79| 
  114|    80|     const userId = userData.user.id;
  115|    81| 
  116|    82|     const { data, error } = await supabase
  117|    83|       .from("financial_profiles")
  118|    84|       .upsert(
  119|    85|         {
  120|    86|           user_id: userId,
  121|    87|           current_savings: currentSavings,
  122|    88|           monthly_savings: monthlySavings,
  123|    89|           expected_return: expectedReturn,
  124|    90|           target_amount: targetAmount,
  125|    91|           time_horizon: timeHorizon,
  126|    92|         },
  127|    93|         { onConflict: "user_id" },
  128|    94|       )
  129|    95|       .select()
  130|    96|       .single();
  131|    97| 
  132|    98|     if (error) {
  133|    99|       return NextResponse.json(
  134|   100|         { error: error.message },
  135|   101|         { status: 500 },
  136|   102|       );
  137|   103|     }
  138|   104| 
  139|   105|     return NextResponse.json({ ok: true, profile: data }, { status: 200 });
  140|   106|   } catch (e) {
  141|   107|     const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : "Unexpected error";
  142|   108|     const status = e instanceof TypeError ? 400 : 500;
  143|   109|     return NextResponse.json({ error: message }, { status });
  144|   110|   }
  145|   111| }

  488|    46|     void (async () => {

  490|    48|       if (!supabase) {
  491|    49|         if (!cancelled) {
  492|    50|           setError(
  493|    51|             "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
  494|    52|           );
  495|    53|         }

  497|    55|       }

  516|    74|     const supabase = createSupabaseClient();
  517|    75|     if (!supabase) {
  518|    76|       setError(
  519|    77|         "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
  520|    78|       );
  521|    79|       return;

  531|    89|   }
  532|    90| 
  533|    91|   const handleSubmit = useCallback((values: FinancialInputs) => {
  534|    92|     try {
  535|    93|       setError(null);
  536|    94| 
  537|    95|       // UI inputs are percent; analysis service expects decimal.
  538|    96|       const engineInputs = {
  539|    97|         currentSavings: values.currentSavings,
  540|    98|         monthlySavings: values.monthlySavings,
  541|    99|         expectedReturn: values.expectedReturn / 100,
  542|   100|         targetAmount: values.targetAmount,

  548|   106| 
  549|   107|       setInputs(values);
  550|   108| 
  551|   109|       // Persist inputs for the authenticated user.
  552|   110|       // Store expected_return as a decimal rate (engine format).
  553|   111|       void saveFinancialProfile({
  554|   112|         current_savings: values.currentSavings,

    1| "use client";
    2| 
    3| import { useState } from "react";
    4| 
    5| type DebugInputs = {
    6|   currentSavings: number;
    7|   monthlySavings: number;
    8|   expectedReturn: number;
    9|   targetAmount: number;
   10|   timeHorizon: number;
   11| };
   12| 
   13| type DebugResult = {
   14|   projectedFutureValue: number;
   15|   nActual: number;
   16|   compression: number;
   17|   accelerationScore?: number;
   18| };
   19| 
   20| function formatNumber(value: number, decimals = 2) {
   21|   return Number(value.toFixed(decimals));
   22| }
   23| 
   24| export default function DebugPanel({
   25|   inputs,
   26|   result,
   27| }: {
   28|   inputs: DebugInputs;
   29|   result: DebugResult;
   30| }) {
   31|   const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
   32| 
   33|   const projectedFutureValueDisplay = formatNumber(
   34|     result.projectedFutureValue,
   35|     0,
   36|   );
   37|   const nActualDisplay = formatNumber(result.nActual, 2);
   38|   const compressionDisplay = formatNumber(result.compression, 2);
   39|   const accelerationScoreDisplay =
   40|     typeof result.accelerationScore === "number"
   41|       ? formatNumber(result.accelerationScore, 3)
   42|       : null;
   43| 
   44|   return (
   45|     <div className="mt-6">
   46|       <button
   47|         className="text-xs underline mb-2"
   48|         type="button"
   49|         onClick={() => setOpen(!open)}
   50|       >
   51|         {open ? "Hide Debug Panel" : "Show Debug Panel"}
   52|       </button>
   53| 
   54|       {open && (
   55|         <div className="border border-foreground/20 rounded-lg p-4 text-xs font-mono bg-foreground/5">
   56|           <div className="font-semibold">DEBUG PANEL</div>
   57| 
   58|           <div className="mt-3">
   59|             <div className="font-semibold">Inputs</div>
   60|             <div className="mt-1 space-y-0.5">
   61|               <div>PV: {inputs.currentSavings}</div>
   62|               <div>PMT: {inputs.monthlySavings}</div>
   63|               <div>Return: {inputs.expectedReturn}</div>
   64|               <div>Target: {inputs.targetAmount}</div>
   65|               <div>Horizon: {inputs.timeHorizon}</div>
   66|             </div>
   67|           </div>
   68| 
   69|           <div className="mt-3">
   70|             <div className="font-semibold">Engine Output</div>
   71|             <div className="mt-1 space-y-0.5">
   72|               <div>Projected FV: {projectedFutureValueDisplay}</div>
   73|               <div>Years to target: {nActualDisplay}</div>
   74|               <div>Compression: {compressionDisplay} years</div>
   75|             </div>
   76|           </div>
   77| 
   78|           {accelerationScoreDisplay !== null ? (
   79|             <div className="mt-3">
   80|               <div className="font-semibold">Acceleration Score</div>
   81|               <div className="mt-1">{accelerationScoreDisplay}</div>
   82|             </div>
   83|           ) : null}
   84|         </div>
   85|       )}
   86|     </div>
   87|   );
   88| }

===== FILE: components\ImprovementSuggestions.tsx =====

    1| import type { ImprovementSuggestion } from "@/engines/improvementEngine";
    2| 
    3| export default function ImprovementSuggestions({
    4|   suggestions,
    5| }: {
    6|   suggestions: ImprovementSuggestion[];
    7| }) {
    8|   if (suggestions.length === 0) return null;
    9| 
   10|   return (
   11|     <div className="border border-foreground/15 rounded-lg p-4 mt-4">
   12|       <div className="text-sm font-semibold">Suggested Improvements</div>
   13| 
   14|       <div className="mt-3 space-y-3">
   15|         {suggestions.map((s, index) => {
   16|           let rankLabel = "";
   17| 
   18|           if (index === 0) rankLabel = "Best Improvement";
   19|           else if (index === 1) rankLabel = "Alternative";
   20|           else rankLabel = "Minor Impact";
   21| 
   22|           return (
   23|             <div
   24|               key={s.type}
   25|               className="rounded-md border border-foreground/15 p-3"
   26|             >
   27|               <div className="text-xs font-semibold text-foreground/70">
   28|                 {rankLabel}
   29|               </div>
   30|               <div className="mt-2 text-sm font-medium">{s.label}</div>
   31|               <div className="mt-0.5 text-sm text-foreground/70">
   32|                 → Reach goal {s.monthsImproved} months earlier
   33|               </div>
   34|             </div>
   35|           );
   36|         })}
   37|       </div>
   38|     </div>
   39|   );
   40| }

    1| "use client";

    5| export type FinancialInputs = {

   14|   /** Called with validated numeric values when the form is submitted. */
   15|   onSubmit: (values: FinancialInputs) => void;
   16|   /** Optional initial values to pre-populate the form (e.g. loaded from persistence). */
   17|   initialValues?: Partial<FinancialInputs>;
   18| };
   19| 
   20| type FormState = {
   21|   currentSavings: string;
   22|   monthlySavings: string;
   23|   expectedReturn: string;
   24|   targetAmount: string;
   25|   timeHorizon: string;
   26| };
   27| 
   28| type FormErrors = Partial<Record<keyof FormState, string>>;
   29| 
   30| function parseFiniteNumber(raw: string): number | null {
   31|   // Treat empty/whitespace as invalid.
   32|   const trimmed = raw.trim();
   33|   if (trimmed.length === 0) return null;
   34| 
   35|   const value = Number(trimmed);
   36|   return Number.isFinite(value) ? value : null;
   37| }
   38| 
   39| export default function InputForm({ onSubmit, initialValues }: InputFormProps) {
   40|   const [form, setForm] = useState<FormState>({
   41|     currentSavings: "",
   42|     monthlySavings: "",
   43|     expectedReturn: "",
   44|     targetAmount: "",
   45|     timeHorizon: "",
   46|   });
   47| 
   48|   const [errors, setErrors] = useState<FormErrors>({});
   49| 
   50|   useEffect(() => {
   51|     if (!initialValues) return;
   52| 
   53|     setForm((prev) => ({
   54|       ...prev,
   55|       currentSavings:
   56|         initialValues.currentSavings === undefined
   57|           ? prev.currentSavings
   58|           : String(initialValues.currentSavings),
   59|       monthlySavings:
   60|         initialValues.monthlySavings === undefined
   61|           ? prev.monthlySavings
   62|           : String(initialValues.monthlySavings),
   63|       expectedReturn:
   64|         initialValues.expectedReturn === undefined
   65|           ? prev.expectedReturn
   66|           : String(initialValues.expectedReturn),
   67|       targetAmount:
   68|         initialValues.targetAmount === undefined
   69|           ? prev.targetAmount
   70|           : String(initialValues.targetAmount),
   71|       timeHorizon:
   72|         initialValues.timeHorizon === undefined
   73|           ? prev.timeHorizon
   74|           : String(initialValues.timeHorizon),
   75|     }));
   76|   }, [initialValues]);
   77| 
   78|   function updateField(field: keyof FormState, value: string) {
   79|     setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));
   80|   }
   81| 
   82|   function validate(): { values: FinancialInputs | null; errors: FormErrors } {
   83|     const nextErrors: FormErrors = {};
   84| 
   85|     const currentSavings = parseFiniteNumber(form.currentSavings);
   86|     const monthlySavings = parseFiniteNumber(form.monthlySavings);
   87|     // User enters a percentage (e.g. 10 for 10%).
   88|     // Conversion to decimal is handled by the dashboard before calling engine functions.
   89|     const expectedReturnPercent = parseFiniteNumber(form.expectedReturn);
   90|     const targetAmount = parseFiniteNumber(form.targetAmount);
   91|     const timeHorizon = parseFiniteNumber(form.timeHorizon);
   92| 
   93|     if (currentSavings === null) nextErrors.currentSavings = "Enter a valid number.";
   94|     if (monthlySavings === null) nextErrors.monthlySavings = "Enter a valid number.";
   95|     if (expectedReturnPercent === null) nextErrors.expectedReturn = "Enter a valid number.";
   96|     if (targetAmount === null) nextErrors.targetAmount = "Enter a valid number.";
   97|     if (timeHorizon === null) nextErrors.timeHorizon = "Enter a valid number.";
   98| 
   99|     if (timeHorizon !== null && timeHorizon < 0) {
  100|       nextErrors.timeHorizon = "Must be 0 or greater.";
  101|     }
  102| 
  103|     // Expected return is entered as a percentage (e.g. 10 for 10%). Enforce >= 0.
  104|     if (expectedReturnPercent !== null && expectedReturnPercent < 0) {
  105|       nextErrors.expectedReturn = "Must be 0 or greater.";
  106|     }
  107| 
  108|     const hasErrors = Object.keys(nextErrors).length > 0;
  109|     if (hasErrors) {
  110|       return { values: null, errors: nextErrors };
  111|     }
  112| 
  113|     return {
  114|       values: {
  115|         currentSavings: currentSavings!,
  116|         monthlySavings: monthlySavings!,
  117|         expectedReturn: expectedReturnPercent!,
  118|         targetAmount: targetAmount!,
  119|         timeHorizon: timeHorizon!,
  120|       },
  121|       errors: {},
  122|     };
  123|   }
  124| 
  125|   function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent<HTMLFormElement>) {
  126|     e.preventDefault();
  127| 
  128|     const result = validate();
  129|     setErrors(result.errors);
  130| 
  131|     if (result.values) {
  132|       onSubmit(result.values);
  133|     }
  134|   }
  135| 
  136|   const inputClassName =
  137|     "mt-1 w-full rounded-md border border-foreground/20 bg-background px-3 py-2 text-foreground outline-none focus:border-foreground/40";
  138| 
  139|   const errorClassName = "mt-1 text-sm text-foreground/70";
  140| 
  141|   return (
  142|     <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
  143|       <div>
  144|         <label htmlFor="currentSavings" className="block text-sm font-medium">
  145|           Current savings
  146|         </label>
  147|         <input
  148|           id="currentSavings"
  149|           name="currentSavings"
  150|           type="number"
  151|           inputMode="decimal"
  152|           step="any"
  153|           value={form.currentSavings}
  154|           onChange={(e) => updateField("currentSavings", e.target.value)}
  155|           className={inputClassName}
  156|         />
  157|         {errors.currentSavings ? <p className={errorClassName}>{errors.currentSavings}</p> : null}
  158|       </div>
  159| 
  160|       <div>
  161|         <label htmlFor="monthlySavings" className="block text-sm font-medium">
  162|           Monthly savings
  163|         </label>
  164|         <input
  165|           id="monthlySavings"
  166|           name="monthlySavings"
  167|           type="number"
  168|           inputMode="decimal"
  169|           step="any"
  170|           value={form.monthlySavings}
  171|           onChange={(e) => updateField("monthlySavings", e.target.value)}
  172|           className={inputClassName}
  173|         />
  174|         {errors.monthlySavings ? <p className={errorClassName}>{errors.monthlySavings}</p> : null}
  175|       </div>
  176| 
  177|       <div>
  178|         <label htmlFor="expectedReturn" className="block text-sm font-medium">
  179|           Expected Annual Return (%)
  180|         </label>
  181|         <input
  182|           id="expectedReturn"
  183|           name="expectedReturn"
  184|           type="number"
  185|           inputMode="decimal"
  186|           step="any"
  187|           value={form.expectedReturn}
  188|           onChange={(e) => updateField("expectedReturn", e.target.value)}
  189|           className={inputClassName}
  190|         />
  191|         {errors.expectedReturn ? <p className={errorClassName}>{errors.expectedReturn}</p> : null}
  192|       </div>
  193| 
  194|       <div>
  195|         <label htmlFor="targetAmount" className="block text-sm font-medium">
  196|           Target amount
  197|         </label>
  198|         <input
  199|           id="targetAmount"
  200|           name="targetAmount"
  201|           type="number"
  202|           inputMode="decimal"
  203|           step="any"
  204|           value={form.targetAmount}
  205|           onChange={(e) => updateField("targetAmount", e.target.value)}
  206|           className={inputClassName}
  207|         />
  208|         {errors.targetAmount ? <p className={errorClassName}>{errors.targetAmount}</p> : null}
  209|       </div>
  210| 
  211|       <div>
  212|         <label htmlFor="timeHorizon" className="block text-sm font-medium">
  213|           Time horizon (years)
  214|         </label>
  215|         <input
  216|           id="timeHorizon"
  217|           name="timeHorizon"
  218|           type="number"
  219|           inputMode="decimal"
  220|           step="any"
  221|           min={0}
  222|           value={form.timeHorizon}
  223|           onChange={(e) => updateField("timeHorizon", e.target.value)}
  224|           className={inputClassName}
  225|         />
  226|         {errors.timeHorizon ? <p className={errorClassName}>{errors.timeHorizon}</p> : null}
  227|       </div>
  228| 
  229|       <button
  230|         type="submit"
  231|         className="rounded-md border border-foreground/20 bg-background px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-foreground hover:border-foreground/40"
  232|       >
  233|         Calculate
  234|       </button>
  235|     </form>
  236|   );
  237| }

   10| function formatINR(value: number): string {
   11|   const safe = Number.isFinite(value) ? value : 0;
   12|   return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
   13|     style: "currency",
   14|     currency: "INR",
   15|     maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   16|   }).format(safe);
   17| }

===== FILE: components\ProjectionGraph.tsx =====

    1| "use client";
    2| 
    3| import {
    4|   CartesianGrid,
    5|   Legend,
    6|   Line,
    7|   LineChart,
    8|   ResponsiveContainer,
    9|   Tooltip,
   10|   XAxis,
   11|   YAxis,
   12| } from "recharts";
   13| 
   14| import { futureValue } from "@/lib/finance";
   15| 
   16| export type ProjectionGraphProps = {
   17|   /** Present value (current savings). */
   18|   PV: number;
   19|   /** Monthly contribution. */
   20|   PMT: number;
   21|   /** Expected annual return (decimal, e.g. 0.10). */
   22|   r: number;
   23|   /** Time horizon in years; chart will plot yearly points from 0..n (integer years). */
   24|   n: number;
   25| };
   26| 
   27| type DataPoint = {
   28|   year: number;
   29|   baseline: number;
   30|   shock?: number;
   31| };
   32| 
   33| function assertFiniteNumber(name: string, value: number): void {
   34|   if (typeof value !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(value)) {
   35|     throw new TypeError(`${name} must be a finite number`);
   36|   }
   37| }
   38| 
   39| function formatMoney(value: number): string {
   40|   return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
   41|     maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   42|   }).format(value);
   43| }
   44| 
   45| function formatINRCurrency(value: number): string {
   46|   return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
   47|     style: "currency",
   48|     currency: "INR",
   49|     maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   50|   }).format(value);
   51| }
   52| 
   53| export default function ProjectionGraph({
   54|   PV,
   55|   PMT,
   56|   r,
   57|   n,
   58| }: ProjectionGraphProps) {
   59|   assertFiniteNumber("PV", PV);
   60|   assertFiniteNumber("PMT", PMT);
   61|   assertFiniteNumber("r", r);
   62|   assertFiniteNumber("n", n);
   63| 
   64|   // Generate whole-year points from 0 to n.
   65|   // If n is non-integer, this naturally includes 0..floor(n).
   66|   const maxYear = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n));
   67| 
   68|   // Inflation shock scenario: return reduced by 1%.
   69|   const rShock = r - 0.01;
   70|   const hasShock = rShock >= 0;
   71| 
   72|   // Generate discrete yearly projection points.
   73|   // Each point uses the same annual compounding model as the rest of the engine.
   74|   const data: DataPoint[] = [];
   75|   for (let year = 0; year <= maxYear; year++) {
   76|     const baseline = futureValue(PV, PMT, r, year);
   77| 
   78|     if (hasShock) {
   79|       data.push({
   80|         year,
   81|         baseline,
   82|         shock: futureValue(PV, PMT, rShock, year),
   83|       });
   84|     } else {
   85|       // Do not generate shock data when the shocked rate is negative.
   86|       data.push({ year, baseline });
   87|     }
   88|   }
   89| 
   90|   return (
   91|     <div className="h-96 w-full rounded-lg border border-foreground/15 p-3">
   92|       <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
   93|         <LineChart data={data} margin={{ top: 8, right: 12, bottom: 8, left: 12 }}>
   94|           <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" />
   95|           <XAxis
   96|             dataKey="year"
   97|             tickMargin={8}
   98|             label={{ value: "Years", position: "insideBottom", offset: -5 }}
   99|           />
  100|           <YAxis
  101|             domain={["auto", "auto"]}
  102|             tickMargin={8}
  103|             tickFormatter={(value) =>
  104|               new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN").format(Number(value))
  105|             }
  106|             label={{
  107|               value: "Wealth (₹)",
  108|               angle: -90,
  109|               position: "insideLeft",
  110|             }}
  111|             width={84}
  112|           />
  113|           <Tooltip
  114|             formatter={(value) => formatINRCurrency(Number(value))}
  115|             labelFormatter={(label) => `Year ${label}`}
  116|           />
  117|           <Legend />
  118|           <Line
  119|             type="monotoneX"
  120|             dataKey="baseline"
  121|             name="Baseline projection"
  122|             stroke="#2563eb"
  123|             dot={false}
  124|             strokeWidth={2}
  125|           />
  126|           {hasShock ? (
  127|             <Line
  128|               type="monotone"
  129|               dataKey="shock"
  130|               name="Shock projection"
  131|               stroke="#dc2626"
  132|               dot={false}
  133|               strokeWidth={2}
  134|             />
  135|           ) : null}
  136|         </LineChart>
  137|       </ResponsiveContainer>
  138|     </div>
  139|   );
  140| }

===== FILE: components\TrajectoryStatus.tsx =====

    1| import React from "react";
    2| 
    3| export type TrajectoryStatusProps = {
    4|   accelerationScore: number;
    5| };
    6| 
    7| type StatusDef = {
    8|   label: "Strongly Ahead" | "Ahead" | "On Track" | "Behind" | "Off Track";
    9|   containerClassName: string;
   10|   dotClassName: string;
   11| };
   12| 
   13| function getStatus(accelerationScore: number): StatusDef {
   14|   // Rules:
   15|   // >= 1.2  -> Strongly Ahead
   16|   // >= 1.05 -> Ahead
   17|   // 0.95..1.05 -> On Track
   18|   // 0.80..0.95 -> Behind
   19|   // < 0.80 -> Off Track
   20|   if (accelerationScore >= 1.2) {
   21|     return {
   22|       label: "Strongly Ahead",
   23|       containerClassName: "border-green-200 bg-green-50 text-green-800",
   24|       dotClassName: "bg-green-600",
   25|     };
   26|   }
   27| 
   28|   if (accelerationScore >= 1.05) {
   29|     return {
   30|       label: "Ahead",
   31|       containerClassName: "border-green-200 bg-green-50 text-green-700",
   32|       dotClassName: "bg-green-500",
   33|     };
   34|   }
   35| 
   36|   if (accelerationScore >= 0.95 && accelerationScore <= 1.05) {
   37|     return {
   38|       label: "On Track",
   39|       containerClassName: "border-foreground/15 bg-background text-foreground",
   40|       dotClassName: "bg-foreground/40",
   41|     };
   42|   }
   43| 
   44|   if (accelerationScore >= 0.8) {
   45|     return {
   46|       label: "Behind",
   47|       containerClassName: "border-orange-200 bg-orange-50 text-orange-800",
   48|       dotClassName: "bg-orange-500",
   49|     };
   50|   }
   51| 
   52|   return {
   53|     label: "Off Track",
   54|     containerClassName: "border-red-200 bg-red-50 text-red-800",
   55|     dotClassName: "bg-red-600",
   56|   };
   57| }
   58| 
   59| export default function TrajectoryStatus({
   60|   accelerationScore,
   61| }: TrajectoryStatusProps) {
   62|   const status = getStatus(accelerationScore);
   63| 
   64|   return (
   65|     <div
   66|       className={`rounded-lg border p-4 ${status.containerClassName}`}
   67|       aria-label="Trajectory Status"
   68|     >
   69|       <p className="text-sm font-medium">
   70|         Trajectory Status: <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-2">
   71|           <span
   72|             className={`inline-block h-2.5 w-2.5 rounded-full ${status.dotClassName}`}
   73|             aria-hidden="true"
   74|           />
   75|           {status.label}
   76|         </span>
   77|       </p>
   78|     </div>
   79|   );
   80| }

===== FILE: engines\eventClassifier.ts =====

    1| export type MacroEventType =
    2|   | "inflation"
    3|   | "interest_rate"
    4|   | "market"
    5|   | "tax"
    6|   | "policy"
    7|   | "unknown";
    8| 
    9| export function classifyEvent(eventText: string): MacroEventType {
   10|   const text = eventText.toLowerCase();
   11| 
   12|   if (text.includes("inflation")) return "inflation";
   13|   if (text.includes("interest") || text.includes("repo")) return "interest_rate";
   14|   if (text.includes("stock") || text.includes("market")) return "market";
   15|   if (text.includes("tax")) return "tax";
   16|   if (text.includes("policy")) return "policy";
   17| 
   18|   return "unknown";
   19| }

===== FILE: engines\impactEngine.ts =====

    1| import { type MacroEventType } from "./eventClassifier";
    2| 
    3| export type ImpactResult = {
    4|   returnAdjustment: number;
    5|   timelineAdjustmentMonths: number;
    6| };
    7| 
    8| export function computeEventImpact(eventType: MacroEventType): ImpactResult {
    9|   switch (eventType) {
   10|     case "inflation":
   11|       return { returnAdjustment: -0.01, timelineAdjustmentMonths: 6 };
   12| 
   13|     case "interest_rate":
   14|       return { returnAdjustment: -0.005, timelineAdjustmentMonths: 3 };
   15| 
   16|     case "market":
   17|       return { returnAdjustment: 0, timelineAdjustmentMonths: 0 };
   18| 
   19|     case "tax":
   20|     case "policy":
   21|     case "unknown":
   22|     default:
   23|       return { returnAdjustment: 0, timelineAdjustmentMonths: 0 };
   24|   }
   25| }

===== FILE: engines\improvementEngine.ts =====

    1| import { futureValue } from "@/lib/finance";
    2| import { solveForN } from "@/lib/solver";
    3| 
    4| export type ImprovementInputs = {
    5|   currentSavings: number;
    6|   monthlySavings: number;
    7|   expectedReturn: number; // decimal (e.g. 0.10)
    8|   timeHorizon: number; // years
    9|   targetAmount: number;
   10| };
   11| 
   12| export type ImprovementSuggestion = {
   13|   type: "savings" | "return" | "timeline";
   14|   label: string;
   15|   monthsImproved: number;
   16| };
   17| 
   18| const inrInteger = new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
   19|   maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   20| });
   21| 
   22| export function generateImprovements(
   23|   inputs: ImprovementInputs,
   24|   baselineYearsOverride?: number,
   25| ): ImprovementSuggestion[] {
   26|   const baselineYears =
   27|     typeof baselineYearsOverride === "number" &&
   28|     Number.isFinite(baselineYearsOverride)
   29|       ? baselineYearsOverride
   30|       : solveForN(
   31|           inputs.currentSavings,
   32|           inputs.monthlySavings,
   33|           inputs.expectedReturn,
   34|           inputs.targetAmount,
   35|         );
   36| 
   37|   // Step 2: Simulate improvements
   38|   // A) Savings increase (10% bump)
   39|   const simulateSavings = inputs.monthlySavings * 1.1;
   40|   const yearsSavings = solveForN(
   41|     inputs.currentSavings,
   42|     simulateSavings,
   43|     inputs.expectedReturn,
   44|     inputs.targetAmount,
   45|   );
   46|   const monthsSavedSavings = Math.round((baselineYears - yearsSavings) * 12);
   47|   const savingsDelta = Math.round(simulateSavings - inputs.monthlySavings);
   48| 
   49|   // B) Return increase (+0.5%)
   50|   const simulateReturn = inputs.expectedReturn + 0.005;
   51|   const yearsReturn = solveForN(
   52|     inputs.currentSavings,
   53|     inputs.monthlySavings,
   54|     simulateReturn,
   55|     inputs.targetAmount,
   56|   );
   57|   const monthsSavedReturn = Math.round((baselineYears - yearsReturn) * 12);
   58| 
   59|   // C) Timeline extension (+2 years)
   60|   const simulateTimeline = inputs.timeHorizon + 2;
   61|   const fvExtended = futureValue(
   62|     inputs.currentSavings,
   63|     inputs.monthlySavings,
   64|     inputs.expectedReturn,
   65|     simulateTimeline,
   66|   );
   67| 
   68|   const monthsSavedTimeline =
   69|     fvExtended >= inputs.targetAmount
   70|       ? Math.round((baselineYears - inputs.timeHorizon) * 12)
   71|       : 0;
   72| 
   73|   const suggestions: ImprovementSuggestion[] = [
   74|     {
   75|       type: "savings",
   76|       label: `Increase monthly savings by ₹${inrInteger.format(savingsDelta)}`,
   77|       monthsImproved: monthsSavedSavings,
   78|     },
   79|     {
   80|       type: "return",
   81|       label: "Increase expected return by 0.5%",
   82|       monthsImproved: monthsSavedReturn,
   83|     },
   84|     {
   85|       type: "timeline",
   86|       label: "Extend timeline by 2 years",
   87|       monthsImproved: monthsSavedTimeline,
   88|     },
   89|   ];
   90| 
   91|   return suggestions
   92|     .filter((s) => s.monthsImproved > 0)
   93|     .sort((a, b) => b.monthsImproved - a.monthsImproved);
   94| }

===== FILE: engines\insightEngine.ts =====

    1| /**
    2|  * Trajectos — Layer-2 Insight Logic
    3|  *
    4|  * This module contains pure classification logic that interprets
    5|  * numerical outputs from the financial engine into human-readable insights.
    6|  */
    7| 
    8| export type TrajectoryInsight = { title: string; message: string };
    9| 
   10| export type TrajectoryCause = { primary: string; secondary?: string };
   11| 
   12| export function classifyTrajectory(
   13|   compression: number,
   14|   accelerationScore: number,
   15| ): TrajectoryInsight {
   16|   // `compression` is included in the signature to allow future rules that
   17|   // incorporate timeline lead/lag directly. Current rules are score-based.
   18|   void compression;
   19| 
   20|   if (!Number.isFinite(accelerationScore)) {
   21|     return {
   22|       title: "Trajectory",
   23|       message: "Your trajectory insight is unavailable for the current inputs.",
   24|     };
   25|   }
   26| 
   27|   if (accelerationScore >= 1.2) {
   28|     return {
   29|       title: "Trajectory Strongly Ahead",
   30|       message:
   31|         "Your current savings rate and expected returns exceed the pace required to reach your financial target.",
   32|     };
   33|   }
   34| 
   35|   if (accelerationScore >= 1.0) {
   36|     return {
   37|       title: "Trajectory On Track",
   38|       message: "Your current financial trajectory is aligned with your target timeline.",
   39|     };
   40|   }
   41| 
   42|   if (accelerationScore >= 0.9) {
   43|     return {
   44|       title: "Trajectory Slightly Behind",
   45|       message:
   46|         "You are slightly below the pace required to meet your financial goal within the selected timeline.",
   47|     };
   48|   }
   49| 
   50|   if (accelerationScore < 0.9) {
   51|     return {
   52|       title: "Trajectory Behind Target",
   53|       message:
   54|         "Your savings rate and expected returns are not sufficient to reach the target within the selected time horizon.",
   55|     };
   56|   }
   57| 
   58|   return {
   59|     title: "Trajectory",
   60|     message: "Your current trajectory is being evaluated.",
   61|   };
   62| }
   63| 
   64| export function detectTrajectoryCause(
   65|   compression: number,
   66|   monthlySavings: number,
   67|   expectedReturn: number,
   68|   timeHorizon: number,
   69|   requiredMonthlySavings?: number,
   70| ): TrajectoryCause {
   71|   void timeHorizon;
   72| 
   73|   if (compression >= 0) {
   74|     return {
   75|       primary: "Your financial trajectory is currently aligned with your target.",
   76|     };
   77|   }
   78| 
   79|   // User is behind target; detect causes prioritized by controllability.
   80|   const savingsInsufficient =
   81|     typeof requiredMonthlySavings === "number" &&
   82|     Number.isFinite(requiredMonthlySavings) &&
   83|     requiredMonthlySavings > monthlySavings;
   84|   const expectedReturnTooLow = expectedReturn < 0.07;
   85|   const timelineTooAggressive = compression < -0.5;
   86| 
   87|   if (savingsInsufficient) {
   88|     return {
   89|       primary: "Monthly savings are too low relative to the target.",
   90|       secondary:
   91|         "Increasing contributions would significantly improve the trajectory.",
   92|     };
   93|   }
   94| 
   95|   if (expectedReturnTooLow) {
   96|     return {
   97|       primary: "The expected return assumption may be too conservative.",
   98|       secondary:
   99|         "A higher-return investment strategy could accelerate the trajectory.",
  100|     };
  101|   }
  102| 
  103|   if (timelineTooAggressive) {
  104|     return {
  105|       primary: "The selected timeline may be too aggressive for the target.",
  106|       secondary: "Extending the time horizon could make the goal achievable.",
  107|     };
  108|   }
  109| 
  110|   return {
  111|     primary: "Multiple factors are contributing to the delay in reaching the target.",
  112|   };
  113| }

===== FILE: engines\relevanceEngine.ts =====

    1| import { classifyEvent, type MacroEventType } from "@/engines/eventClassifier";
    2| 
    3| export type MacroEvent = {
    4|   id: string;
    5|   title: string;
    6|   description: string;
    7|   source: string;
    8|   timestamp: number;
    9|   category: string;
   10|   geography?: string;
   11|   industries?: string[];
   12| };
   13| 
   14| export type UserProfile = {
   15|   country?: string;
   16|   industries?: string[];
   17|   assetClasses?: string[];
   18| };
   19| 
   20| export type RelevanceResult = {
   21|   score: number;
   22|   feedType: "impact" | "relevant" | "ignore";
   23| };
   24| 
   25| const WEIGHTS = {
   26|   macroImportance: 50,
   27|   geographyMatch: 20,
   28|   industryMatch: 20,
   29|   assetClassMatch: 10,
   30| } as const;
   31| 
   32| function normalize(value: string | undefined): string {
   33|   return (value ?? "").trim().toLowerCase();
   34| }
   35| 
   36| function normalizeList(values: string[] | undefined): string[] {
   37|   if (!values) return [];
   38|   return values.map((v) => normalize(v)).filter(Boolean);
   39| }
   40| 
   41| function hasOverlap(a: string[] | undefined, b: string[] | undefined): boolean {
   42|   const setA = new Set(normalizeList(a));
   43|   if (setA.size === 0) return false;
   44| 
   45|   for (const item of normalizeList(b)) {
   46|     if (setA.has(item)) return true;
   47|   }
   48| 
   49|   return false;
   50| }
   51| 
   52| function toMacroEventType(event: MacroEvent): MacroEventType | "industry" {
   53|   // If the incoming event.category is already aligned with our taxonomy, use it.
   54|   const category = normalize(event.category);
   55|   const allowed: Array<MacroEventType | "industry"> = [
   56|     "inflation",
   57|     "interest_rate",
   58|     "market",
   59|     "tax",
   60|     "policy",
   61|     "unknown",
   62|     "industry",
   63|   ];
   64| 
   65|   // Treat "unknown" as a hint, but allow text-based detection/classification.
   66|   if (allowed.includes(category as MacroEventType | "industry") && category !== "unknown") {
   67|     return category as MacroEventType | "industry";
   68|   }
   69| 
   70|   // Industry keyword detection (helps when category is missing/incorrect).
   71|   const text = `${event.title} ${event.description} ${event.category}`.toLowerCase();
   72|   const industryKeywords = [
   73|     "technology",
   74|     "tech",
   75|     "software",
   76|     "semiconductor",
   77|     "chip",
   78|     "chips",
   79|     "banking",
   80|     "finance",
   81|     "fintech",
   82|     "energy",
   83|     "oil",
   84|     "gas",
   85|     "automotive",
   86|     "manufacturing",
   87|     "healthcare",
   88|     "biotech",
   89|     "pharma",
   90|   ] as const;
   91| 
   92|   for (const keyword of industryKeywords) {
   93|     if (text.includes(keyword)) {
   94|       return "industry";
   95|     }
   96|   }
   97| 
   98|   // Fallback: classify from free text.
   99|   return classifyEvent(`${event.title} ${event.description}`);
  100| }
  101| 
  102| function macroImportanceScore(eventType: MacroEventType | "industry"): number {
  103|   switch (eventType) {
  104|     case "inflation":
  105|       return 50;
  106|     case "interest_rate":
  107|       return 50;
  108|     case "tax":
  109|       return 40;
  110|     case "market":
  111|       return 30;
  112|     case "industry":
  113|       return 20;
  114|     case "policy":
  115|       return 20;
  116|     case "unknown":
  117|     default:
  118|       return 10;
  119|   }
  120| }
  121| 
  122| function geographyScore(event: MacroEvent, user: UserProfile): number {
  123|   const eventGeo = normalize(event.geography);
  124|   const userCountry = normalize(user.country);
  125| 
  126|   // Exact match.
  127|   if (eventGeo.length > 0 && userCountry.length > 0 && eventGeo === userCountry) {
  128|     return WEIGHTS.geographyMatch;
  129|   }
  130| 
  131|   // Treat explicit global markers (or missing geography) as broadly relevant.
  132|   const isGlobal =
  133|     eventGeo.length === 0 ||
  134|     eventGeo === "global" ||
  135|     eventGeo === "world" ||
  136|     eventGeo === "international";
  137| 
  138|   if (isGlobal) {
  139|     return 10;
  140|   }
  141| 
  142|   return 0;
  143| }
  144| 
  145| type AssetClass = "equities" | "bonds" | "crypto" | "commodities";
  146| 
  147| function inferAssetClasses(event: MacroEvent, eventType: MacroEventType | "industry"): AssetClass[] {
  148|   const text = `${event.title} ${event.description} ${event.category}`.toLowerCase();
  149|   const classes = new Set<AssetClass>();
  150| 
  151|   // Keyword heuristics.
  152|   if (
  153|     /(equity|equities|stock|stocks|share|shares|index|nifty|sensex|nasdaq|s\&p|dow)/i.test(
  154|       text,
  155|     )
  156|   ) {
  157|     classes.add("equities");
  158|   }
  159| 
  160|   if (/(bond|bonds|yield|yields|treasury|gilt|gilts|debt|duration)/i.test(text)) {
  161|     classes.add("bonds");
  162|   }
  163| 
  164|   if (/(crypto|bitcoin|btc|ethereum|eth|token|altcoin|blockchain)/i.test(text)) {
  165|     classes.add("crypto");
  166|   }
  167| 
  168|   if (/(commodity|commodities|gold|silver|oil|crude|brent|wti|copper)/i.test(text)) {
  169|     classes.add("commodities");
  170|   }
  171| 
  172|   // Macro-type hints (kept conservative).
  173|   if (eventType === "interest_rate") {
  174|     classes.add("bonds");
  175|   }
  176|   if (eventType === "market") {
  177|     classes.add("equities");
  178|   }
  179| 
  180|   return Array.from(classes);
  181| }
  182| 
  183| function assetClassScore(event: MacroEvent, user: UserProfile, eventType: MacroEventType | "industry"): number {
  184|   const userAssets = new Set(normalizeList(user.assetClasses));
  185|   if (userAssets.size === 0) return 0;
  186| 
  187|   const related = inferAssetClasses(event, eventType);
  188|   for (const asset of related) {
  189|     if (userAssets.has(asset)) {
  190|       return WEIGHTS.assetClassMatch;
  191|     }
  192|   }
  193| 
  194|   return 0;
  195| }
  196| 
  197| export function computeRelevance(event: MacroEvent, user: UserProfile): RelevanceResult {
  198|   const eventType = toMacroEventType(event);
  199| 
  200|   const macroImportance = macroImportanceScore(eventType);
  201|   const geo = geographyScore(event, user);
  202|   const industry = hasOverlap(event.industries, user.industries)
  203|     ? WEIGHTS.industryMatch
  204|     : 0;
  205|   const asset = assetClassScore(event, user, eventType);
  206| 
  207|   const hasGeographyMatch = geo > 0;
  208|   const hasIndustryMatch = industry > 0;
  209|   const hasAssetMatch = asset > 0;
  210|   const hasRelevanceSignal = hasGeographyMatch || hasIndustryMatch || hasAssetMatch;
  211| 
  212|   const score = macroImportance + geo + industry + asset;
  213| 
  214|   const feedType: RelevanceResult["feedType"] =
  215|     macroImportance >= 40 && hasRelevanceSignal
  216|       ? "impact"
  217|       : score >= 30
  218|         ? "relevant"
  219|         : "ignore";
  220| 
  221|   return { score, feedType };
  222| }

===== FILE: engines\returnInsightEngine.ts =====

    1| export type ReturnInsight = {
    2|   label: string;
    3|   message: string;
    4| };
    5| 
    6| export function getReturnInsight(expectedReturn: number): ReturnInsight {
    7|   const returnPercent = expectedReturn * 100;
    8| 
    9|   if (!Number.isFinite(returnPercent)) {
   10|     return {
   11|       label: "Unknown",
   12|       message: "Unable to evaluate your expected return assumption.",
   13|     };
   14|   }
   15| 
   16|   if (returnPercent < 5) {
   17|     return {
   18|       label: "Very Conservative",
   19|       message:
   20|         "Your expected return is very conservative compared to typical market returns.",
   21|     };
   22|   }
   23| 
   24|   if (returnPercent >= 5 && returnPercent < 7) {
   25|     return {
   26|       label: "Conservative",
   27|       message:
   28|         "Your expected return is conservative relative to long-term equity averages.",
   29|     };
   30|   }
   31| 
   32|   if (returnPercent >= 7 && returnPercent <= 12) {
   33|     return {
   34|       label: "Realistic",
   35|       message:
   36|         "Your expected return falls within a realistic long-term equity range.",
   37|     };
   38|   }
   39| 
   40|   if (returnPercent > 12 && returnPercent <= 15) {
   41|     return {
   42|       label: "Optimistic",
   43|       message: "Your expected return is optimistic compared to historical averages.",
   44|     };
   45|   }
   46| 
   47|   if (returnPercent > 15) {
   48|     return {
   49|       label: "Potentially Unrealistic",
   50|       message:
   51|         "Your expected return may be unrealistic compared to typical market performance.",
   52|     };
   53|   }
   54| 
   55|   return {
   56|     label: "Neutral",
   57|     message: "Your expected return assumption could not be classified.",
   58|   };
   59| }

    1| export function generateClusterKey(title: string): string {

===== FILE: lib\finance.ts =====

    1| /**
    2|  * Trajectos — financial calculation helpers.
    3|  *
    4|  * All rates are expressed in decimal form (e.g. 0.10 for 10%).
    5|  */
    6| 
    7| /**
    8|  * Ensures the provided value is a finite number.
    9|  * @throws {TypeError} If the value is not a finite number.
   10|  */
   11| function assertFiniteNumber(name: string, value: number): void {
   12|   if (typeof value !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(value)) {
   13|     throw new TypeError(`${name} must be a finite number`);
   14|   }
   15| }
   16| 
   17| /**
   18|  * Computes the future value (FV) of an investment with annual compounding.
   19|  *
   20|  * Inputs:
   21|  * - PV: current savings (present value)
   22|  * - PMT: monthly savings (payment per month)
   23|  * - r: expected annual return rate in decimal form (e.g. 0.10)
   24|  * - n: time in years
   25|  *
   26|  * The classic future value formula (annual compounding) is:
   27|  *
   28|  *   FV = PV(1 + r)^n + PMT_annual * ((1 + r)^n - 1) / r
   29|  *
   30|  * Where:
   31|  * - PMT_annual = PMT * 12 (monthly contribution converted to annual)
   32|  *
   33|  * Special case:
   34|  * - If r === 0, the growth terms collapse and:
   35|  *     FV = PV + PMT_annual * n
   36|  *
   37|  * @throws {TypeError} If any input is not a finite number.
   38|  */
   39| export function futureValue(PV: number, PMT: number, r: number, n: number): number {
   40|   assertFiniteNumber("PV", PV);
   41|   assertFiniteNumber("PMT", PMT);
   42|   assertFiniteNumber("r", r);
   43|   assertFiniteNumber("n", n);
   44| 
   45|   const annualContribution = PMT * 12;
   46| 
   47|   if (r === 0) {
   48|     return PV + annualContribution * n;
   49|   }
   50| 
   51|   const growth = (1 + r) ** n;
   52| 
   53|   // FV = PV(1+r)^n + PMT_annual * ((1+r)^n - 1)/r
   54|   return PV * growth + annualContribution * ((growth - 1) / r);
   55| }

    1| export const MACRO_FACTORS = [
