    6|   "risk_sentiment",
    7|   "commodity_pressure",
    8| ];

===== FILE: lib\solver.ts =====

    1| import { futureValue } from "./finance";
    2| 
    3| /**
    4|  * Ensures the provided value is a finite number.
    5|  * @throws {TypeError} If the value is not a finite number.
    6|  */
    7| function assertFiniteNumber(name: string, value: number): void {
    8|   if (typeof value !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(value)) {
    9|     throw new TypeError(`${name} must be a finite number`);
   10|   }
   11| }
   12| 
   13| /**
   14|  * Solve for the number of years (n) required to reach a target future value.
   15|  *
   16|  * This uses binary search over a fixed range of years because, under typical
   17|  * assumptions (non-negative PV/PMT and r >= 0), futureValue is monotonic
   18|  * increasing with time.
   19|  *
   20|  * Search constraints:
   21|  * - Range: 0..50 years
   22|  * - Precision: 0.01 years
   23|  * - Max iterations: 100
   24|  *
   25|  * Binary search logic (high level):
   26|  * - Maintain an interval [lo, hi] that is guaranteed to contain the answer.
   27|  * - Evaluate FV at mid.
   28|  * - If FV(mid) is already >= target, the answer is at or before mid => move hi.
   29|  * - Otherwise, the answer is after mid => move lo.
   30|  * - Stop once the interval is narrower than the desired precision (or hit max iterations).
   31|  *
   32|  * @throws {TypeError} If any input is not a finite number.
   33|  * @throws {RangeError} If the target cannot be reached within 0..50 years.
   34|  */
   35| export function solveForN(PV: number, PMT: number, r: number, target: number): number {
   36|   assertFiniteNumber("PV", PV);
   37|   assertFiniteNumber("PMT", PMT);
   38|   assertFiniteNumber("r", r);
   39|   assertFiniteNumber("target", target);
   40| 
   41|   if (r < 0) {
   42|     throw new RangeError("r must be >= 0");
   43|   }
   44| 
   45|   const minYears = 0;
   46|   const maxYears = 50;
   47|   const precision = 0.01;
   48|   const maxIterations = 100;
   49| 
   50|   // Quick exits and feasibility checks within the allowed search range.
   51|   const fvAtMin = futureValue(PV, PMT, r, minYears);
   52|   if (target <= fvAtMin) {
   53|     return 0;
   54|   }
   55| 
   56|   const fvAtMax = futureValue(PV, PMT, r, maxYears);
   57|   if (target > fvAtMax) {
   58|     throw new RangeError("Target cannot be reached within 0..50 years");
   59|   }
   60| 
   61|   let lo = minYears;
   62|   let hi = maxYears;
   63| 
   64|   for (let i = 0; i < maxIterations && hi - lo > precision; i++) {
   65|     const mid = (lo + hi) / 2;
   66|     const fv = futureValue(PV, PMT, r, mid);
   67| 
   68|     if (fv >= target) {
   69|       // We have reached (or exceeded) the target; try to find an earlier time.
   70|       hi = mid;
   71|     } else {
   72|       // Still below target; need more time.
   73|       lo = mid;
   74|     }
   75|   }
   76| 
   77|   // Return the smallest time within the precision that reaches the target.
   78|   // Rounding to 2 decimals matches the 0.01-year precision requirement.
   79|   return Number(hi.toFixed(2));
   80| }
   81| 
   82| /**
   83|  * Solve for the required monthly savings (PMT) to reach a target amount in n years.
   84|  *
   85|  * We start from the annual-compounding future value equation used by `futureValue`:
   86|  *
   87|  *   target = PV(1 + r)^n + PMT_annual * ((1 + r)^n - 1) / r
   88|  *
   89|  * Solve for PMT_annual:
   90|  *
   91|  *   PMT_annual = (target - PV(1 + r)^n) * r / ((1 + r)^n - 1)
   92|  *
   93|  * Then convert back to monthly savings:
   94|  *
   95|  *   PMT_monthly = PMT_annual / 12
   96|  *
   97|  * Edge cases:
   98|  * - If r === 0: target = PV + PMT_annual * n  =>  PMT_monthly = (target - PV) / (12n)
   99|  * - If n === 0: target must equal PV (no time for contributions/growth)
  100|  *
  101|  * @throws {TypeError} If any input is not a finite number.
  102|  * @throws {RangeError} If inputs are outside the solvable domain (e.g. negative n).
  103|  */
  104| export function solveForPMT(PV: number, r: number, n: number, target: number): number {
  105|   assertFiniteNumber("PV", PV);
  106|   assertFiniteNumber("r", r);
  107|   assertFiniteNumber("n", n);
  108|   assertFiniteNumber("target", target);
  109| 
  110|   if (n < 0) {
  111|     throw new RangeError("n must be >= 0");
  112|   }
  113|   if (r < 0) {
  114|     throw new RangeError("r must be >= 0");
  115|   }
  116| 
  117|   // With no time, the only way to hit the target is if it's already met by PV.
  118|   if (n === 0) {
  119|     if (target === PV) {
  120|       return 0;
  121|     }
  122|     throw new RangeError("Target cannot be reached with n = 0 unless target === PV");
  123|   }
  124| 
  125|   if (r === 0) {
  126|     // target = PV + (PMT * 12) * n  =>  PMT = (target - PV) / (12n)
  127|     return (target - PV) / (12 * n);
  128|   }
  129| 
  130|   const growth = (1 + r) ** n;
  131|   const numerator = (target - PV * growth) * r;
  132|   const denominator = growth - 1;
  133| 
  134|   // If denominator is 0 here, n is effectively 0 (handled above), or r is tiny.
  135|   if (denominator === 0) {
  136|     throw new RangeError("Cannot solve for PMT with the provided r and n");
  137|   }
  138| 
  139|   const annualPMT = numerator / denominator;
  140|   return annualPMT / 12;
  141| }

===== FILE: lib\supabase.ts =====

    1| import { createClient, type SupabaseClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
    2| 
    3| /**
    4|  * Supabase setup notes (Trajectos)
    5|  *
    6|  * 1) Create a Supabase project:
    7|  *    Supabase Dashboard → New project
    8|  *
    9|  * 2) Add env vars locally:
   10|  *    - Copy `.env.local.example` → `.env.local`
   11|  *    - Fill in values from: Project Settings → API
   12|  *
   13|  * 3) Create the DB table:
   14|  *    - Supabase Dashboard → SQL Editor
   15|  *    - Run the migration SQL in `supabase/migrations/0001_financial_profiles.sql`
   16|  */
   17| 
   18| type SupabaseEnv = {
   19|   url: string;
   20|   anonKey: string;
   21| };
   22| 
   23| let hasWarnedMissingEnv = false;
   24| 
   25| function warnMissingEnv(): void {
   26|   if (hasWarnedMissingEnv) return;
   27|   hasWarnedMissingEnv = true;
   28| 
   29|   // Avoid crashing the UI; missing env is a common local setup issue.
   30|   // Developers can use `.env.local.example` as the source of truth.
   31|   console.warn(
   32|     "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY in .env.local.",
   33|   );
   34| }
   35| 
   36| function getSupabaseEnv(): SupabaseEnv | null {
   37|   const url = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL;
   38|   const anonKey = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY;
   39| 
   40|   if (!url || !anonKey) {
   41|     warnMissingEnv();
   42|     return null;
   43|   }
   44| 
   45|   return { url, anonKey };
   46| }
   47| 
   48| /**
   49|  * Creates a Supabase client using the project's public URL and anon key.
   50|  *
   51|  * Environment variables required:
   52|  * - NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL
   53|  * - NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY
   54|  */
   55| export function createSupabaseClient(): SupabaseClient | null {
   56|   const env = getSupabaseEnv();
   57|   if (!env) return null;
   58|   return createClient(env.url, env.anonKey, {
   59|     auth: {
   60|       persistSession: true,
   61|       autoRefreshToken: true,
   62|       detectSessionInUrl: true,
   63|     },
   64|   });
   65| }
   66| 
   67| /**
   68|  * Creates a Supabase client that will authenticate requests using the provided
   69|  * access token (typically sent as `Authorization: Bearer <token>`).
   70|  *
   71|  * This is useful in server routes where you want to validate the user and then
   72|  * rely on Row Level Security policies.
   73|  */
   74| export function createSupabaseClientWithAccessToken(
   75|   accessToken: string,
   76| ): SupabaseClient | null {
   77|   const env = getSupabaseEnv();
   78|   if (!env) return null;
   79| 
   80|   return createClient(env.url, env.anonKey, {
   81|     global: {
   82|       headers: {
   83|         Authorization: `Bearer ${accessToken}`,
   84|       },
   85|     },
   86|   });
   87| }
   88| 
   89| export type FinancialProfileUpsert = {
   90|   current_savings: number;
   91|   monthly_savings: number;
   92|   expected_return: number;
   93|   target_amount: number;
   94|   time_horizon: number;
   95| };
   96| 
   97| export type FinancialProfileRow = FinancialProfileUpsert & {
   98|   user_id: string;
   99|   created_at?: string;
  100|   updated_at?: string;
  101| };
  102| 
  103| /**
  104|  * Persists the current user's financial profile in Supabase.
  105|  *
  106|  * - Requires an authenticated Supabase user (client-side session).
  107|  * - Uses `upsert` on `financial_profiles` with `user_id` as the unique key.
  108|  *
  109|  * @throws {Error} If the user is not authenticated or the upsert fails.
  110|  */
  111| export async function saveFinancialProfile(
  112|   profile: FinancialProfileUpsert,
  113| ): Promise<void> {
  114|   // This helper is intended for client-side usage (browser session).
  115|   const supabase = createSupabaseClient();
  116|   if (!supabase) {
  117|     throw new Error(
  118|       "Supabase is not configured. Set NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL and NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
  119|     );
  120|   }
  121| 
  122|   const { data: userData, error: userError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  123|   if (userError || !userData.user) {
  124|     throw new Error("User is not authenticated");
  125|   }
  126| 
  127|   const userId = userData.user.id;
  128| 
  129|   const { error } = await supabase.from("financial_profiles").upsert(
  130|     {
  131|       user_id: userId,
  132|       ...profile,
  133|     },
  134|     { onConflict: "user_id" },
  135|   );
  136| 
  137|   if (error) {
  138|     throw new Error(error.message);
  139|   }
  140| }
  141| 
  142| /**
  143|  * Loads the current user's financial profile from Supabase.
  144|  *
  145|  * Returns `null` when:
  146|  * - the user is not authenticated, or
  147|  * - no profile exists yet.
  148|  *
  149|  * @throws {Error} For unexpected Supabase errors.
  150|  */
  151| export async function getFinancialProfile(): Promise<FinancialProfileRow | null> {
  152|   const supabase = createSupabaseClient();
  153|   if (!supabase) return null;
  154| 
  155|   const { data: userData, error: userError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
  156|   if (userError || !userData.user) {
  157|     return null;
  158|   }
  159| 
  160|   const userId = userData.user.id;
  161| 
  162|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  163|     .from("financial_profiles")
  164|     .select(
  165|       "user_id,current_savings,monthly_savings,expected_return,target_amount,time_horizon,created_at,updated_at",
  166|     )
  167|     .eq("user_id", userId)
  168|     .maybeSingle();
  169| 
  170|   // `maybeSingle()` returns `data: null` with no error when no rows match.
  171|   if (error) {
  172|     throw new Error(error.message);
  173|   }
  174| 
  175|   return (data as FinancialProfileRow | null) ?? null;
  176| }

===== FILE: lib\vectorSearch.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "@/services/newsFetcher";
    2| 
    3| export async function findSimilarEvents(
    4|   embedding: number[],
    5|   bucketFilter?: string | Date | null,
    6| ) {
    7|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
    8| 
    9|   const { data } = await supabase.rpc("match_macro_events", {
   10|     query_embedding: embedding,
   11|     match_threshold: 0.85,
   12|     match_count: 5,
   13|     bucket_filter:
   14|       bucketFilter instanceof Date
   15|         ? bucketFilter.toISOString()
   16|         : (bucketFilter ?? null),
   17|   });
   18| 
   19|   return data ?? [];
   20| }

===== FILE: scripts\resetPipeline.ts =====

    1| import { loadEnvConfig } from "@next/env";
    2| 
    3| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "@/services/newsFetcher";
    4| import type { SupabaseClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
    5| 
    6| loadEnvConfig(process.cwd());
    7| 
    8| function nowMs(): number {
    9|   return Date.now();
   10| }
   11| 
   12| type TableSpec = {
   13|   name: string;
   14|   keyColumn: string;
   15| };
   16| 
   17| const TABLES_TO_CLEAR: TableSpec[] = [
   18|   // Downstream/user-facing tables first
   19|   { name: "insight_user_edges", keyColumn: "user_id" },
   20|   { name: "user_feed_cache", keyColumn: "user_id" },
   21|   { name: "user_feed", keyColumn: "id" },
   22|   { name: "user_relevance_index", keyColumn: "id" },
   23|   { name: "insight_tags", keyColumn: "id" },
   24|   { name: "portfolio_allocations", keyColumn: "id" },
   25|   { name: "event_insights", keyColumn: "id" },
   26|   { name: "portfolio_signals", keyColumn: "id" },
   27|   { name: "event_impact_scores", keyColumn: "id" },
   28|   { name: "event_factor_exposures", keyColumn: "id" },
   29|   // Dependent cluster state
   30|   { name: "event_timelines", keyColumn: "id" },
   31|   // Canonicalization/clustering last because others may FK to clusters
   32|   { name: "canonical_events", keyColumn: "cluster_id" },
   33|   { name: "event_clusters", keyColumn: "id" },
   34| ];
   35| 
   36| async function tableExistsWithClient(
   37|   supabase: SupabaseClient,
   38|   table: string,
   39|   probeColumn: string,
   40| ): Promise<boolean> {
   41|   const { error } = await supabase.from(table).select(probeColumn).limit(1);
   42|   return !error;
   43| }
   44| 
   45| async function countRows(
   46|   supabase: SupabaseClient,
   47|   table: string,
   48|   keyColumn: string,
   49|   filters?: (q: any) => any,
   50| ): Promise<number> {
   51|   if (!(await tableExistsWithClient(supabase, table, keyColumn))) {
   52|     return 0;
   53|   }
   54| 
   55|   const pageSize = 1000;
   56|   let total = 0;
   57| 
   58|   for (let from = 0; ; from += pageSize) {
   59|     let query = supabase.from(table).select(keyColumn).range(from, from + pageSize - 1);
   60|     if (filters) query = filters(query);
   61| 
   62|     const { data, error } = await query;
   63|     if (error) {
   64|       throw new Error(`Failed to count ${table}: ${error.message}`);
   65|     }
   66| 
   67|     const pageCount = (data as unknown[] | null)?.length ?? 0;
   68|     total += pageCount;
   69| 
   70|     if (pageCount < pageSize) break;
   71|   }
   72| 
   73|   return total;
   74| }
   75| 
   76| async function deleteAllRows(supabase: SupabaseClient, table: string, keyColumn: string): Promise<void> {
   77|   if (!(await tableExistsWithClient(supabase, table, keyColumn))) {
   78|     console.warn(`[resetPipeline] Skipping missing table: ${table}`);
   79|     return;
   80|   }
   81| 
   82|   // PostgREST requires a filter for delete; `NOT IS NULL` on a non-null key is effectively "all rows".
   83|   const { error } = await supabase.from(table).delete().not(keyColumn, "is", null);
   84| 
   85|   if (error) {
   86|     throw new Error(`Failed to clear ${table}: ${error.message}`);
   87|   }
   88| }
   89| 
   90| async function resetMacroEventFlags(supabase: SupabaseClient): Promise<void> {
   91|   if (!(await tableExistsWithClient(supabase, "macro_events_raw", "id"))) {
   92|     console.warn("[resetPipeline] macro_events_raw missing; skipping flag reset.");
   93|     return;
   94|   }
   95| 
   96|   const { error } = await supabase
   97|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   98|     .update({ clustered: false, cluster_id: null })
   99|     .not("id", "is", null);
  100| 
  101|   if (error) {
  102|     throw new Error(`Failed to reset macro_events_raw flags: ${error.message}`);
  103|   }
  104| }
  105| 
  106| async function clearPipelineEvents(supabase: SupabaseClient): Promise<void> {
  107|   if (!(await tableExistsWithClient(supabase, "pipeline_events", "id"))) {
  108|     console.warn("[resetPipeline] pipeline_events missing; skipping.");
  109|     return;
  110|   }
  111| 
  112|   const { error } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").delete().not("id", "is", null);
  113|   if (error) {
  114|     throw new Error(`Failed to clear pipeline_events: ${error.message}`);
  115|   }
  116| }
  117| 
  118| async function main(): Promise<void> {
  119|   const started = nowMs();
  120|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  121| 
  122|   console.log("[resetPipeline] Starting pipeline reset...");
  123|   console.log("[resetPipeline] NOTE: Does NOT delete event_queue or macro_events_raw rows.");
  124| 
  125|   // Pre-counts (best-effort; missing tables count as 0)
  126|   const before: Record<string, number> = {};
  127|   for (const t of TABLES_TO_CLEAR) {
  128|     before[t.name] = await countRows(supabase, t.name, t.keyColumn);
  129|   }
  130| 
  131|   const pipelineEventsBefore = await countRows(supabase, "pipeline_events", "id");
  132|   const flaggedBefore = await countRows(supabase, "macro_events_raw", "id", (q) =>
  133|     q.or("clustered.eq.true,cluster_id.not.is.null"),
  134|   );
  135| 
  136|   // Clear state tables
  137|   for (const t of TABLES_TO_CLEAR) {
  138|     await deleteAllRows(supabase, t.name, t.keyColumn);
  139|   }
  140| 
  141|   // Reset flags and clear pipeline events
  142|   await resetMacroEventFlags(supabase);
  143|   await clearPipelineEvents(supabase);
  144| 
  145|   // Post-counts
  146|   const after: Record<string, number> = {};
  147|   for (const t of TABLES_TO_CLEAR) {
  148|     after[t.name] = await countRows(supabase, t.name, t.keyColumn);
  149|   }
  150| 
  151|   const pipelineEventsAfter = await countRows(supabase, "pipeline_events", "id");
  152|   const flaggedAfter = await countRows(supabase, "macro_events_raw", "id", (q) =>
  153|     q.or("clustered.eq.true,cluster_id.not.is.null"),
  154|   );
  155| 
  156|   console.log("\n[resetPipeline] Reset summary:");
  157|   for (const t of TABLES_TO_CLEAR) {
  158|     const b = before[t.name] ?? 0;
  159|     const a = after[t.name] ?? 0;
  160|     console.log(`- ${t.name}: ${b} -> ${a}`);
  161|   }
  162|   console.log(`- pipeline_events: ${pipelineEventsBefore} -> ${pipelineEventsAfter}`);
  163|   console.log(`- macro_events_raw flagged (clustered=true or cluster_id set): ${flaggedBefore} -> ${flaggedAfter}`);
  164| 
  165|   console.log(`\n[resetPipeline] Done in ${nowMs() - started}ms.`);
  166| }
  167| 
  168| main().catch((err: unknown) => {
  169|   console.error("[resetPipeline] Failed:", err);
  170|   process.exitCode = 1;
  171| });

===== FILE: scripts\runFactorEngine.ts =====

   14|   });

   17| function nowMs(): number {
   18|   return Date.now();
   19| }
   20| 
   21| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
   22|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   23| }
   24| 
   25| async function tryExecSql(sql: string): Promise<boolean> {
   26|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   27|   const rpcCandidates = ["exec_sql", "execute_sql", "run_sql"] as const;
   28| 
   29|   for (const fn of rpcCandidates) {
   30|     const { error } = await supabase.rpc(fn, { sql });
   31|     if (!error) return true;
   32|   }
   33| 
   34|   return false;
   35| }
   36| 
   37| async function ensureTable(params: { name: string; probeColumn?: string; ddlSql: string }): Promise<void> {
   38|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   39|   const probeColumn = params.probeColumn ?? "id";
   40| 
   41|   const probe = await supabase.from(params.name).select(probeColumn).limit(1);
   42|   if (!probe.error) return;
   43| 
   44|   const created = await tryExecSql(params.ddlSql);
   45|   if (!created) {
   46|     throw new Error(
   47|       `Missing table ${params.name} and no SQL-exec RPC available to auto-create it. Apply migrations or add an RPC like exec_sql(sql text).`,
   48|     );
   49|   }
   50| 
   51|   const reprobe = await supabase.from(params.name).select(probeColumn).limit(1);
   52|   if (reprobe.error) {
   53|     throw new Error(`Failed to initialize missing table: ${params.name} (${reprobe.error.message})`);
   54|   }
   55| }
   56| 
   57| async function ensureColumn(params: { table: string; select: string; ddlSql: string }): Promise<void> {
   58|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   59| 
   60|   const probe = await supabase.from(params.table).select(params.select).limit(1);
   61|   if (!probe.error) return;
   62| 
   63|   const altered = await tryExecSql(params.ddlSql);
   64|   if (!altered) {
   65|     throw new Error(
   66|       `Missing column(s) for ${params.table} and no SQL-exec RPC available to auto-fix it. Apply migrations or add an RPC like exec_sql(sql text).`,
   67|     );
   68|   }
   69| 
   70|   const reprobe = await supabase.from(params.table).select(params.select).limit(1);
   71|   if (reprobe.error) {
   72|     throw new Error(`Failed to initialize missing column(s) on ${params.table}: ${reprobe.error.message}`);
   73|   }
   74| }
   75| 
   76| async function countRows(table: string, filters?: (q: any) => any): Promise<number> {
   77|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   78| 
   79|   const keyColumnByTable: Record<string, string> = {
   80|     canonical_events: "cluster_id",
   81|     user_feed_cache: "user_id",
   82|     insight_user_edges: "user_id",
   83|   };
   84| 
   85|   const keyColumn = keyColumnByTable[table] ?? "id";
   86|   const pageSize = 1000;
   87| 
   88|   async function tableExists(tableName: string): Promise<boolean> {
   89|     const { error } = await supabase.from(tableName).select(keyColumn).limit(1);
   90|     return !error;
   91|   }
   92| 
   93|   if (!(await tableExists(table))) {
   94|     console.warn(`Skipping count, table missing: ${table}`);
   95|     return 0;
   96|   }
   97| 
   98|   let total = 0;
   99|   for (let from = 0; ; from += pageSize) {
  100|     let query = supabase.from(table).select(keyColumn).range(from, from + pageSize - 1);
  101|     if (filters) query = filters(query);
  102| 
  103|     const { data, error } = await query;
  104| 
  105|     if (error) {
  106|       console.error("Supabase count error:", { table, error });
  107|       throw new Error(`Failed to count ${table}`);
  108|     }
  109| 
  110|     const pageCount = (data as unknown[] | null)?.length ?? 0;
  111|     total += pageCount;
  112| 
  113|     if (pageCount < pageSize) break;
  114|   }
  115| 
  116|   return total;
  117| }
  118| 
  119| async function ensureTableReadable(table: string, probeColumn = "id"): Promise<void> {
  120|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  121|   const { error } = await supabase.from(table).select(probeColumn).limit(1);
  122|   if (error) {
  123|     throw new Error(`Missing required table or permissions: ${table} (${error.message})`);
  124|   }
  125| }

  127| async function seedSimulationPrereqs(): Promise<void> {
  128|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  129| 
  130|   // Ensure key tables exist.
  131|   await ensureTableReadable("event_queue");
  132|   await ensureTableReadable("macro_events_raw");
  133|   await ensureTableReadable("event_clusters");
  134|   await ensureTableReadable("pipeline_events");
  135|   await ensureTableReadable("event_factor_exposures");
  136|   await ensureTableReadable("portfolio_signals");
  137|   await ensureTableReadable("event_insights");
  138|   await ensureTableReadable("user_feed");
  139| 
  140|   // ranking_score is optional: if the migration hasn't been applied yet,
  141|   // the feed engines will fall back to relevance_score ordering.
  142|   const { error: rankingProbeError } = await supabase
  143|     .from("user_feed")
  144|     .select("id,ranking_score")
  145|     .limit(1);
  146| 
  147|   if (rankingProbeError) {
  148|     console.warn(
  149|       "[simulatePipeline] user_feed.ranking_score not available; feed will fall back to relevance_score ordering. Apply migration 0037_user_feed_ranking_score.sql to enable ranking persistence.",
  150|     );
  151|   }
  152| 
  153|   // Ensure prerequisite tables exist. If your DB doesn't expose an SQL-exec RPC,
  154|   // apply migrations / DDL manually instead of relying on auto-create.
  155|   try {
  156|     await ensureTable({
  157|       name: "asset_tags",
  158|       ddlSql: `
  159|         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.asset_tags (
  160|           id uuid PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  161|           asset text,
  162|           tag text,
  163|           created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now()
  164|         );
  165| 
  166|         CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_asset_tags_asset
  167|         ON public.asset_tags(asset);
  168| 
  169|         CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_asset_tags_tag
  170|         ON public.asset_tags(tag);
  171|       `,
  172|     });
  173|   } catch (e) {
  174|     const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e);
  175|     throw new Error(
  176|       `Missing required table asset_tags. Apply supabase/migrations/0026_asset_tags.sql (or create public.asset_tags manually). Original error: ${message}`,
  177|     );
  178|   }
  179| 
  180|   try {
  181|     await ensureTable({
  182|       name: "user_portfolios",
  183|       ddlSql: `
  184|         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.user_portfolios (
  185|           id uuid PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  186|           user_id uuid,
  187|           asset text,
  188|           created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now(),
  189|           UNIQUE(user_id, asset)
  190|         );
  191| 
  192|         CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_user_portfolios_user
  193|         ON public.user_portfolios(user_id);
  194|       `,
  195|     });
  196|   } catch (e) {
  197|     const message = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e);
  198|     throw new Error(
  199|       `Missing required table user_portfolios. Create public.user_portfolios (DDL embedded in scripts/simulatePipeline.ts) or add an SQL-exec RPC. Original error: ${message}`,
  200|     );
  201|   }
  202| 
  203|   // Seed test user portfolios so relevance/feed stages have data.
  204|   const { error: seedPortfolioError } = await supabase.from("user_portfolios").upsert(
  205|     [
  206|       { user_id: "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001", asset: "equities" },
  207|       { user_id: "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000001", asset: "bonds" },
  208|       { user_id: "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000002", asset: "commodities" },
  209|     ],
  210|     { onConflict: "user_id,asset" },
  211|   );
  212| 
  213|   if (seedPortfolioError) {
  214|     throw new Error(`Failed to seed user_portfolios: ${seedPortfolioError.message}`);
  215|   }
  216| 
  217|   // Seed asset tags so user relevance can match insight tags.
  218|   const { error: seedAssetTagsError } = await supabase.from("asset_tags").upsert(
  219|     [
  220|       { asset: "equities", tag: "equities" },
  221|       { asset: "bonds", tag: "bonds" },
  222|       { asset: "commodities", tag: "commodities" },
  223|       { asset: "usd", tag: "currency" },
  224|     ],
  225|     { onConflict: "asset,tag" },
  226|   );
  227| 
  228|   if (seedAssetTagsError) {
  229|     throw new Error(`Failed to seed asset_tags: ${seedAssetTagsError.message}`);
  230|   }
  231| 
  232|   // Optional: seed segments so segment engine can build indexes.
  233|   // If segment tables are missing, skip silently (simulation can still validate user feed).
  234|   const segProbe = await supabase.from("segment_tags").select("id").limit(1);
  235|   if (!segProbe.error) {
  236|     await supabase.from("segment_tags").upsert(
  237|       [
  238|         { segment: "tech_investors", tag: "equities" },
  239|         { segment: "bond_investors", tag: "bonds" },
  240|         { segment: "crypto_investors", tag: "commodities" },
  241|       ],
  242|       { onConflict: "segment,tag" },
  243|     );
  244|   }
  245| 
  246|   console.log("Seeded simulation prereqs (user_portfolios, asset_tags). ");
  247| }

  249| type SyntheticEvent = {
  250|   title: string;
  251|   description: string;
  252|   source: string;
  253|   url: string;
  254|   category: string;
  255|   geography: string;
  256|   industries: string[];
  257|   published_at: string;
  258|   processed: boolean;
  259| };
  260| 
  261| function pick<T>(items: readonly T[], index: number): T {
  262|   return items[index % items.length] as T;
  263| }
  264| 
  265| function buildSyntheticEvents(count: number): SyntheticEvent[] {
  266|   const now = Date.now();
  267|   const sources = ["pipeline_simulator"] as const;
  268|   const categories = ["macro", "rates", "inflation", "growth", "risk"] as const;
  269|   const geographies = ["US", "EU", "UK", "JP", "CN", "Global"] as const;
  270|   const industries = ["technology", "energy", "financials", "industrials", "healthcare"] as const;
  271| 
  272|   const out: SyntheticEvent[] = [];
  273| 
  274|   for (let i = 0; i < count; i += 1) {
  275|     const publishedMs = now - i * 60_000;
  276|     const geography = pick(geographies, i);
  277|     const category = pick(categories, i);
  278|     const industryA = pick(industries, i);
  279|     const industryB = pick(industries, i + 2);
  280| 
  281|     // Titles are written to intentionally trigger insightTagEngine tags.
  282|     const title =
  283|       i % 3 === 0
  284|         ? `Inflation rises as bond yields move (${geography}) #${i}`
  285|         : i % 3 === 1
  286|           ? `Equities wobble amid tighter liquidity and risk sentiment (${geography}) #${i}`
  287|           : `Oil and energy prices lift commodities; USD reacts (${geography}) #${i}`;
  288| 
  289|     const description =
  290|       i % 3 === 0
  291|         ? "Inflation data surprised to the upside; interest rates expectations shifted and bond pricing adjusted."
  292|         : i % 3 === 1
  293|           ? "Liquidity conditions tightened, weighing on equities as risk sentiment deteriorated."
  294|           : "Energy markets tightened; oil prices moved higher, supporting commodities while the dollar responded to funding demand.";
  295| 
  296|     out.push({
  297|       title,
  298|       description,
  299|       source: sources[0],
  300|       url: `https://example.com/simulated/pipeline/${now}-${i}`,
  301|       category,
  302|       geography,
  303|       industries: [industryA, industryB],
  304|       published_at: new Date(publishedMs).toISOString(),
  305|       processed: false,
  306|     });
  307|   }
  308| 
  309|   return out;
  310| }
  311| 
  312| async function insertSyntheticQueueEvents(count: number): Promise<void> {
  313|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  314| 
  315|   const batch = buildSyntheticEvents(count);
  316|   const { error } = await supabase.from("event_queue").upsert(batch, {
  317|     onConflict: "url",
  318|   });
  319| 
  320|   if (error) {
  321|     throw new Error(`Failed to insert synthetic event_queue rows: ${error.message}`);
  322|   }
  323| 
  324|   console.log(`Inserted ${count} synthetic events into event_queue.`);
  325| }
  326| 
  327| async function emitClusterCreatedForSimulationClusters(params: {
  328|   sinceIso: string;
  329| }): Promise<number> {
  330|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  331| 
  332|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  333|     .from("macro_events_raw")
  334|     .select("cluster_id")
  335|     .eq("source", "pipeline_simulator")
  336|     .gte("published_at", params.sinceIso)
  337|     .not("cluster_id", "is", null)
  338|     .limit(5000);
  339| 
  340|   if (error) {
  341|     throw new Error(`Failed to load simulation macro events for cluster emission: ${error.message}`);
  342|   }
  343| 
  344|   const clusterIds = Array.from(
  345|     new Set(
  346|       ((data as Array<{ cluster_id: string | null }> | null) ?? [])
  347|         .map((r) => (r.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim())
  348|         .filter(Boolean),
  349|     ),
  350|   );
  351| 
  352|   if (clusterIds.length === 0) return 0;
  353| 
  354|   let emitted = 0;
  355| 
  356|   // Emit events only if no unprocessed CLUSTER_CREATED exists for that cluster.
  357|   for (const clusterId of clusterIds) {
  358|     const { data: existing, error: existingError } = await supabase
  359|       .from("pipeline_events")
  360|       .select("id")
  361|       .eq("event_type", "CLUSTER_CREATED")
  362|       .eq("processed", false)
  363|       .eq("payload->>cluster_id", clusterId)
  364|       .limit(1);
  365| 
  366|     if (existingError) {
  367|       // If we can't check, skip emission (safe).
  368|       continue;
  369|     }
  370| 
  371|     if ((existing ?? []).length > 0) continue;
  372| 
  373|     const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  374|       event_type: "CLUSTER_CREATED",
  375|       payload: { cluster_id: clusterId },
  376|     });
  377| 
  378|     if (insertError) {
  379|       throw new Error(`Failed to emit CLUSTER_CREATED for ${clusterId}: ${insertError.message}`);
  380|     }
  381| 
  382|     emitted += 1;
  383|   }
  384| 
  385|   return emitted;
  386| }
  387| 
  388| async function runStage(name: string, fn: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void> {
  389|   const started = nowMs();
  390|   console.log(`Running stage: ${name}`);
  391|   await fn();
  392|   console.log(`Stage completed: ${name} (${nowMs() - started}ms)`);
  393| }
  394| 
  395| async function drainStage(params: {
  396|   name: string;
  397|   runOnce: () => Promise<void>;
  398|   pendingCount: () => Promise<number>;
  399|   maxIterations?: number;
  400| }): Promise<void> {
  401|   const started = nowMs();
  402|   const maxIterations = params.maxIterations ?? 25;
  403|   const deadline = Date.now() + 90_000;
  404| 
  405|   console.log(`Running stage: ${params.name}`);
  406| 
  407|   let lastPending = await params.pendingCount();
  408|   for (let i = 0; i < maxIterations; i += 1) {
  409|     if (Date.now() > deadline) {
  410|       throw new Error(`Drain timeout exceeded for ${params.name}`);
  411|     }
  412| 
  413|     if (lastPending === 0) {
  414|       console.log(`Stage completed: ${params.name} (drained in ${i} iterations, ${nowMs() - started}ms)`);
  415|       return;
  416|     }
  417| 
  418|     await params.runOnce();
  419| 
  420|     const nextPending = await params.pendingCount();
  421|     if (nextPending === lastPending) {
  422|       console.log(
  423|         `Stage completed: ${params.name} (stopped: no progress; pending=${nextPending}, ${nowMs() - started}ms)`,
  424|       );
  425|       return;
  426|     }
  427| 
  428|     lastPending = nextPending;
  429|     await sleep(50);
  430|   }
  431| 
  432|   const finalPending = await params.pendingCount();
  433|   console.log(
  434|     `Stage completed: ${params.name} (max iterations reached; pending=${finalPending}, ${nowMs() - started}ms)`,
  435|   );
  436| }
  437| 
  438| async function main(): Promise<void> {
  439|   const simCount = Number(process.env.SIM_EVENT_COUNT ?? "100");
  440|   const n = Number.isFinite(simCount) && simCount > 0 ? Math.floor(simCount) : 100;
  441| 
  442|   await seedSimulationPrereqs();
  443| 
  444|   const before = {
  445|     event_clusters: await countRows("event_clusters"),
  446|     factor_exposures: await countRows("event_factor_exposures"),
  447|     portfolio_signals: await countRows("portfolio_signals"),
  448|     event_insights: await countRows("event_insights"),
  449|     user_feed: await countRows("user_feed"),
  450|   };
  451| 
  452|   const sinceIso = new Date(Date.now() - 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString();
  453| 
  454|   await insertSyntheticQueueEvents(n);
  455| 
  456|   await drainStage({
  457|     name: "Queue processing (processEventQueue)",
  458|     runOnce: async () => {
  459|       await processEventQueue();
  460|     },
  461|     pendingCount: async () => countRows("event_queue", (q) => q.eq("processed", false)),
  462|     maxIterations: 20,
  463|   });
  464| 
  465|   // Clustering: prefer vector-based clustering if available; fallback to incremental clustering + CLUSTER_CREATED emission.
  466|   let clusteringUsed: "eventClustering" | "incrementalClustering" = "eventClustering";
  467| 
  468|   try {
  469|     await runStage("Clustering (runEventClustering)", async () => {
  470|       for (let i = 0; i < 6; i += 1) {
  471|         await runEventClustering();
  472|       }
  473|     });
  474|   } catch (err: unknown) {
  475|     const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
  476|     console.warn("runEventClustering failed; falling back to runIncrementalClustering", { message });
  477|     clusteringUsed = "incrementalClustering";
  478| 
  479|     await runStage("Clustering fallback (runIncrementalClustering)", async () => {
  480|       for (let i = 0; i < 6; i += 1) {
  481|         await runIncrementalClustering();
  482|       }
  483|     });
  484| 
  485|     const emitted = await emitClusterCreatedForSimulationClusters({ sinceIso });
  486|     console.log(`Emitted ${emitted} CLUSTER_CREATED events for fallback clustering.`);
  487|   }
  488| 
  489|   await runStage("Canonicalization (runCanonicalizer)", async () => {
  490|     for (let i = 0; i < 6; i += 1) {
  491|       await runCanonicalizer();
  492|     }
  493|   });
  494| 
  495|   await runStage("Pipeline DAG (runPipelineOrchestrator)", async () => {
  496|     // Run multiple passes so downstream engines are kicked promptly.
  497|     await runPipelineOrchestrator({ batchSize: 75, maxPasses: 40 });
  498|   });
  499| 
  500|   // Post-DAG: tagging + relevance + feed + cache.
  501|   await runStage("Insight tagging (runInsightTagEngine)", async () => {
  502|     for (let i = 0; i < 10; i += 1) {
  503|       await runInsightTagEngine();
  504|     }
  505|   });
  506| 
  507|   await runStage("Segment relevance (runSegmentRelevanceEngine)", async () => {
  508|     await runSegmentRelevanceEngine();
  509|   });
  510| 
  511|   await runStage("User relevance (runUserRelevanceEngine)", async () => {
  512|     await runUserRelevanceEngine();
  513|   });
  514| 
  515|   await drainStage({
  516|     name: "Feed generation (runUserFeedEngine)",
  517|     runOnce: async () => {
  518|       await runUserFeedEngine();
  519|     },
  520|     pendingCount: async () =>
  521|       countRows("pipeline_events", (q) => q.eq("event_type", "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED").eq("processed", false)),
  522|     maxIterations: 25,
  523|   });
  524| 
  525|   await drainStage({
  526|     name: "Feed cache (runFeedCacheEngine)",
  527|     runOnce: async () => {
  528|       await runFeedCacheEngine();
  529|     },
  530|     pendingCount: async () =>
  531|       countRows("pipeline_events", (q) => q.eq("event_type", "USER_FEED_DELTA").eq("processed", false)),
  532|     maxIterations: 25,
  533|   });
  534| 
  535|   const after = {
  536|     event_clusters: await countRows("event_clusters"),
  537|     factor_exposures: await countRows("event_factor_exposures"),
  538|     portfolio_signals: await countRows("portfolio_signals"),
  539|     event_insights: await countRows("event_insights"),
  540|     user_feed: await countRows("user_feed"),
  541|   };
  542| 
  543|   console.log("\n=== PIPELINE SIMULATION SUMMARY ===");
  544|   console.log(`Clustering mode: ${clusteringUsed}`);
  545| 
  546|   console.log("\nRequested output (deltas):");
  547|   console.log(`• clusters created: ${after.event_clusters - before.event_clusters}`);
  548|   console.log(`• factor exposures generated: ${after.factor_exposures - before.factor_exposures}`);
  549|   console.log(`• signals generated: ${after.portfolio_signals - before.portfolio_signals}`);
  550|   console.log(`• insights created: ${after.event_insights - before.event_insights}`);
  551|   console.log(`• feed entries generated: ${after.user_feed - before.user_feed}`);
  552| }
  553| 
  554| main().catch((err: unknown) => {
  555|   const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
  556|   console.error("Pipeline simulation failed:", message);
  557|   process.exit(1);
  558| });

   20| type StepResult = {
   21|   step: string;
   22|   ok: boolean;
   23|   details: string;
   24|   ms: number;
   25| };
   26| 
   27| function nowMs(): number {
   28|   return Date.now();
   29| }
   30| 
   31| async function countRows(
   32|   table: string,
   33|   filters?: (q: any) => any,
   34| ): Promise<number> {
   35|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   36| 
   37|   // Avoid { count: 'exact', head: true } because it can fail intermittently on some setups.
   38|   // Instead, fetch a minimal key column and count rows client-side (paginated).
   39|   const keyColumnByTable: Record<string, string> = {
   40|     canonical_events: "cluster_id",
   41|     user_feed_cache: "user_id",
   42|     insight_user_edges: "user_id",
   43|   };
   44| 
   45|   const keyColumn = keyColumnByTable[table] ?? "id";
   46|   const pageSize = 1000;
   47| 
   48|   async function tableExists(tableName: string): Promise<boolean> {
   49|     const { error } = await supabase.from(tableName).select(keyColumn).limit(1);
   50|     return !error;
   51|   }
   52| 
   53|   if (!(await tableExists(table))) {
   54|     console.warn(`Skipping count, table missing: ${table}`);
   55|     return 0;
   56|   }
   57| 
   58|   let total = 0;
   59|   for (let from = 0; ; from += pageSize) {
   60|     let query = supabase.from(table).select(keyColumn).range(from, from + pageSize - 1);
   61|     if (filters) query = filters(query);
   62| 
   63|     const { data, error } = await query;
   64| 
   65|     if (error) {
   66|       console.error("Supabase count error:", { table, error });
   67|       throw new Error(`Failed to count ${table}`);
   68|     }
   69| 
   70|     const pageCount = (data as unknown[] | null)?.length ?? 0;
   71|     total += pageCount;
   72| 
   73|     if (pageCount < pageSize) {
   74|       break;
   75|     }
   76|   }
   77| 
   78|   return total;
   79| }
   80| 
   81| async function tryStep(name: string, fn: () => Promise<void>): Promise<StepResult> {
   82|   const started = nowMs();
   83|   try {
   84|     console.log(`Running stage: ${name}`);
   85|     await fn();
   86|     console.log(`Stage completed: ${name}`);
   87|     return { step: name, ok: true, details: "ok", ms: nowMs() - started };
   88|   } catch (err: unknown) {
   89|     console.error(`Stage failed: ${name}`, err);
   90|     const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   91|     return { step: name, ok: false, details: message, ms: nowMs() - started };
   92|   }
   93| }
   94| 
   95| async function drain(
   96|   name: string,
   97|   runOnce: () => Promise<void>,
   98|   pendingCount: () => Promise<number>,
   99|   maxIterations = 15,
  100| ): Promise<StepResult> {
  101|   const started = nowMs();
  102|   const startTime = Date.now();
  103| 
  104|   console.log(`Running stage: ${name}`);
  105| 
  106|   const complete = (result: StepResult): StepResult => {
  107|     if (result.ok) {
  108|       console.log(`Stage completed: ${name}`);
  109|     } else {
  110|       console.error(`Stage failed: ${name}`, new Error(result.details));
  111|     }
  112|     return result;
  113|   };
  114| 
  115|   try {
  116|     let lastPending = await pendingCount();
  117|     for (let i = 0; i < maxIterations; i += 1) {
  118|       if (Date.now() - startTime > 60000) {
  119|         throw new Error(`Drain timeout exceeded for ${name}`);
  120|       }
  121| 
  122|       if (lastPending === 0) {
  123|         return complete({
  124|           step: name,
  125|           ok: true,
  126|           details: `drained (${i} iterations)`,
  127|           ms: nowMs() - started,
  128|         });
  129|       }
  130| 
  131|       await runOnce();
  132| 
  133|       const nextPending = await pendingCount();
  134| 
  135|       // Prevent infinite loops for engines that intentionally leave events pending
  136|       // (e.g. factor engine waiting for validation).
  137|       if (nextPending === lastPending) {
  138|         return complete({
  139|           step: name,
  140|           ok: true,
  141|           details: `stopped (no pending progress; pending=${nextPending})`,
  142|           ms: nowMs() - started,
  143|         });
  144|       }
  145| 
  146|       lastPending = nextPending;
  147|     }
  148| 
  149|     const finalPending = await pendingCount();
  150|     return complete({
  151|       step: name,
  152|       ok: finalPending === 0,
  153|       details: `max iterations reached (pending=${finalPending})`,
  154|       ms: nowMs() - started,
  155|     });
  156|   } catch (err: unknown) {
  157|     console.error(`Stage failed: ${name}`, err);
  158|     const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
  159|     return { step: name, ok: false, details: message, ms: nowMs() - started };
  160|   }
  161| }
  162| 
  163| async function checkPipelineHealth(): Promise<void> {
  164|   const pending = await countRows("pipeline_events", (q) => q.eq("processed", false));
  165| 
  166|   if (pending > 200) {
  167|     throw new Error(`Pipeline backlog detected: ${pending} unprocessed events`);
  168|   }
  169| 
  170|   console.log("Pipeline health OK");
  171| }

  173| async function cleanupPipelineEvents(): Promise<void> {
  174|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  175| 
  176|   const cutoffIso = new Date(Date.now() - 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString();
  177| 
  178|   const { error } = await supabase
  179|     .from("pipeline_events")
  180|     .delete()
  181|     .lt("created_at", cutoffIso);
  182| 
  183|   if (error) {
  184|     // Keep tests running even if cleanup fails (e.g. missing table).
  185|     console.warn("Failed to cleanup old pipeline events", {
  186|       error,
  187|     });
  188|     return;
  189|   }
  190| 
  191|   console.log("Cleaned up old pipeline events");
  192| }

  194| async function ensurePipelineTables(): Promise<void> {
  195|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  196| 
  197|   const probe = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").select("id").limit(1);
  198|   if (!probe.error) return;
  199| 
  200|   // Best-effort local initialization: Supabase cannot execute arbitrary SQL via
  201|   // the JS client unless the database exposes an RPC that runs SQL.
  202|   // If your local project defines one (commonly named exec_sql/execute_sql),
  203|   // we can use it here.
  204|   const sql = `
  205|     CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.pipeline_events (
  206|       id uuid PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  207|       event_type text NOT NULL,
  208|       payload jsonb,
  209|       processed boolean DEFAULT false,
  210|       created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now()
  211|     );
  212| 
  213|     CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_pipeline_events_type
  214|       ON public.pipeline_events(event_type);
  215| 
  216|     CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_pipeline_events_processed
  217|       ON public.pipeline_events(processed);
  218|   `;
  219| 
  220|   const rpcCandidates = ["exec_sql", "execute_sql", "run_sql"] as const;
  221|   for (const fn of rpcCandidates) {
  222|     const { error } = await supabase.rpc(fn, { sql });
  223|     if (!error) {
  224|       console.log("Initialized missing pipeline tables.");
  225|       return;
  226|     }
  227|   }
  228| 
  229|   console.warn(
  230|     "pipeline_events appears missing, but no SQL-exec RPC was available to auto-initialize. Apply migrations (recommended) or create an RPC like exec_sql(sql text).",
  231|     {
  232|       probeError: probe.error,
  233|     },
  234|   );
  235| }
  236| 
  237| async function verifySchema(): Promise<void> {
  238|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  239| 
  240|   const requiredTables = [
  241|     "pipeline_events",
  242|     "event_clusters",
  243|     "macro_events_raw",
  244|     "event_insights",
  245|     "portfolio_signals",
  246|   ];
  247| 
  248|   for (const table of requiredTables) {
  249|     const { error } = await supabase.from(table).select("id").limit(1);
  250|     if (error) {
  251|       throw new Error(`Missing required table: ${table}`);
  252|     }
  253|   }
  254| 
  255|   // Verify required columns exist.
  256|   const { error: columnError } = await supabase
  257|     .from("event_clusters")
  258|     .select("id,validated,processed")
  259|     .limit(1);
  260| 
  261|   if (columnError) {
  262|     throw new Error("Schema migration missing: event_clusters validation columns");
  263|   }
  264| }

  683|       ms: r.ms,

  686|   );

  688|   console.log("\n=== TABLE COUNTS (before -> after) ===");

  690|     Object.keys(after).map((k) => ({
  691|       table: k,
  692|       before: (before as any)[k],
  693|       after: (after as any)[k],
  694|       delta: (after as any)[k] - (before as any)[k],
  695|     })),
  696|   );
  697| 
  698|   const failed = results.filter((r) => !r.ok);
  699|   if (failed.length > 0) {
  700|     process.exitCode = 1;
  701|   }
  702| }
  703|

  705|   const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
  706|   console.error("System test failed:", message);
  707|   process.exit(1);
  708| });

===== FILE: services\allocationEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { allocationModel, type AllocationSignal } from "@/lib/allocationModel";
    3| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    4| import { workerPoolForEach } from "./workerPool";
    5| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";
    6| 
    7| type PipelineEventRow = {
    8|   id: string;
    9|   payload: unknown;
   10| };
   11| 
   12| type PortfolioSignal = {
   13|   asset: string | null;
   14|   signal: string | null;
   15|   confidence: number | null;
   16| };
   17| 
   18| function extractClusterIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   19|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   20|   const clusterId = (payload as { cluster_id?: unknown }).cluster_id;
   21|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   22|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   23|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   24| }
   25| 
   26| function normalizeSignal(signal: string | null | undefined): AllocationSignal {
   27|   const s = (signal ?? "").toString().trim().toUpperCase();
   28|   if (s === "BUY" || s === "SELL" || s === "NEUTRAL") return s;
   29|   return "NEUTRAL";
   30| }
   31| 
   32| function clamp01(value: number): number {
   33|   if (!Number.isFinite(value)) return 0;
   34|   return Math.min(1, Math.max(0, value));
   35| }
   36| 
   37| function normalizeAllocations(weights: Record<string, number>): Record<string, number> {
   38|   const out: Record<string, number> = {};
   39| 
   40|   for (const [asset, weight] of Object.entries(weights)) {
   41|     out[asset] = clamp01(weight);
   42|   }
   43| 
   44|   const sum = Object.values(out).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
   45|   if (sum <= 0) {
   46|     return { ...Object.fromEntries(Object.keys(out).map((k) => [k, 0])), cash: 1 };
   47|   }
   48| 
   49|   for (const asset of Object.keys(out)) {
   50|     out[asset] = out[asset] / sum;
   51|   }
   52| 
   53|   return out;
   54| }
   55| 
   56| function avg(nums: number[]): number {
   57|   const finite = nums.filter((n) => Number.isFinite(n));
   58|   if (finite.length === 0) return 0;
   59|   return finite.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / finite.length;
   60| }
   61| 
   62| export async function runAllocationEngine(): Promise<void> {
   63|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   64| 
   65|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
   66|     .from("pipeline_events")
   67|     .select("id,payload")
   68|     .eq("event_type", "INSIGHT_CREATED")
   69|     .eq("processed", false)
   70|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   71|     .limit(20);
   72| 
   73|   if (error) {
   74|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
   75|   }
   76| 
   77|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
   78|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
   79| 
   80|   const seen = new Set<string>();
   81|   const unique: PipelineEventRow[] = [];
   82|   for (const evt of pending) {
   83|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
   84|     if (!clusterId) {
   85|       unique.push(evt);
   86|       continue;
   87|     }
   88|     if (seen.has(clusterId)) continue;
   89|     seen.add(clusterId);
   90|     unique.push(evt);
   91|   }
   92| 
   93|   await workerPoolForEach(
   94|     unique,
   95|     async (evt) => {
   96|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
   97| 
   98|     await withStageSpan({
   99|       supabase,
  100|       stageName: "allocation",
  101|       clusterId,
  102|       eventId: evt.id,
  103|       statusOnSuccess: clusterId ? "success" : "skipped",
  104|       fn: async () => {
  105|         if (!clusterId) {
  106|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
  107|             .from("pipeline_events")
  108|             .update({ processed: true })
  109|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  110| 
  111|           if (markError) {
  112|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  113|           }
  114| 
  115|           return;
  116|         }
  117| 
  118|         const { data: existing, error: existingError } = await supabase
  119|           .from("portfolio_allocations")
  120|           .select("id")
  121|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  122|           .limit(1);
  123| 
  124|         if (existingError) {
  125|           throw new Error(`Failed to check existing allocations: ${existingError.message}`);
  126|         }
  127| 
  128|         if ((existing ?? []).length > 0) {
  129|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
  130|             .from("pipeline_events")
  131|             .update({ processed: true })
  132|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  133| 
  134|           if (markError) {
  135|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  136|           }
  137| 
  138|           return;
  139|         }
  140| 
  141|         const { data: signalsRows, error: signalsError } = await supabase
  142|           .from("portfolio_signals")
  143|           .select("asset,signal,confidence")
  144|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId);
  145| 
  146|         if (signalsError) {
  147|           throw new Error(`Failed to load portfolio signals: ${signalsError.message}`);
  148|         }
  149| 
  150|         const rows = (signalsRows as PortfolioSignal[] | null) ?? [];
  151|         if (rows.length === 0) {
  152|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
  153|             .from("pipeline_events")
  154|             .update({ processed: true })
  155|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  156| 
  157|           if (markError) {
  158|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  159|           }
  160| 
  161|           return;
  162|         }
  163| 
  164|         const signalByAsset = new Map<string, { signal: AllocationSignal; confidence: number }>();
  165|         for (const row of rows) {
  166|           const asset = (row.asset ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase();
  167|           if (!asset) continue;
  168|           const signal = normalizeSignal(row.signal);
  169|           const conf = Number(row.confidence);
  170|           signalByAsset.set(asset, {
  171|             signal,
  172|             confidence: Number.isFinite(conf) ? conf : 0.6,
  173|           });
  174|         }
  175| 
  176|         // Base weights example
  177|         const baseWeights: Record<string, number> = {
  178|           equities: 0.4,
  179|           bonds: 0.3,
  180|           commodities: 0.2,
  181|           usd: 0.1,
  182|           cash: 0,
  183|         };
  184| 
  185|         const rawWeights: Record<string, number> = { ...baseWeights };
  186| 
  187|         for (const asset of Object.keys(baseWeights)) {
  188|           if (asset === "cash") continue;
  189|           const entry = signalByAsset.get(asset);
  190|           if (!entry) continue;
  191|           rawWeights[asset] = (rawWeights[asset] ?? 0) + allocationModel[entry.signal];
  192|         }
  193| 
  194|         const normalized = normalizeAllocations(rawWeights);
  195| 
  196|         const clusterConfidence = Math.min(
  197|           0.95,
  198|           Math.max(0.5, avg(Array.from(signalByAsset.values()).map((v) => v.confidence))),
  199|         );
  200| 
  201|         const inserts = Object.entries(normalized).map(([asset, allocation]) => {
  202|           const entry = signalByAsset.get(asset);
  203|           const confidence = entry?.confidence ?? clusterConfidence;
  204|           return {
  205|             cluster_id: clusterId,
  206|             asset,
  207|             allocation,
  208|             confidence,
  209|           };
  210|         });
  211| 
  212|         const { error: insertError } = await supabase
  213|           .from("portfolio_allocations")
  214|           .insert(inserts);
  215| 
  216|         if (insertError) {
  217|           throw new Error(`Failed to insert portfolio allocations: ${insertError.message}`);
  218|         }
  219| 
  220|         const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  221|           .from("pipeline_events")
  222|           .update({ processed: true })
  223|           .eq("id", evt.id);
  224| 
  225|         if (markEventError) {
  226|           throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`);
  227|         }
  228| 
  229|         await emitClusterEventOnce({
  230|           supabase,
  231|           eventType: "ALLOCATION_CREATED",
  232|           clusterId,
  233|         });
  234|       },
  235|     });
  236|     },
  237|     { concurrency: Number(process.env.PIPELINE_CONCURRENCY ?? 5) || 5 },
  238|   );
  239| }

===== FILE: services\archiveEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import path from "path";
    3| import { fileURLToPath } from "url";
    4| 
    5| type MacroEventRow = {
    6|   id: string;
    7|   title: string;
    8|   description: string;
    9|   source: string;
   10|   url: string;
   11|   published_at: string;
   12|   ingested_at: string;
   13|   processed: boolean;
   14|   category: string;
   15|   geography: string | null;
   16|   industries: string[] | null;
   17| };
   18| 
   19| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
   20|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   21| }
   22| 
   23| function daysAgoIso(days: number): string {
   24|   const ms = Date.now() - days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   25|   return new Date(ms).toISOString();
   26| }
   27| 
   28| function envInt(name: string, fallback: number): number {
   29|   const raw = process.env[name];
   30|   if (!raw) return fallback;
   31|   const n = Number(raw);
   32|   return Number.isFinite(n) && n > 0 ? Math.floor(n) : fallback;
   33| }
   34| 
   35| function log(message: string, data?: Record<string, unknown>): void {
   36|   const prefix = `[${new Date().toISOString()}] [archiveEngine]`;
   37|   if (!data) {
   38|     console.log(`${prefix} ${message}`);
   39|     return;
   40|   }
   41|   console.log(`${prefix} ${message}`, data);
   42| }
   43| 
   44| async function tableExists(table: string): Promise<boolean> {
   45|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   46| 
   47|   // Best-effort probe: select 0 rows.
   48|   const { error } = await supabase.from(table).select("*").limit(1);
   49|   return !error;
   50| }
   51| 
   52| async function moveMacroEventsBatch(params: {
   53|   sourceTable: string;
   54|   batchSize: number;
   55|   olderThanIso: string;
   56| }): Promise<number> {
   57|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   58| 
   59|   const { data: idsRows, error: idsError } = await supabase
   60|     .from(params.sourceTable)
   61|     .select("id")
   62|     .lt("published_at", params.olderThanIso)
   63|     .order("published_at", { ascending: true })
   64|     .limit(params.batchSize);
   65| 
   66|   if (idsError) {
   67|     log("failed selecting macro event ids", { table: params.sourceTable, error: idsError.message });
   68|     return 0;
   69|   }
   70| 
   71|   const ids = ((idsRows as Array<{ id: string }> | null) ?? [])
   72|     .map((r) => (r.id ?? "").toString().trim())
   73|     .filter(Boolean);
   74| 
   75|   if (ids.length === 0) return 0;
   76| 
   77|   const { data: rows, error: rowsError } = await supabase
   78|     .from(params.sourceTable)
   79|     .select(
   80|       "id,title,description,source,url,published_at,ingested_at,processed,category,geography,industries",
   81|     )
   82|     .in("id", ids);
   83| 
   84|   if (rowsError) {
   85|     log("failed loading macro event rows", { table: params.sourceTable, error: rowsError.message });
   86|     return 0;
   87|   }
   88| 
   89|   const toInsert = ((rows as MacroEventRow[] | null) ?? []).map((r) => ({
   90|     ...r,
   91|     archived_at: new Date().toISOString(),
   92|   }));
   93| 
   94|   if (toInsert.length === 0) return 0;
   95| 
   96|   // Idempotent: upsert on primary key id.
   97|   const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("macro_events_archive").upsert(toInsert, {
   98|     onConflict: "id",
   99|     ignoreDuplicates: true,
  100|   });
  101| 
  102|   if (insertError) {
  103|     log("failed inserting archive rows", { error: insertError.message });
  104|     return 0;
  105|   }
  106| 
  107|   const { error: deleteError } = await supabase.from(params.sourceTable).delete().in("id", ids);
  108| 
  109|   if (deleteError) {
  110|     // Safe to rerun (upsert above is idempotent).
  111|     log("failed deleting source rows after archival", { table: params.sourceTable, error: deleteError.message });
  112|     return 0;
  113|   }
  114| 
  115|   return ids.length;
  116| }
  117| 
  118| async function deleteOldRowsBatch(params: {
  119|   table: string;
  120|   timeColumn: string;
  121|   olderThanIso: string;
  122|   batchSize: number;
  123| }): Promise<number> {
  124|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  125| 
  126|   const { data: idsRows, error: idsError } = await supabase
  127|     .from(params.table)
  128|     .select("id")
  129|     .lt(params.timeColumn, params.olderThanIso)
  130|     .order(params.timeColumn, { ascending: true })
  131|     .limit(params.batchSize);
  132| 
  133|   if (idsError) {
  134|     log("failed selecting ids for deletion", {
  135|       table: params.table,
  136|       error: idsError.message,
  137|     });
  138|     return 0;
  139|   }
  140| 
  141|   const ids = ((idsRows as Array<{ id: string }> | null) ?? [])
  142|     .map((r) => (r.id ?? "").toString().trim())
  143|     .filter(Boolean);
  144| 
  145|   if (ids.length === 0) return 0;
  146| 
  147|   const { error: deleteError } = await supabase.from(params.table).delete().in("id", ids);
  148| 
  149|   if (deleteError) {
  150|     log("failed deleting old rows", { table: params.table, error: deleteError.message });
  151|     return 0;
  152|   }
  153| 
  154|   return ids.length;
  155| }
  156| 
  157| export type ArchiveEngineResult = {
  158|   macroEventsArchived: number;
  159|   pipelineEventsDeleted: number;
  160|   stageRuntimeDeleted: number;
  161|   failuresDeleted: number;
  162| };
  163| 
  164| /**
  165|  * Runs a single archival pass using bounded batches.
  166|  * Safe to run multiple times.
  167|  */
  168| export async function runArchiveEngineOnce(): Promise<ArchiveEngineResult> {
  169|   const batchSize = envInt("ARCHIVE_BATCH_SIZE", 500);
  170|   const maxBatches = envInt("ARCHIVE_MAX_BATCHES", 50);
  171| 
  172|   const macroOlderThanIso = daysAgoIso(30);
  173|   const pipelineOlderThanIso = daysAgoIso(7);
  174|   const runtimeOlderThanIso = daysAgoIso(14);
  175|   const failureOlderThanIso = daysAgoIso(30);
  176| 
  177|   const sourceTable = (await tableExists("macro_events")) ? "macro_events" : "macro_events_raw";
  178| 
  179|   let macroEventsArchived = 0;
  180|   let pipelineEventsDeleted = 0;
  181|   let stageRuntimeDeleted = 0;
  182|   let failuresDeleted = 0;
  183| 
  184|   log("starting archival pass", {
  185|     sourceTable,
  186|     batchSize,
  187|     maxBatches,
  188|     macroOlderThanIso,
  189|     pipelineOlderThanIso,
  190|     runtimeOlderThanIso,
  191|     failureOlderThanIso,
  192|   });
  193| 
  194|   // 1) Archive old macro events.
  195|   for (let i = 0; i < maxBatches; i += 1) {
  196|     const moved = await moveMacroEventsBatch({
  197|       sourceTable,
  198|       batchSize,
  199|       olderThanIso: macroOlderThanIso,
  200|     });
  201|     macroEventsArchived += moved;
  202|     if (moved === 0) break;
  203|     await sleep(100);
  204|   }
  205| 
  206|   // 2) Delete old pipeline events.
  207|   for (let i = 0; i < maxBatches; i += 1) {
  208|     const deleted = await deleteOldRowsBatch({
  209|       table: "pipeline_events",
  210|       timeColumn: "created_at",
  211|       olderThanIso: pipelineOlderThanIso,
  212|       batchSize,
  213|     });
  214|     pipelineEventsDeleted += deleted;
  215|     if (deleted === 0) break;
  216|     await sleep(50);
  217|   }
  218| 
  219|   // 3) Delete old stage runtime rows.
  220|   for (let i = 0; i < maxBatches; i += 1) {
  221|     const deleted = await deleteOldRowsBatch({
  222|       table: "pipeline_stage_runtime",
  223|       timeColumn: "end_time",
  224|       olderThanIso: runtimeOlderThanIso,
  225|       batchSize,
  226|     });
  227|     stageRuntimeDeleted += deleted;
  228|     if (deleted === 0) break;
  229|     await sleep(50);
  230|   }
  231| 
  232|   // 4) Delete old failures.
  233|   for (let i = 0; i < maxBatches; i += 1) {
  234|     const deleted = await deleteOldRowsBatch({
  235|       table: "pipeline_failures",
  236|       timeColumn: "occurred_at",
  237|       olderThanIso: failureOlderThanIso,
  238|       batchSize,
  239|     });
  240|     failuresDeleted += deleted;
  241|     if (deleted === 0) break;
  242|     await sleep(50);
  243|   }
  244| 
  245|   log("archival pass completed", {
  246|     macroEventsArchived,
  247|     pipelineEventsDeleted,
  248|     stageRuntimeDeleted,
  249|     failuresDeleted,
  250|   });
  251| 
  252|   return {
  253|     macroEventsArchived,
  254|     pipelineEventsDeleted,
  255|     stageRuntimeDeleted,
  256|     failuresDeleted,
  257|   };
  258| }
  259| 
  260| export async function runArchiveEngineDaily(): Promise<void> {
  261|   const intervalMs = envInt("ARCHIVE_INTERVAL_MS", 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  262|   log("starting daily scheduler", { intervalMs });
  263| 
  264|   while (true) {
  265|     try {
  266|       await runArchiveEngineOnce();
  267|     } catch (err) {
  268|       log("archival pass failed", {
  269|         error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
  270|       });
  271|     }
  272| 
  273|     await sleep(intervalMs);
  274|   }
  275| }
  276| 
  277| function isMainModule(): boolean {
  278|   try {
  279|     const current = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
  280|     const invoked = process.argv[1] ?? "";
  281|     const invokedAbs = path.resolve(process.cwd(), invoked);
  282|     return path.normalize(invokedAbs).toLowerCase() === path.normalize(current).toLowerCase();
  283|   } catch {
  284|     return false;
  285|   }
  286| }
  287| 
  288| // Runnable via: npx tsx services/archiveEngine.ts
  289| if (isMainModule()) {
  290|   runArchiveEngineDaily().catch((err) => {
  291|     console.error(err);
  292|     process.exit(1);
  293|   });
  294| }

===== FILE: services\backupService.ts =====

    1| import { createWriteStream } from "fs";
    2| import { mkdir, rename } from "fs/promises";
    3| import path from "path";
    4| 
    5| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    6| 
    7| type TableBackupSpec = {
    8|   table: string;
    9|   orderBy: string;
   10| };
   11| 
   12| const CRITICAL_TABLES: TableBackupSpec[] = [
   13|   { table: "macro_events_raw", orderBy: "id" },
   14|   { table: "event_clusters", orderBy: "id" },
   15|   { table: "event_insights", orderBy: "id" },
   16|   { table: "portfolio_signals", orderBy: "id" },
   17|   { table: "user_feed", orderBy: "id" },
   18| ];
   19| 
   20| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
   21|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   22| }
   23| 
   24| function timestampForFilename(d: Date): string {
   25|   // Example: 2026-03-14T12-34-56Z
   26|   return d.toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, "-");
   27| }
   28| 
   29| async function waitForDrain(stream: NodeJS.WritableStream): Promise<void> {
   30|   await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
   31|     stream.once("drain", resolve);
   32|     stream.once("error", reject);
   33|   });
   34| }
   35| 
   36| async function writeChunk(stream: NodeJS.WritableStream, chunk: string): Promise<void> {
   37|   const ok = stream.write(chunk);
   38|   if (!ok) {
   39|     await waitForDrain(stream);
   40|   }
   41| }
   42| 
   43| async function streamTableToJsonFile(params: {
   44|   table: string;
   45|   orderBy: string;
   46|   outDir: string;
   47|   timestamp: string;
   48|   pageSize?: number;
   49| }): Promise<{ filePath: string; rowCount: number } | null> {
   50|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   51|   const pageSize = params.pageSize ?? 1000;
   52| 
   53|   // Best-effort existence check (some environments may not have all tables).
   54|   const probe = await supabase.from(params.table).select(params.orderBy).limit(1);
   55|   if (probe.error) {
   56|     console.warn(`[backupService] Skipping missing/unreadable table: ${params.table} (${probe.error.message})`);
   57|     return null;
   58|   }
   59| 
   60|   const baseName = `${params.table}_${params.timestamp}.json`;
   61|   const finalPath = path.join(params.outDir, baseName);
   62|   const tmpPath = `${finalPath}.tmp`;
   63| 
   64|   const stream = createWriteStream(tmpPath, { encoding: "utf8" });
   65| 
   66|   let wroteAny = false;
   67|   let total = 0;
   68| 
   69|   try {
   70|     await writeChunk(stream, "[\n");
   71| 
   72|     for (let from = 0; ; from += pageSize) {
   73|       const { data, error } = await supabase
   74|         .from(params.table)
   75|         .select("*")
   76|         .order(params.orderBy, { ascending: true })
   77|         .range(from, from + pageSize - 1);
   78| 
   79|       if (error) {
   80|         console.warn(`[backupService] Failed to export ${params.table}: ${error.message}`);
   81|         break;
   82|       }
   83| 
   84|       const rows = (data as unknown[] | null) ?? [];
   85|       for (const row of rows) {
   86|         const json = JSON.stringify(row);
   87|         if (wroteAny) {
   88|           await writeChunk(stream, ",\n");
   89|         }
   90|         await writeChunk(stream, json);
   91|         wroteAny = true;
   92|         total += 1;
   93|       }
   94| 
   95|       if (rows.length < pageSize) break;
   96|     }
   97| 
   98|     await writeChunk(stream, "\n]\n");
   99| 
  100|     await new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
  101|       stream.end(() => resolve());
  102|       stream.once("error", reject);
  103|     });
  104| 
  105|     await rename(tmpPath, finalPath);
  106|     return { filePath: finalPath, rowCount: total };
  107|   } catch (err) {
  108|     console.error(`[backupService] Export failed for ${params.table}`, err);
  109| 
  110|     // Best-effort: attempt to close stream; leaving tmp file is acceptable.
  111|     try {
  112|       stream.end();
  113|     } catch {
  114|       // ignore
  115|     }
  116| 
  117|     return null;
  118|   }
  119| }
  120| 
  121| export async function runBackupOnce(): Promise<void> {
  122|   const started = Date.now();
  123|   const timestamp = timestampForFilename(new Date());
  124|   const outDir = path.resolve(process.cwd(), "backups");
  125| 
  126|   try {
  127|     await mkdir(outDir, { recursive: true });
  128|   } catch (err) {
  129|     console.error("[backupService] Failed to create backups directory", err);
  130|     return;
  131|   }
  132| 
  133|   const results: Array<{ table: string; rows: number } > = [];
  134| 
  135|   for (const spec of CRITICAL_TABLES) {
  136|     try {
  137|       const result = await streamTableToJsonFile({
  138|         table: spec.table,
  139|         orderBy: spec.orderBy,
  140|         outDir,
  141|         timestamp,
  142|       });
  143| 
  144|       if (result) {
  145|         results.push({ table: spec.table, rows: result.rowCount });
  146|         console.log(`[backupService] Wrote ${spec.table} rows=${result.rowCount} -> ${path.basename(result.filePath)}`);
  147|       }
  148|     } catch (err) {
  149|       // Backups are best-effort and must not take down any long-running process.
  150|       console.error(`[backupService] Table backup failed: ${spec.table}`, err);
  151|     }
  152|   }
  153| 
  154|   const tookMs = Date.now() - started;
  155|   console.log(
  156|     `[backupService] Snapshot complete tables=${results.length}/${CRITICAL_TABLES.length} took_ms=${tookMs}`,
  157|   );
  158| }
  159| 
  160| /**
  161|  * Runs the backup snapshot loop.
  162|  *
  163|  * Intended to be run as a separate background process.
  164|  * Backups are best-effort and should never block the main pipeline.
  165|  */
  166| export async function runBackupService(): Promise<void> {
  167|   console.log("[backupService] starting");
  168| 
  169|   // Run once on startup.
  170|   try {
  171|     await runBackupOnce();
  172|   } catch (err) {
  173|     console.error("[backupService] initial snapshot failed", err);
  174|   }
  175| 
  176|   while (true) {
  177|     await sleep(12 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  178| 
  179|     try {
  180|       await runBackupOnce();
  181|     } catch (err) {
  182|       console.error("[backupService] snapshot failed", err);
  183|     }
  184|   }
  185| }
  186| 
  187| /**
  188|  * Starts the backup loop on a timer and returns immediately.
  189|  *
  190|  * This is suitable for running alongside the main pipeline in the same process
  191|  * without blocking it.
  192|  */
  193| export function startBackupService(): void {
  194|   console.log("[backupService] starting (timer mode)");
  195| 
  196|   let running = false;
  197| 
  198|   const run = async () => {
  199|     if (running) return;
  200|     running = true;
  201|     try {
  202|       await runBackupOnce();
  203|     } catch (err) {
  204|       console.error("[backupService] snapshot failed", err);
  205|     } finally {
  206|       running = false;
  207|     }
  208|   };
  209| 
  210|   // Fire and forget.
  211|   void run();
  212|   setInterval(() => {
  213|     void run();
  214|   }, 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  215| }

===== FILE: services\clusterEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { generateClusterKey } from "@/lib/clusterKey";
    3| 
    4| type MacroEvent = {
    5|   id: string;
    6|   title: string;
    7|   cluster_key: string | null;
    8| };
    9| 
   10| type EventCluster = {
   11|   id: string;
   12| };
   13| 
   14| export async function runIncrementalClustering(): Promise<void> {
   15|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   16| 
   17|   const { data: newEvents, error: newEventsError } = await supabase
   18|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   19|     .select("id,title,cluster_key")
   20|     .eq("clustered", false)
   21|     .limit(100);
   22| 
   23|   if (newEventsError) {
   24|     throw new Error(`Failed to load unclustered events: ${newEventsError.message}`);
   25|   }
   26| 
   27|   if (!newEvents?.length) return;
   28| 
   29|   for (const event of newEvents as MacroEvent[]) {
   30|     const clusterKey = event.cluster_key ?? generateClusterKey(event.title);
   31| 
   32|     if (!clusterKey) {
   33|       await supabase
   34|         .from("macro_events_raw")
   35|         .update({ clustered: true })
   36|         .eq("id", event.id);
   37|       continue;
   38|     }
   39| 
   40|     const { data: existingCluster, error: existingClusterError } = await supabase
   41|       .from("event_clusters")
   42|       .select("id")
   43|       .eq("title", clusterKey)
   44|       .limit(1)
   45|       .maybeSingle();
   46| 
   47|     if (existingClusterError) {
   48|       throw new Error(
   49|         `Failed to load existing cluster: ${existingClusterError.message}`,
   50|       );
   51|     }
   52| 
   53|     let clusterId: string;
   54| 
   55|     if (existingCluster) {
   56|       clusterId = (existingCluster as EventCluster).id;
   57|     } else {
   58|       const { data: newCluster, error: newClusterError } = await supabase
   59|         .from("event_clusters")
   60|         .insert({
   61|           title: clusterKey,
   62|           summary: event.title,
   63|           article_count: 1,
   64|         })
   65|         .select("id")
   66|         .single();
   67| 
   68|       if (newClusterError) {
   69|         throw new Error(`Failed to create cluster: ${newClusterError.message}`);
   70|       }
   71| 
   72|       clusterId = (newCluster as EventCluster).id;
   73|     }
   74| 
   75|     const { error: updateError } = await supabase
   76|       .from("macro_events_raw")
   77|       .update({
   78|         cluster_id: clusterId,
   79|         clustered: true,
   80|       })
   81|       .eq("id", event.id);
   82| 
   83|     if (updateError) {
   84|       throw new Error(`Failed to mark event clustered: ${updateError.message}`);
   85|     }
   86|   }
   87| }

===== FILE: services\eventCanonicalizer.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| 
    3| type ClusterRow = {
    4|   id: string;
    5| };
    6| 
    7| type ArticleRow = {
    8|   title: string | null;
    9|   description: string | null;
   10|   published_at?: string | null;
   11| };
   12| 
   13| function normalizeTitlePattern(title: string): string {
   14|   return title
   15|     .toLowerCase()
   16|     .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s]/g, " ")
   17|     .replace(/\s+/g, " ")
   18|     .trim();
   19| }
   20| 
   21| function pickCanonicalTitle(articles: ArticleRow[]): string {
   22|   // Prefer the most frequent title "pattern"; fallback to first non-empty title.
   23|   const counts = new Map<string, { count: number; firstIndex: number; raw: string }>();
   24| 
   25|   for (let index = 0; index < articles.length; index += 1) {
