   26|     const raw = (articles[index]?.title ?? "").toString().trim();
   27|     if (!raw) continue;
   28| 
   29|     const pattern = normalizeTitlePattern(raw);
   30|     if (!pattern) continue;
   31| 
   32|     const existing = counts.get(pattern);
   33|     if (existing) {
   34|       existing.count += 1;
   35|       continue;
   36|     }
   37| 
   38|     counts.set(pattern, { count: 1, firstIndex: index, raw });
   39|   }
   40| 
   41|   let best: { count: number; firstIndex: number; raw: string } | null = null;
   42|   for (const entry of counts.values()) {
   43|     if (!best) {
   44|       best = entry;
   45|       continue;
   46|     }
   47| 
   48|     if (entry.count > best.count) {
   49|       best = entry;
   50|       continue;
   51|     }
   52| 
   53|     if (entry.count === best.count && entry.firstIndex < best.firstIndex) {
   54|       best = entry;
   55|     }
   56|   }
   57| 
   58|   if (best?.raw) return best.raw;
   59| 
   60|   for (const a of articles) {
   61|     const t = (a.title ?? "").toString().trim();
   62|     if (t) return t;
   63|   }
   64| 
   65|   return "";
   66| }
   67| 
   68| function buildCanonicalSummary(articles: ArticleRow[]): string {
   69|   const parts: string[] = [];
   70| 
   71|   for (const a of articles) {
   72|     const d = (a.description ?? "").toString().trim();
   73|     if (!d) continue;
   74|     parts.push(d);
   75|     if (parts.length >= 5) break;
   76|   }
   77| 
   78|   return parts.join(" ");
   79| }
   80| 
   81| export async function runCanonicalizer(): Promise<void> {
   82|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   83| 
   84|   // 1) Load clusters that do not yet have canonical entries.
   85|   // Supabase/PostgREST doesn't support NOT IN (subquery) directly via the query builder,
   86|   // so we use a left join and filter nulls (equivalent semantics).
   87|   const { data: clusters, error: clustersError } = await supabase
   88|     .from("event_clusters")
   89|     .select("id, canonical_events!left(cluster_id)")
   90|     .is("canonical_events.cluster_id", null)
   91|     .limit(20);
   92| 
   93|   if (clustersError) {
   94|     throw new Error(`Failed to load clusters: ${clustersError.message}`);
   95|   }
   96| 
   97|   const clusterRows = (clusters as Array<ClusterRow & { canonical_events?: unknown }> | null) ?? [];
   98|   if (clusterRows.length === 0) return;
   99| 
  100|   for (const cluster of clusterRows) {
  101|     const clusterId = (cluster.id ?? "").toString().trim();
  102|     if (!clusterId) continue;
  103| 
  104|     // 2) Fetch articles in each cluster
  105|     const { data: articles, error: articlesError } = await supabase
  106|       .from("macro_events_raw")
  107|       .select("title,description,published_at")
  108|       .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  109|       .order("published_at", { ascending: true })
  110|       .limit(200);
  111| 
  112|     if (articlesError) {
  113|       throw new Error(
  114|         `Failed to load cluster articles: ${articlesError.message} (cluster_id=${clusterId})`,
  115|       );
  116|     }
  117| 
  118|     const articleRows = (articles as ArticleRow[] | null) ?? [];
  119|     if (articleRows.length === 0) continue;
  120| 
  121|     // 3) Choose canonical title
  122|     const canonicalTitle = pickCanonicalTitle(articleRows);
  123| 
  124|     // 4) Generate canonical summary
  125|     const canonicalSummary = buildCanonicalSummary(articleRows);
  126| 
  127|     // 5) Upsert canonical event (idempotent on cluster_id)
  128|     // - Updates canonical_title, canonical_summary, article_count
  129|     // - Preserves created_at by not including it in the payload
  130|     const { error: upsertError } = await supabase.from("canonical_events").upsert(
  131|       {
  132|         cluster_id: clusterId,
  133|         canonical_title: canonicalTitle,
  134|         canonical_summary: canonicalSummary,
  135|         article_count: articleRows.length,
  136|       },
  137|       {
  138|         onConflict: "cluster_id",
  139|       },
  140|     );
  141| 
  142|     if (upsertError) {
  143|       throw new Error(
  144|         `Failed to upsert canonical event: ${upsertError.message} (cluster_id=${clusterId})`,
  145|       );
  146|     }
  147|   }
  148| }

===== FILE: services\eventClustering.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { findSimilarEvents } from "@/lib/vectorSearch";
    3| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";
    4| import { generateClusterKey } from "@/lib/clusterKey";
    5| 
    6| type MacroEventRow = {
    7|   id: string;
    8|   title: string;
    9|   description: string;
   10|   published_at: string | null;
   11|   time_bucket: string | null;
   12|   embedding: number[] | null;
   13|   cluster_key?: string | null;
   14|   cluster_id: string | null;
   15|   clustered: boolean;
   16| };
   17| 
   18| export async function runEventClustering(): Promise<void> {
   19|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   20| 
   21|   const diagnostics = {
   22|     rowsLoaded: 0,
   23|     nullEmbedding: 0,
   24|     clusterKeysGenerated: 0,
   25|     clustersInserted: 0,
   26|     assignedToExistingCluster: 0,
   27|   };
   28| 
   29|   const { data: checkpoint, error: checkpointError } = await supabase
   30|     .from("clustering_checkpoints")
   31|     .select("id,last_processed_event")
   32|     .single();
   33| 
   34|   if (checkpointError) {
   35|     throw new Error(`Failed to load clustering checkpoint: ${checkpointError.message}`);
   36|   }
   37| 
   38|   const lastProcessed = (() => {
   39|     const value = (checkpoint as { last_processed_event?: unknown } | null)
   40|       ?.last_processed_event;
   41|     if (value instanceof Date) return value;
   42|     if (typeof value === "string" || typeof value === "number") {
   43|       const parsed = new Date(value);
   44|       if (!Number.isNaN(parsed.getTime())) return parsed;
   45|     }
   46|     return new Date(0);
   47|   })();
   48| 
   49|   const lastProcessedIso = lastProcessed.toISOString();
   50| 
   51|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
   52|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   53|     .select("*")
   54|     .eq("clustered", false)
   55|     .gte("published_at", lastProcessedIso)
   56|     .order("published_at", { ascending: true })
   57|     .limit(50);
   58| 
   59|   if (error) {
   60|     throw new Error(`Failed to load events: ${error.message}`);
   61|   }
   62| 
   63|   diagnostics.rowsLoaded = events?.length ?? 0;
   64|   console.log(`[eventClustering] Loaded ${diagnostics.rowsLoaded} macro_events_raw rows`);
   65| 
   66|   if (!events?.length) return;
   67| 
   68|   let lastCheckpointIso: string | null = null;
   69| 
   70|   for (const event of events as MacroEventRow[]) {
   71|     const existingClusterKey = (event.cluster_key ?? "").toString().trim();
   72|     if (!existingClusterKey) {
   73|       const generated = generateClusterKey(event.title);
   74|       if (generated) diagnostics.clusterKeysGenerated += 1;
   75|     }
   76| 
   77|     const embedding = Array.isArray(event.embedding) ? event.embedding : null;
   78|     if (!embedding) diagnostics.nullEmbedding += 1;
   79|     const similar = embedding
   80|       ? await findSimilarEvents(embedding, event.time_bucket)
   81|       : [];
   82| 
   83|     let clusterId: string | null | undefined;
   84| 
   85|     if (similar.length > 0) {
   86|       diagnostics.assignedToExistingCluster += 1;
   87|       const { data: cluster, error: clusterError } = await supabase
   88|         .from("macro_events_raw")
   89|         .select("cluster_id")
   90|         .eq("id", similar[0].id)
   91|         .single();
   92| 
   93|       if (clusterError) {
   94|         throw new Error(`Failed to load cluster_id: ${clusterError.message}`);
   95|       }
   96| 
   97|       clusterId = (cluster as { cluster_id: string | null } | null)?.cluster_id;
   98|     } else {
   99|       const { data: newCluster, error: newClusterError } = await supabase
  100|         .from("event_clusters")
  101|         .insert({
  102|           title: event.title,
  103|           summary: event.title,
  104|           article_count: 1,
  105|         })
  106|         .select("id")
  107|         .single();
  108| 
  109|       if (newClusterError) {
  110|         throw new Error(`Failed to create cluster: ${newClusterError.message}`);
  111|       }
  112| 
  113|       clusterId = (newCluster as { id: string }).id;
  114| 
  115|       diagnostics.clustersInserted += 1;
  116| 
  117|       await emitClusterEventOnce({
  118|         supabase,
  119|         eventType: "CLUSTER_CREATED",
  120|         clusterId,
  121|       });
  122|     }
  123| 
  124|     if (clusterId && clusterId !== "null") {
  125|       const published = event.published_at;
  126|       const publishedDate = published ? new Date(published) : new Date();
  127|       if (!Number.isNaN(publishedDate.getTime())) {
  128|         lastCheckpointIso = publishedDate.toISOString();
  129|       }
  130|     }
  131| 
  132|     const { error: updateError } = await supabase
  133|       .from("macro_events_raw")
  134|       .update({
  135|         cluster_id: clusterId,
  136|         clustered: true,
  137|       })
  138|       .eq("id", event.id);
  139| 
  140|     if (updateError) {
  141|       throw new Error(`Failed to update event: ${updateError.message}`);
  142|     }
  143| 
  144|     if (!clusterId) {
  145|       continue;
  146|     }
  147| 
  148|     const titleProbe = event.title.slice(0, 40);
  149|     const { data: existingStage, error: existingStageError } = await supabase
  150|       .from("event_timelines")
  151|       .select("id")
  152|       .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  153|       .ilike("title", `%${titleProbe}%`)
  154|       .limit(1);
  155| 
  156|     if (existingStageError) {
  157|       throw new Error(
  158|         `Failed to check existing timeline stage: ${existingStageError.message}`,
  159|       );
  160|     }
  161| 
  162|     if (!existingStage?.length) {
  163|       const { count, error: countError } = await supabase
  164|         .from("event_timelines")
  165|         .select("*", { count: "exact", head: true })
  166|         .eq("cluster_id", clusterId);
  167| 
  168|       if (countError) {
  169|         throw new Error(`Failed to count timeline stages: ${countError.message}`);
  170|       }
  171| 
  172|       const stage = (count ?? 0) + 1;
  173| 
  174|       const { error: insertError } = await supabase
  175|         .from("event_timelines")
  176|         .insert({
  177|           cluster_id: clusterId,
  178|           stage,
  179|           title: event.title,
  180|           description: event.description,
  181|           event_timestamp: event.published_at ?? new Date(),
  182|         });
  183| 
  184|       if (insertError) {
  185|         throw new Error(`Failed to insert timeline record: ${insertError.message}`);
  186|       }
  187|     }
  188|   }
  189| 
  190|   console.log(
  191|     `[eventClustering] Diagnostics: nullEmbedding=${diagnostics.nullEmbedding}, clusterKeysGenerated=${diagnostics.clusterKeysGenerated}, clustersInserted=${diagnostics.clustersInserted}`,
  192|   );
  193| 
  194|   if (diagnostics.rowsLoaded > 0 && diagnostics.clustersInserted === 0) {
  195|     const reason =
  196|       diagnostics.assignedToExistingCluster === diagnostics.rowsLoaded
  197|         ? "all loaded events matched existing clusters (vector similarity found matches)"
  198|         : diagnostics.nullEmbedding === diagnostics.rowsLoaded
  199|           ? "all loaded events had null embeddings (vector similarity skipped)"
  200|           : "no new clusters were inserted for the loaded events";
  201| 
  202|     console.warn(
  203|       `[eventClustering] WARNING: Loaded ${diagnostics.rowsLoaded} rows but created 0 clusters; ${reason}. assignedToExistingCluster=${diagnostics.assignedToExistingCluster}, nullEmbedding=${diagnostics.nullEmbedding}`,
  204|     );
  205|   }
  206| 
  207|   if (lastCheckpointIso) {
  208|     const checkpointId = (checkpoint as { id?: string } | null)?.id;
  209| 
  210|     const checkpointUpdate = checkpointId
  211|       ? await supabase
  212|           .from("clustering_checkpoints")
  213|           .update({ last_processed_event: lastCheckpointIso })
  214|           .eq("id", checkpointId)
  215|       : await supabase
  216|           .from("clustering_checkpoints")
  217|           .insert({ last_processed_event: lastCheckpointIso });
  218| 
  219|     if (checkpointUpdate.error) {
  220|       throw new Error(
  221|         `Failed to update clustering checkpoint: ${checkpointUpdate.error.message}`,
  222|       );
  223|     }
  224|   }
  225| }

===== FILE: services\eventProcessor.ts =====

    1| import { createHash } from "node:crypto";
    2| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    3| import { generateClusterKey } from "@/lib/clusterKey";
    4| 
    5| type QueuedEvent = {
    6|   id: string;
    7|   title: string | null;
    8|   description: string | null;
    9|   source: string | null;
   10|   url: string | null;
   11|   category: string | null;
   12|   geography: string | null;
   13|   industries: string[] | null;
   14|   published_at: string | null;
   15|   processed: boolean | null;
   16| };
   17| 
   18| function stableId(input: string): string {
   19|   return createHash("sha256").update(input).digest("hex");
   20| }
   21| 
   22| function toEpochMs(value: unknown): number {
   23|   if (typeof value === "number" && Number.isFinite(value)) return value;
   24| 
   25|   if (typeof value === "string") {
   26|     const parsed = Date.parse(value);
   27|     if (Number.isFinite(parsed)) return parsed;
   28|   }
   29| 
   30|   if (value instanceof Date) {
   31|     const ms = value.getTime();
   32|     if (Number.isFinite(ms)) return ms;
   33|   }
   34| 
   35|   return Date.now();
   36| }
   37| 
   38| export async function processEventQueue(): Promise<void> {
   39|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   40| 
   41|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   42|     .from("event_queue")
   43|     .select(
   44|       "id,title,description,source,url,category,geography,industries,published_at,processed",
   45|     )
   46|     .eq("processed", false)
   47|     .limit(50);
   48| 
   49|   if (error) {
   50|     throw new Error(`Failed to load event_queue: ${error.message}`);
   51|   }
   52| 
   53|   if (!data?.length) return;
   54| 
   55|   for (const event of data as QueuedEvent[]) {
   56|     if (!event.url || !event.title || !event.description || !event.source) {
   57|       await supabase
   58|         .from("event_queue")
   59|         .update({ processed: true })
   60|         .eq("id", event.id);
   61|       continue;
   62|     }
   63| 
   64|     const clusterKey = generateClusterKey(event.title);
   65| 
   66|     const timestamp = toEpochMs(event.published_at);
   67|     const id = stableId(
   68|       `${event.source}::${event.title}::${event.url}::${timestamp}`,
   69|     );
   70| 
   71|     const { error: upsertError } = await supabase.from("macro_events_raw").upsert(
   72|       {
   73|         id,
   74|         title: event.title,
   75|         description: event.description,
   76|         source: event.source,
   77|         url: event.url,
   78|         published_at: new Date(timestamp).toISOString(),
   79|         processed: false,
   80|         category: (event.category ?? "unknown").toString(),
   81|         geography: event.geography,
   82|         industries: event.industries,
   83|         cluster_key: clusterKey,
   84|       },
   85|       { onConflict: "url" },
   86|     );
   87| 
   88|     if (upsertError) {
   89|       throw new Error(`Failed to upsert macro_events_raw: ${upsertError.message}`);
   90|     }
   91| 
   92|     const { error: markError } = await supabase
   93|       .from("event_queue")
   94|       .update({ processed: true })
   95|       .eq("id", event.id);
   96| 
   97|     if (markError) {
   98|       throw new Error(`Failed to mark queue processed: ${markError.message}`);
   99|     }
  100|   }
  101| }

===== FILE: services\eventValidationEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    3| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";
    4| 
    5| type ClusterRow = {
    6|   id: string;
    7| };
    8| 
    9| function clamp(min: number, value: number, max: number): number {
   10|   return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
   11| }
   12| 
   13| async function getArticleCount(supabase: ReturnType<typeof createSupabaseServerClient>, clusterId: string): Promise<number> {
   14|   const { count, error } = await supabase
   15|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   16|     .select("id", { count: "exact", head: true })
   17|     .eq("cluster_id", clusterId);
   18| 
   19|   if (error) {
   20|     throw new Error(`Failed to count articles: ${error.message}`);
   21|   }
   22| 
   23|   return count ?? 0;
   24| }
   25| 
   26| async function getSourceDiversity(supabase: ReturnType<typeof createSupabaseServerClient>, clusterId: string): Promise<number> {
   27|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   28|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   29|     .select("source")
   30|     .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
   31|     .limit(200);
   32| 
   33|   if (error) {
   34|     throw new Error(`Failed to load sources: ${error.message}`);
   35|   }
   36| 
   37|   const sources = new Set<string>();
   38|   for (const row of (data as Array<{ source: string | null }> | null) ?? []) {
   39|     const s = (row.source ?? "").toString().trim();
   40|     if (s) sources.add(s);
   41|   }
   42| 
   43|   return sources.size;
   44| }
   45| 
   46| async function getTimeSpreadMs(
   47|   supabase: ReturnType<typeof createSupabaseServerClient>,
   48|   clusterId: string,
   49| ): Promise<number> {
   50|   const { data: earliest, error: earliestError } = await supabase
   51|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   52|     .select("published_at")
   53|     .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
   54|     .order("published_at", { ascending: true })
   55|     .limit(1);
   56| 
   57|   if (earliestError) {
   58|     throw new Error(`Failed to load earliest published_at: ${earliestError.message}`);
   59|   }
   60| 
   61|   const { data: latest, error: latestError } = await supabase
   62|     .from("macro_events_raw")
   63|     .select("published_at")
   64|     .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
   65|     .order("published_at", { ascending: false })
   66|     .limit(1);
   67| 
   68|   if (latestError) {
   69|     throw new Error(`Failed to load latest published_at: ${latestError.message}`);
   70|   }
   71| 
   72|   const minIso = (earliest?.[0] as { published_at?: string | null } | undefined)
   73|     ?.published_at;
   74|   const maxIso = (latest?.[0] as { published_at?: string | null } | undefined)
   75|     ?.published_at;
   76| 
   77|   const minMs = minIso ? Date.parse(minIso) : NaN;
   78|   const maxMs = maxIso ? Date.parse(maxIso) : NaN;
   79| 
   80|   if (!Number.isFinite(minMs) || !Number.isFinite(maxMs)) return 0;
   81|   return Math.max(0, maxMs - minMs);
   82| }
   83| 
   84| function computeValidationScore(params: {
   85|   articleCount: number;
   86|   sourceDiversity: number;
   87|   timeSpreadMs: number;
   88| }): number {
   89|   let score = 0;
   90| 
   91|   if (params.articleCount >= 5) score += 0.4;
   92|   if (params.sourceDiversity >= 3) score += 0.4;
   93|   if (params.timeSpreadMs >= 60 * 60 * 1000) score += 0.2;
   94| 
   95|   return clamp(0, score, 1);
   96| }
   97| 
   98| export async function runEventValidationEngine(): Promise<void> {
   99|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  100| 
  101|   const { data: clusters, error: clustersError } = await supabase
  102|     .from("event_clusters")
  103|     .select("id")
  104|     .eq("validated", false)
  105|     .limit(20);
  106| 
  107|   if (clustersError) {
  108|     throw new Error(`Failed to load clusters to validate: ${clustersError.message}`);
  109|   }
  110| 
  111|   const clusterRows = (clusters as ClusterRow[] | null) ?? [];
  112|   if (clusterRows.length === 0) return;
  113| 
  114|   for (const cluster of clusterRows) {
  115|     const clusterId = (cluster.id ?? "").toString().trim();
  116|     if (!clusterId) continue;
  117| 
  118|     await withStageSpan({
  119|       supabase,
  120|       stageName: "event_validation",
  121|       clusterId,
  122|       eventId: null,
  123|       fn: async () => {
  124|         const articleCount = await getArticleCount(supabase, clusterId);
  125|         const sourceDiversity = await getSourceDiversity(supabase, clusterId);
  126|         const timeSpreadMs = await getTimeSpreadMs(supabase, clusterId);
  127| 
  128|         const validationScore = computeValidationScore({
  129|           articleCount,
  130|           sourceDiversity,
  131|           timeSpreadMs,
  132|         });
  133| 
  134|         const validated = validationScore >= 0.6;
  135| 
  136|         const { error: updateError } = await supabase
  137|           .from("event_clusters")
  138|           .update({
  139|             validated,
  140|             validation_score: validationScore,
  141|           })
  142|           .eq("id", clusterId);
  143| 
  144|         if (updateError) {
  145|           throw new Error(
  146|             `Failed to update validation status: ${updateError.message} (cluster_id=${clusterId})`,
  147|           );
  148|         }
  149| 
  150|         if (validated) {
  151|           await emitClusterEventOnce({
  152|             supabase,
  153|             eventType: "CLUSTER_VALIDATED",
  154|             clusterId,
  155|           });
  156|         }
  157|       },
  158|     });
  159|   }
  160| }

===== FILE: services\factorEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    3| import { workerPoolForEach } from "./workerPool";
    4| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";
    5| 
    6| type PipelineEventRow = {
    7|   id: string;
    8|   payload: unknown;
    9| };
   10| 
   11| function extractClusterIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   12|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   13|   const clusterId = (payload as { cluster_id?: unknown }).cluster_id;
   14|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   15|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   16|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   17| }
   18| 
   19| export async function runFactorEngine(): Promise<void> {
   20|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   21| 
   22|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
   23|     .from("pipeline_events")
   24|     .select("id,payload")
   25|     .eq("event_type", "CLUSTER_CREATED")
   26|     .eq("processed", false)
   27|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   28|     .limit(20);
   29| 
   30|   if (error) {
   31|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
   32|   }
   33| 
   34|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
   35|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
   36| 
   37|   // Avoid processing the same cluster multiple times in a single run.
   38|   const seen = new Set<string>();
   39|   const unique: PipelineEventRow[] = [];
   40|   for (const evt of pending) {
   41|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
   42|     if (!clusterId) {
   43|       unique.push(evt);
   44|       continue;
   45|     }
   46|     if (seen.has(clusterId)) continue;
   47|     seen.add(clusterId);
   48|     unique.push(evt);
   49|   }
   50| 
   51|   await workerPoolForEach(
   52|     unique,
   53|     async (evt) => {
   54|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
   55|     await withStageSpan({
   56|       supabase,
   57|       stageName: "factor",
   58|       clusterId,
   59|       eventId: evt.id,
   60|       statusOnSuccess: clusterId ? "success" : "skipped",
   61|       fn: async () => {
   62|         if (!clusterId) {
   63|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
   64|             .from("pipeline_events")
   65|             .update({ processed: true })
   66|             .eq("id", evt.id);
   67|           if (markError) {
   68|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
   69|           }
   70|           return;
   71|         }
   72| 
   73|         const { data: cluster, error: clusterError } = await supabase
   74|           .from("event_clusters")
   75|           .select("id,title,validated,processed")
   76|           .eq("id", clusterId)
   77|           .maybeSingle();
   78| 
   79|         if (clusterError) {
   80|           throw new Error(`Failed to load cluster: ${clusterError.message}`);
   81|         }
   82| 
   83|         if (!cluster) {
   84|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
   85|             .from("pipeline_events")
   86|             .update({ processed: true })
   87|             .eq("id", evt.id);
   88|           if (markError) {
   89|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
   90|           }
   91|           return;
   92|         }
   93| 
   94|         // Preserve existing gating behavior: only process validated & unprocessed clusters.
   95|         if (cluster.processed) {
   96|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
   97|             .from("pipeline_events")
   98|             .update({ processed: true })
   99|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  100|           if (markError) {
  101|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  102|           }
  103|           return;
  104|         }
  105| 
  106|         if (!cluster.validated) {
  107|           // Leave the event unprocessed so it can be retried after validation.
  108|           return;
  109|         }
  110| 
  111|         // Idempotency: if factor exposures already exist, do not insert duplicates.
  112|         const { data: existingExposure, error: existingExposureError } = await supabase
  113|           .from("event_factor_exposures")
  114|           .select("id")
  115|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  116|           .limit(1);
  117| 
  118|         if (existingExposureError) {
  119|           throw new Error(
  120|             `Failed to check existing factor exposures: ${existingExposureError.message}`,
  121|           );
  122|         }
  123| 
  124|         const title = (cluster.title ?? "").toString().toLowerCase();
  125| 
  126|         const exposures: Array<{ factor: string; exposure: number }> = [];
  127| 
  128|         if (title.includes("rate") || title.includes("interest")) {
  129|           exposures.push(
  130|             { factor: "liquidity", exposure: -0.8 },
  131|             { factor: "growth", exposure: -0.3 },
  132|             { factor: "inflation", exposure: -0.4 },
  133|           );
  134|         }
  135| 
  136|         if (title.includes("oil") || title.includes("energy")) {
  137|           exposures.push(
  138|             { factor: "inflation", exposure: 0.7 },
  139|             { factor: "commodity_pressure", exposure: 0.6 },
  140|           );
  141|         }
  142| 
  143|         if (title.includes("war") || title.includes("conflict")) {
  144|           exposures.push({ factor: "risk_sentiment", exposure: -0.7 });
  145|         }
  146| 
  147|         if ((existingExposure ?? []).length === 0) {
  148|           for (const exposure of exposures) {
  149|             const { error: insertError } = await supabase
  150|               .from("event_factor_exposures")
  151|               .insert({
  152|                 cluster_id: clusterId,
  153|                 factor: exposure.factor,
  154|                 exposure: exposure.exposure,
  155|               });
  156| 
  157|             if (insertError) {
  158|               throw new Error(
  159|                 `Failed to insert factor exposure: ${insertError.message}`,
  160|               );
  161|             }
  162|           }
  163|         }
  164| 
  165|         const { error: markProcessedError } = await supabase
  166|           .from("event_clusters")
  167|           .update({ processed: true })
  168|           .eq("id", clusterId);
  169| 
  170|         if (markProcessedError) {
  171|           throw new Error(
  172|             `Failed to mark cluster processed: ${markProcessedError.message}`,
  173|           );
  174|         }
  175| 
  176|         const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  177|           .from("pipeline_events")
  178|           .update({ processed: true })
  179|           .eq("id", evt.id);
  180| 
  181|         if (markEventError) {
  182|           throw new Error(
  183|             `Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`,
  184|           );
  185|         }
  186| 
  187|         await emitClusterEventOnce({
  188|           supabase,
  189|           eventType: "FACTOR_CREATED",
  190|           clusterId,
  191|         });
  192|       },
  193|     });
  194|     },
  195|     { concurrency: Number(process.env.PIPELINE_CONCURRENCY ?? 5) || 5 },
  196|   );
  197| }

===== FILE: services\feedCacheEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| 
    3| type PipelineEventRow = {
    4|   id: string;
    5|   payload: unknown;
    6| };
    7| 
    8| type UserFeedRow = {
    9|   user_id: string | null;
   10|   insight_id: string | null;
   11|   relevance_score: number | null;
   12|   ranking_score?: number | null;
   13|   event_insights:
   14|     | {
   15|         insight: string | null;
   16|         created_at: string | null;
   17|         cluster_id: string | null;
   18|       }
   19|     | Array<{
   20|         insight: string | null;
   21|         created_at: string | null;
   22|         cluster_id: string | null;
   23|       }>
   24|     | null;
   25| };
   26| 
   27| type CanonicalEventRow = {
   28|   cluster_id: string;
   29|   canonical_title: string | null;
   30|   canonical_summary: string | null;
   31| };
   32| 
   33| type PortfolioSignalRow = {
   34|   cluster_id: string | null;
   35|   asset: string | null;
   36|   signal: string | null;
   37| };
   38| 
   39| type InsightTagRow = {
   40|   insight_id: string | null;
   41|   tag: string | null;
   42| };
   43| 
   44| export type FeedCardSignal = {
   45|   asset: string;
   46|   signal: string;
   47| };
   48| 
   49| export type FeedCard = {
   50|   headline: string;
   51|   summary: string;
   52|   signals: FeedCardSignal[];
   53|   tags: string[];
   54|   score: number;
   55|   timestamp: string;
   56| };
   57| 
   58| function getEmbeddedInsight(row: UserFeedRow):
   59|   | {
   60|       insight: string | null;
   61|       created_at: string | null;
   62|       cluster_id: string | null;
   63|     }
   64|   | null {
   65|   const embedded = row.event_insights;
   66|   if (!embedded) return null;
   67|   if (Array.isArray(embedded)) return embedded[0] ?? null;
   68|   return embedded;
   69| }
   70| 
   71| function extractUserIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   72|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   73|   const userId = (payload as { user_id?: unknown }).user_id;
   74|   if (typeof userId !== "string" && typeof userId !== "number") return null;
   75|   const trimmed = userId.toString().trim();
   76|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   77| }
   78| 
   79| function uniq<T>(items: T[]): T[] {
   80|   return Array.from(new Set(items));
   81| }
   82| 
   83| export async function runFeedCacheEngine(): Promise<void> {
   84|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   85| 
   86|   const { error: rankingProbeError } = await supabase
   87|     .from("user_feed")
   88|     .select("ranking_score")
   89|     .limit(1);
   90| 
   91|   const supportsRankingScore = !rankingProbeError;
   92| 
   93|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
   94|     .from("pipeline_events")
   95|     .select("id,payload")
   96|     .eq("event_type", "USER_FEED_DELTA")
   97|     .eq("processed", false)
   98|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   99|     .limit(50);
  100| 
  101|   if (error) {
  102|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
  103|   }
  104| 
  105|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
  106|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
  107| 
  108|   for (const evt of pending) {
  109|     const userId = extractUserIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
  110| 
  111|     if (!userId) {
  112|       const { error: markError } = await supabase
  113|         .from("pipeline_events")
  114|         .update({ processed: true })
  115|         .eq("id", evt.id);
  116| 
  117|       if (markError) {
  118|         throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  119|       }
  120| 
  121|       continue;
  122|     }
  123| 
  124|     const query = supportsRankingScore
  125|       ? supabase
  126|           .from("user_feed")
  127|           .select(
  128|             "user_id,insight_id,relevance_score,ranking_score,event_insights!inner(insight,created_at,cluster_id)",
  129|           )
  130|           .eq("user_id", userId)
  131|           .order("ranking_score", { ascending: false, nullsFirst: false })
  132|           .order("relevance_score", { ascending: false })
  133|           .limit(20)
  134|       : supabase
  135|           .from("user_feed")
  136|           .select(
  137|             "user_id,insight_id,relevance_score,event_insights!inner(insight,created_at,cluster_id)",
  138|           )
  139|           .eq("user_id", userId)
  140|           .order("relevance_score", { ascending: false })
  141|           .limit(20);
  142| 
  143|     const { data: rows, error: feedError } = await query;
  144| 
  145|     if (feedError) {
  146|       throw new Error(`Failed to load user feed for cache: ${feedError.message}`);
  147|     }
  148| 
  149|     const joined = ((rows as unknown as UserFeedRow[] | null) ?? []).filter(Boolean);
  150| 
  151|     const insightIds = uniq(
  152|       joined
  153|         .map((r) => (r.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim())
  154|         .filter(Boolean),
  155|     );
  156| 
  157|     const clusterIds = uniq(
  158|       joined
  159|         .map((r) => (getEmbeddedInsight(r)?.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim())
  160|         .filter(Boolean),
  161|     );
  162| 
  163|     // Fetch canonical headline/summary per cluster.
  164|     const canonicalByCluster = new Map<string, CanonicalEventRow>();
  165|     if (clusterIds.length > 0) {
  166|       const { data: canonicalRows, error: canonicalError } = await supabase
  167|         .from("canonical_events")
  168|         .select("cluster_id,canonical_title,canonical_summary")
  169|         .in("cluster_id", clusterIds)
  170|         .limit(2000);
  171| 
  172|       if (canonicalError) {
  173|         throw new Error(`Failed to load canonical events: ${canonicalError.message}`);
  174|       }
  175| 
  176|       for (const row of (canonicalRows as CanonicalEventRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  177|         if (!row?.cluster_id) continue;
  178|         canonicalByCluster.set(row.cluster_id, row);
  179|       }
  180|     }
  181| 
  182|     // Fetch portfolio signals per cluster.
  183|     const signalsByCluster = new Map<string, FeedCardSignal[]>();
  184|     if (clusterIds.length > 0) {
  185|       const { data: signalRows, error: signalsError } = await supabase
  186|         .from("portfolio_signals")
  187|         .select("cluster_id,asset,signal")
  188|         .in("cluster_id", clusterIds)
  189|         .order("created_at", { ascending: false })
  190|         .limit(5000);
  191| 
  192|       if (signalsError) {
  193|         throw new Error(`Failed to load portfolio signals: ${signalsError.message}`);
  194|       }
  195| 
  196|       for (const row of (signalRows as PortfolioSignalRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  197|         const clusterId = (row.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  198|         const asset = (row.asset ?? "").toString().trim();
  199|         const signal = (row.signal ?? "").toString().trim();
  200|         if (!clusterId || !asset || !signal) continue;
  201| 
  202|         const list = signalsByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? [];
  203|         // Keep it tight for cache payload size.
  204|         if (list.length < 10) {
  205|           list.push({ asset, signal });
  206|         }
  207|         signalsByCluster.set(clusterId, list);
  208|       }
  209|     }
  210| 
  211|     // Fetch tags per insight.
  212|     const tagsByInsight = new Map<string, string[]>();
  213|     if (insightIds.length > 0) {
  214|       const { data: tagRows, error: tagsError } = await supabase
  215|         .from("insight_tags")
  216|         .select("insight_id,tag")
  217|         .in("insight_id", insightIds)
  218|         .limit(5000);
  219| 
  220|       if (tagsError) {
  221|         throw new Error(`Failed to load insight tags: ${tagsError.message}`);
  222|       }
  223| 
  224|       for (const row of (tagRows as InsightTagRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  225|         const insightId = (row.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  226|         const tag = (row.tag ?? "").toString().trim();
  227|         if (!insightId || !tag) continue;
  228| 
  229|         const list = tagsByInsight.get(insightId) ?? [];
  230|         if (!list.includes(tag)) list.push(tag);
  231|         tagsByInsight.set(insightId, list);
  232|       }
  233|     }
  234| 
  235|     const feed: FeedCard[] = joined
  236|       .map((r) => {
  237|         const insightId = (r.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  238|         const rankingScore = Number(r.ranking_score);
  239|         const relevanceScore = Number(r.relevance_score);
  240|         const score = Number.isFinite(rankingScore) ? rankingScore : relevanceScore;
  241|         const embedded = getEmbeddedInsight(r);
  242|         const insightText = (embedded?.insight ?? "").toString().trim();
  243|         const clusterId = (embedded?.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  244|         const timestamp = (embedded?.created_at ?? "").toString().trim();
  245| 
  246|         if (!insightId || !Number.isFinite(score) || !timestamp) return null;
  247| 
  248|         const canonical = clusterId ? canonicalByCluster.get(clusterId) : undefined;
  249| 
  250|         const headline = (canonical?.canonical_title ?? insightText).toString().trim();
  251|         const summary = (canonical?.canonical_summary ?? insightText).toString().trim();
  252| 
  253|         return {
  254|           headline,
  255|           summary,
  256|           signals: clusterId ? signalsByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? [] : [],
  257|           tags: tagsByInsight.get(insightId) ?? [],
  258|           score,
  259|           timestamp,
  260|         } satisfies FeedCard;
  261|       })
  262|       .filter((c): c is FeedCard => Boolean(c && c.headline && c.summary));
  263| 
  264|     const nowIso = new Date().toISOString();
  265| 
  266|     const { error: upsertError } = await supabase
  267|       .from("user_feed_cache")
  268|       .upsert(
  269|         {
  270|           user_id: userId,
  271|           feed,
  272|           updated_at: nowIso,
  273|         },
  274|         { onConflict: "user_id" },
  275|       );
  276| 
  277|     if (upsertError) {
  278|       throw new Error(`Failed to upsert user_feed_cache: ${upsertError.message}`);
  279|     }
  280| 
  281|     const { error: markError } = await supabase
  282|       .from("pipeline_events")
  283|       .update({ processed: true })
  284|       .eq("id", evt.id);
  285| 
  286|     if (markError) {
  287|       throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  288|     }
  289|   }
  290| }

===== FILE: services\impactEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    3| import { workerPoolForEach } from "./workerPool";
    4| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";
    5| 
    6| type PipelineEventRow = {
    7|   id: string;
    8|   payload: unknown;
    9| };
   10| 
   11| function extractClusterIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   12|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   13|   const clusterId = (payload as { cluster_id?: unknown }).cluster_id;
   14|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   15|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   16|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   17| }
   18| 
   19| export async function runImpactEngine() {
   20|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   21| 
   22|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
   23|     .from("pipeline_events")
   24|     .select("id,payload")
   25|     .eq("event_type", "FACTOR_CREATED")
   26|     .eq("processed", false)
   27|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   28|     .limit(20);
   29| 
   30|   if (error) {
   31|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
   32|   }
   33| 
   34|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
   35|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
   36| 
   37|   const factorMap: Record<string, string[]> = {
   38|     equities: ["growth", "liquidity"],
   39|     bonds: ["inflation", "liquidity"],
   40|     real_estate: ["inflation", "liquidity"],
   41|   };
   42| 
   43|   // Avoid processing the same cluster multiple times in a single run.
   44|   const seen = new Set<string>();
   45|   const unique: PipelineEventRow[] = [];
   46|   for (const evt of pending) {
   47|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
   48|     if (!clusterId) {
   49|       unique.push(evt);
   50|       continue;
   51|     }
   52|     if (seen.has(clusterId)) continue;
   53|     seen.add(clusterId);
   54|     unique.push(evt);
   55|   }
   56| 
   57|   await workerPoolForEach(
   58|     unique,
   59|     async (evt) => {
   60|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
   61|     await withStageSpan({
   62|       supabase,
   63|       stageName: "impact",
   64|       clusterId,
   65|       eventId: evt.id,
   66|       statusOnSuccess: clusterId ? "success" : "skipped",
   67|       fn: async () => {
   68|         if (!clusterId) {
   69|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
   70|             .from("pipeline_events")
   71|             .update({ processed: true })
   72|             .eq("id", evt.id);
   73|           if (markError) {
   74|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
   75|           }
   76|           return;
   77|         }
   78| 
   79|         // Idempotency: if impact scores already exist, do not insert duplicates.
   80|         const { data: existingImpacts, error: existingImpactsError } = await supabase
   81|           .from("event_impact_scores")
   82|           .select("id")
   83|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
   84|           .limit(1);
   85| 
   86|         if (existingImpactsError) {
   87|           throw new Error(`Failed to check existing impact scores: ${existingImpactsError.message}`);
   88|         }
   89| 
   90|         if ((existingImpacts ?? []).length > 0) {
   91|           const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
   92|             .from("pipeline_events")
   93|             .update({ processed: true })
   94|             .eq("id", evt.id);
   95| 
   96|           if (markEventError) {
   97|             throw new Error(
   98|               `Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`,
   99|             );
  100|           }
  101| 
  102|           await emitClusterEventOnce({
  103|             supabase,
  104|             eventType: "SIGNAL_CREATED",
  105|             clusterId,
  106|           });
  107| 
  108|           return;
  109|         }
  110| 
  111|         const { data: exposures, error: exposuresError } = await supabase
  112|           .from("event_factor_exposures")
  113|           .select("factor,exposure")
  114|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId);
  115| 
  116|         if (exposuresError) {
  117|           throw new Error(
  118|             `Failed to load factor exposures: ${exposuresError.message}`,
  119|           );
  120|         }
  121| 
  122|         if (!exposures?.length) {
  123|           const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  124|             .from("pipeline_events")
  125|             .update({ processed: true })
  126|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  127| 
  128|           if (markEventError) {
  129|             throw new Error(
  130|               `Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`,
  131|             );
  132|           }
  133| 
  134|           return;
  135|         }
  136| 
  137|         const exposureByFactor = new Map<string, number>();
  138|         for (const row of exposures as Array<{ factor: string; exposure: number }>) {
  139|           const factor = (row.factor ?? "").toString();
  140|           const exposure = Number(row.exposure);
  141|           if (!factor || !Number.isFinite(exposure)) continue;
  142|           exposureByFactor.set(factor, (exposureByFactor.get(factor) ?? 0) + exposure);
  143|         }
  144| 
  145|         const impacts: Array<{ asset_class: string; impact_score: number }> = [];
  146|         for (const [assetClass, factors] of Object.entries(factorMap)) {
  147|           const contributions = factors.map((f) => exposureByFactor.get(f) ?? 0);
  148|           const impactScore = contributions.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  149|           if (impactScore === 0) continue;
  150|           impacts.push({ asset_class: assetClass, impact_score: impactScore });
  151|         }
  152| 
  153|         if (impacts.length === 0) {
  154|           const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  155|             .from("pipeline_events")
  156|             .update({ processed: true })
  157|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  158| 
  159|           if (markEventError) {
  160|             throw new Error(
  161|               `Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`,
  162|             );
  163|           }
  164| 
  165|           return;
  166|         }
  167| 
  168|         for (const impact of impacts) {
  169|           const { error: insertError } = await supabase
  170|             .from("event_impact_scores")
  171|             .insert({
  172|               cluster_id: clusterId,
  173|               asset_class: impact.asset_class,
  174|               impact_score: impact.impact_score,
  175|             });
  176| 
  177|           if (insertError) {
  178|             throw new Error(
  179|               `Failed to insert impact score: ${insertError.message}`,
  180|             );
  181|           }
  182|         }
  183| 
  184|         const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  185|           .from("pipeline_events")
  186|           .update({ processed: true })
  187|           .eq("id", evt.id);
  188| 
  189|         if (markEventError) {
  190|           throw new Error(
  191|             `Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`,
  192|           );
  193|         }
  194| 
  195|         await emitClusterEventOnce({
  196|           supabase,
  197|           eventType: "SIGNAL_CREATED",
  198|           clusterId,
  199|         });
  200|       },
  201|     });
  202|     },
  203|     { concurrency: Number(process.env.PIPELINE_CONCURRENCY ?? 5) || 5 },
  204|   );
  205| }

===== FILE: services\insightEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    3| import { workerPoolForEach } from "./workerPool";
    4| 
    5| type PipelineEventRow = {
    6|   id: string;
    7|   payload: unknown;
    8| };
    9| 
   10| function extractClusterIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   11|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   12|   const clusterId = (payload as { cluster_id?: unknown }).cluster_id;
   13|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   14|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   15|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   16| }
   17| 
   18| type PortfolioSignalRow = {
   19|   cluster_id: string | null;
   20|   asset: string | null;
   21|   signal: string | null;
   22|   confidence: number | null;
   23| };
   24| 
   25| type FactorExposureRow = {
   26|   factor: string | null;
   27|   exposure: number | null;
   28| };
   29| 
   30| type ExposureMap = {
   31|   inflation: number;
   32|   liquidity: number;
   33|   growth: number;
   34|   currency: number;
   35|   risk_sentiment: number;
   36|   commodity_pressure: number;
   37|   [key: string]: number;
   38| };
   39| 
   40| function clamp(min: number, value: number, max: number): number {
   41|   return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
   42| }
   43| 
   44| function avg(nums: number[]): number {
   45|   if (nums.length === 0) return 0;
   46|   return nums.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / nums.length;
   47| }
   48| 
   49| function normalizeSignal(signal: string | null | undefined): "BUY" | "SELL" | "NEUTRAL" {
   50|   const s = (signal ?? "").toString().trim().toUpperCase();
   51|   if (s === "BUY" || s === "SELL" || s === "NEUTRAL") return s;
   52|   return "NEUTRAL";
   53| }
   54| 
   55| function toExposureMap(rows: FactorExposureRow[]): ExposureMap {
   56|   const base: ExposureMap = {
   57|     inflation: 0,
   58|     liquidity: 0,
   59|     growth: 0,
   60|     currency: 0,
   61|     risk_sentiment: 0,
   62|     commodity_pressure: 0,
   63|   };
   64| 
   65|   for (const row of rows) {
   66|     const factor = (row.factor ?? "").toString().trim();
   67|     const exposure = Number(row.exposure);
   68|     if (!factor || !Number.isFinite(exposure)) continue;
   69|     base[factor] = (base[factor] ?? 0) + exposure;
   70|   }
   71| 
   72|   return base;
   73| }
   74| 
   75| function buildInsightText(
   76|   exposures: ExposureMap,
   77|   signals: Record<string, { signal: "BUY" | "SELL" | "NEUTRAL"; confidence: number }>,
   78| ): string {
   79|   const lines: string[] = [];
   80| 
   81|   const inflation = exposures.inflation ?? 0;
   82|   const liquidity = exposures.liquidity ?? 0;
   83|   const growth = exposures.growth ?? 0;
   84|   const risk = exposures.risk_sentiment ?? 0;
   85|   const commodity = exposures.commodity_pressure ?? 0;
   86| 
   87|   const bonds = signals.bonds?.signal;
   88|   const equities = signals.equities?.signal;
   89|   const commoditiesSig = signals.commodities?.signal;
   90|   const usd = signals.usd?.signal;
   91| 
   92|   // Examples requested in spec.
   93|   if (inflation > 0.5 && bonds === "SELL") {
   94|     lines.push(
   95|       "Rising inflation pressure may weaken bond prices due to expectations of higher interest rates.",
   96|     );
   97|   }
   98| 
   99|   if (liquidity < -0.5 && equities === "SELL") {
  100|     lines.push(
  101|       "Tighter liquidity conditions may create downside pressure for equity markets.",
  102|     );
  103|   }
  104| 
  105|   // Additional lightweight synthesis (still simple, no extra architecture).
  106|   if (inflation > 0.5 && commoditiesSig === "BUY") {
  107|     lines.push(
  108|       "Elevated inflation tends to support real assets, which can provide a tailwind for commodities.",
  109|     );
  110|   }
  111| 
  112|   if (risk < -0.5 && equities === "SELL") {
  113|     lines.push(
  114|       "Deteriorating risk sentiment often drives a defensive shift, weighing on equities and favoring safer exposures.",
  115|     );
  116|   }
  117| 
  118|   if (growth < -0.5 && equities === "SELL") {
  119|     lines.push(
  120|       "Slowing growth expectations can compress earnings outlooks and reduce risk appetite in equity markets.",
  121|     );
  122|   }
  123| 
  124|   if (liquidity < -0.5 && usd === "BUY") {
  125|     lines.push(
  126|       "Tighter global liquidity can strengthen demand for USD funding, supporting the US dollar.",
  127|     );
  128|   }
  129| 
  130|   if (commodity > 0.5 && commoditiesSig === "BUY") {
  131|     lines.push(
  132|       "Commodity supply pressure can lift spot prices and reinforce upside skew in commodities.",
  133|     );
  134|   }
  135| 
  136|   // Fallback if none of the rules fired.
  137|   if (lines.length === 0) {
  138|     const parts: string[] = [];
  139|     if (inflation !== 0) parts.push(`inflation exposure ${inflation.toFixed(2)}`);
  140|     if (liquidity !== 0) parts.push(`liquidity exposure ${liquidity.toFixed(2)}`);
  141|     if (growth !== 0) parts.push(`growth exposure ${growth.toFixed(2)}`);
  142| 
  143|     const signalParts: string[] = [];
  144|     for (const [asset, v] of Object.entries(signals)) {
  145|       signalParts.push(`${asset} ${v.signal}`);
  146|     }
  147| 
  148|     const exposureText = parts.length ? parts.join(", ") : "mixed macro exposures";
  149|     const signalText = signalParts.length ? signalParts.join(", ") : "neutral positioning";
  150| 
  151|     lines.push(
  152|       `This cluster reflects ${exposureText} and maps to portfolio signals: ${signalText}.`,
  153|     );
  154|   }
  155| 
  156|   // Join into a single paragraph.
  157|   return lines.join(" ");
  158| }
  159| 
  160| async function loadSignalsForCluster(clusterId: string): Promise<PortfolioSignalRow[]> {

  164|     .from("portfolio_signals")

  166|     .eq("cluster_id", clusterId);

  169|     throw new Error(`Failed to load portfolio signals: ${error.message}`);
  170|   }
  171| 
  172|   return (data as PortfolioSignalRow[] | null) ?? [];
  173| }

  190| export async function runInsightEngine(): Promise<void> {
  191|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  192| 
  193|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
  194|     .from("pipeline_events")
  195|     .select("id,payload")
  196|     .eq("event_type", "INSIGHT_REQUIRED")
  197|     .eq("processed", false)
  198|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
  199|     .limit(20);
  200| 
  201|   if (error) {
  202|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
  203|   }
  204| 
  205|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
  206|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
  207| 
  208|   const seen = new Set<string>();
  209|   const unique: PipelineEventRow[] = [];
  210|   for (const evt of pending) {
  211|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
  212|     if (!clusterId) {
  213|       unique.push(evt);
  214|       continue;
  215|     }
  216|     if (seen.has(clusterId)) continue;
  217|     seen.add(clusterId);
  218|     unique.push(evt);
  219|   }
  220| 
  221|   await workerPoolForEach(
  222|     unique,
  223|     async (evt) => {
  224|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
  225| 
  226|     await withStageSpan({
  227|       supabase,
  228|       stageName: "insight",
  229|       clusterId,
  230|       eventId: evt.id,
  231|       statusOnSuccess: clusterId ? "success" : "skipped",
  232|       fn: async () => {
  233|         if (!clusterId) {
  234|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
  235|             .from("pipeline_events")
  236|             .update({ processed: true })
  237|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  238| 
  239|           if (markError) {
  240|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  241|           }
  242| 
  243|           return;
  244|         }
  245| 
  246|         const { data: existingInsight, error: existingError } = await supabase
  247|           .from("event_insights")
  248|           .select("id")
  249|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  250|           .limit(1);
  251| 
  252|         if (existingError) {
  253|           throw new Error(`Failed to check existing insights: ${existingError.message}`);
  254|         }
  255| 
  256|         if ((existingInsight ?? []).length === 0) {
  257|           const signalsRows = await loadSignalsForCluster(clusterId);
  258|           if (signalsRows.length > 0) {
  259|             const exposuresRows = await loadExposuresForCluster(clusterId);
  260|             const exposures = toExposureMap(exposuresRows);
  261| 
  262|             const signals: Record<
  263|               string,
  264|               { signal: "BUY" | "SELL" | "NEUTRAL"; confidence: number }
  265|             > = {};
  266| 
  267|             for (const row of signalsRows) {
  268|               const asset = (row.asset ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase();
  269|               if (!asset) continue;
  270|               const signal = normalizeSignal(row.signal);
  271|               const confidence = Number(row.confidence);
  272|               signals[asset] = {
  273|                 signal,
  274|                 confidence: Number.isFinite(confidence) ? confidence : 0.6,
  275|               };
  276|             }
  277| 
  278|             const insight = buildInsightText(exposures, signals);
  279| 
  280|             const conf = clamp(
  281|               0.5,
  282|               avg(Object.values(signals).map((s) => s.confidence)),
  283|               0.95,
  284|             );
  285| 
  286|             const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("event_insights").insert({
  287|               cluster_id: clusterId,
  288|               insight,
  289|               confidence: conf,
  290|             });
  291| 
  292|             if (insertError) {
  293|               throw new Error(
  294|                 `Failed to insert event insight: ${insertError.message} (cluster_id=${clusterId})`,
  295|               );
  296|             }
  297|           }
  298|         }
  299| 
  300|         const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  301|           .from("pipeline_events")
  302|           .update({ processed: true })
  303|           .eq("id", evt.id);
  304| 
  305|         if (markEventError) {
  306|           throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`);
  307|         }
  308|       },
  309|     });
  310|     },
  311|     { concurrency: Number(process.env.PIPELINE_CONCURRENCY ?? 5) || 5 },
  312|   );
  313| }

===== FILE: services\insightTagEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    3| 
    4| type UntaggedInsightRow = {
    5|   id: string;
    6|   insight: string | null;
    7|   insight_tags?: Array<{ insight_id: string | null }> | null;
    8| };
    9| 
   10| function extractTags(insight: string): string[] {
   11|   const text = insight.toLowerCase();
   12|   const tags = new Set<string>();
   13| 
   14|   if (text.includes("inflation")) tags.add("inflation");
   15|   if (text.includes("bond")) tags.add("bonds");
   16|   if (text.includes("equity")) tags.add("equities");
   17|   if (text.includes("oil") || text.includes("energy")) tags.add("commodities");
   18|   if (text.includes("dollar") || text.includes("usd")) tags.add("currency");
   19|   if (text.includes("interest") || text.includes("rate")) tags.add("interest_rates");
   20| 
   21|   return Array.from(tags);
   22| }
   23| 
   24| export async function runInsightTagEngine(): Promise<void> {
   25|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   26| 
   27|   // Load insights that do not yet have tags.
   28|   // Supabase doesn't support NOT IN subqueries directly; use left join + null filter.
   29|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   30|     .from("event_insights")
   31|     .select("id,insight, insight_tags!left(insight_id)")
   32|     .is("insight_tags.insight_id", null)
   33|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   34|     .limit(20);
   35| 
   36|   if (error) {
   37|     throw new Error(`Failed to load untagged insights: ${error.message}`);
   38|   }
   39| 
   40|   const rows = (data as UntaggedInsightRow[] | null) ?? [];
   41|   if (rows.length === 0) return;
   42| 
   43|   for (const row of rows) {
   44|     const insightId = (row.id ?? "").toString().trim();
   45|     const insight = (row.insight ?? "").toString();
   46| 
   47|     if (!insightId || !insight) continue;
   48| 
   49|     await withStageSpan({
   50|       supabase,
   51|       stageName: "insight_tagging",
   52|       clusterId: null,
   53|       eventId: null,
   54|       fn: async () => {
   55|         const tags = extractTags(insight);
   56|         if (tags.length === 0) return;
   57| 
   58|         const inserts = tags.map((tag) => ({
   59|           insight_id: insightId,
   60|           tag,
   61|         }));
   62| 
   63|         const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("insight_tags").insert(inserts);
   64| 
   65|         if (insertError) {
   66|           throw new Error(`Failed to insert insight tags: ${insertError.message}`);
   67|         }
   68| 
   69|         const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
   70|           event_type: "INSIGHT_TAGGED",
   71|           payload: { insight_id: insightId },
   72|         });
   73| 
   74|         if (emitError) {
   75|           throw new Error(`Failed to emit INSIGHT_TAGGED event: ${emitError.message}`);
   76|         }
   77|       },
   78|       statusOnSuccess: "success",
   79|     });
   80|   }
   81| }

    1| import { createClient, type SupabaseClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";

    6| const BATCH_SIZE = 50;

    9| type MacroEventRow = {
   10|   title: string;
   11|   description: string;
   12|   source: string;
   13|   url: string;
   14|   published_at: string;
   15|   processed: boolean;
   16|   category: string;
   17|   geography?: string | null;
   18|   industries?: string[] | null;

   21| type EventSourceRow = {
   22|   id: string;
   23|   name: string;
   24|   rss_url: string;
   25|   category: string | null;
   26|   active: boolean;
   27|   last_checked?: string | null;
   28|   last_success?: string | null;

   32| function isDuplicateUrlConstraintError(message: string): boolean {
   33|   const m = message.toLowerCase();
   34|   return (
   35|     m.includes("duplicate key value") &&
   36|     (
   37|       m.includes("event_queue_url_key") ||
   38|       m.includes("macro_events_raw_url_key") ||
   39|       m.includes("unique constraint")
   40|     )
   41|   );
   42| }
   43| 
   44| async function getExistingUrls(
   45|   supabase: SupabaseClient,
   46|   urls: string[],
   47| ): Promise<Set<string>> {
   48|   const unique = Array.from(new Set(urls.filter(Boolean)));
   49|   if (unique.length === 0) return new Set();
   50| 
   51|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   52|     .from("event_queue")
   53|     .select("url")
   54|     .in("url", unique);
   55| 
   56|   if (error) {
   57|     // If this pre-check fails, fall back to relying on upsert behavior.
   58|     return new Set();
   59|   }
   60| 
   61|   const existing = new Set<string>();
   62|   for (const row of (data as Array<{ url: string }> | null) ?? []) {
   63|     if (row?.url) existing.add(row.url);
   64|   }
   65|   return existing;
   66| }
   67| 
   68| async function flushBatch(supabase: SupabaseClient) {
   69|   if (batchBuffer.length === 0) return;
   70| 
   71|   const { error } = await supabase.from("event_queue").upsert(batchBuffer, {
   72|     onConflict: "url",
   73|     ignoreDuplicates: true,
   74|   });
   75| 
   76|   if (error) {
   77|     throw new Error(`Supabase batch upsert failed: ${error.message}`);
   78|   }
   79| 
   80|   batchBuffer = [];
   81| }
   82| 
   83| function requireEnv(name: string): string {
   84|   const value = process.env[name];
   85|   if (!value) {
   86|     throw new Error(`Missing required env var: ${name}`);
   87|   }
   88|   return value;
   89| }

   91| export function createSupabaseServerClient(): SupabaseClient {
   92|   const url = requireEnv("NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL");
   93| 
   94|   // Prefer a server-only key for scripts; fall back to anon for local testing.
   95|   const key =
   96|     process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY ??
   97|     process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_KEY ??
   98|     process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY;
   99| 
  100|   if (!key) {
  101|     throw new Error(
  102|       "Missing Supabase key. Set SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY (recommended) or NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY.",
  103|     );
  104|   }
  105|   console.log("Using key type:",
  106|   process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY ? "service_role" : "anon");
  107| 
  108|   return createClient(url, key, {
  109|     auth: {
  110|       persistSession: false,
  111|       autoRefreshToken: false,
  112|       detectSessionInUrl: false,
  113|     },
  114|   });
  115| }
  116| 
  117| async function getActiveEventSources(
  118|   supabase: SupabaseClient,
  119| ): Promise<EventSourceRow[]> {
  120|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  121|     .from("event_sources")
  122|     .select("id,name,rss_url,category,active,last_checked,last_success,error_count")
  123|     .eq("active", true);
  124| 
  125|   if (error) {
  126|     throw new Error(`Failed to load event_sources: ${error.message}`);
  127|   }
  128| 
  129|   return (data as EventSourceRow[] | null) ?? [];
  130| }
  131| 
  132| function toEpochMs(value: unknown): number {
  133|   if (typeof value === "number" && Number.isFinite(value)) return value;
  134| 
  135|   if (typeof value === "string") {
  136|     const parsed = Date.parse(value);
  137|     if (Number.isFinite(parsed)) return parsed;
  138|   }
  139| 
  140|   if (value instanceof Date) {
  141|     const ms = value.getTime();
  142|     if (Number.isFinite(ms)) return ms;
  143|   }
  144| 
  145|   return Date.now();
  146| }
  147| 
  148| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
  149|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
  150| }
  151| 
  152| function withTimeout<T>(promise: Promise<T>, ms: number): Promise<T> {
  153|   let timeoutId: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | undefined;
  154| 
  155|   const timeoutPromise = new Promise<T>((_, reject) => {
  156|     timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
  157|       reject(new Error(`Feed fetch timed out after ${ms}ms`));
  158|     }, ms);
  159|   });
  160| 
  161|   return Promise.race([promise, timeoutPromise]).finally(() => {
  162|     if (timeoutId) clearTimeout(timeoutId);
  163|   });
  164| }
  165| 
  166| export type FetchAndStoreNewsResult = {
  167|   sourcesProcessed: number;
  168|   articlesInserted: number;
  169| };
  170| 
  171| /**
  172|  * Fetches configured RSS feeds (from `event_sources`) and upserts items into
  173|  * the `macro_events` table.
  174|  *
  175|  * Configuration:
  176|  * - NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL
  177|  * - SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY (recommended for scripts) OR NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY
  178|  */
  179| export async function fetchAndStoreNews(): Promise<FetchAndStoreNewsResult> {
  180|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  181|   const sources = await getActiveEventSources(supabase);
  182|   const parser = new Parser({
  183|     headers: {
  184|       "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 TrajectosBot",
  185|     },
  186|     timeout: 10000,
  187|     customFields: {
  188|       item: [
  189|         ["media:content", "mediaContent"],
  190|         ["media:thumbnail", "mediaThumbnail"],
  191|       ],
  192|     },
  193|   });
  194| 
  195|   let sourcesProcessed = 0;
  196|   let articlesInserted = 0;
  197| 
  198|   for (const src of sources) {
  199|     sourcesProcessed += 1;
  200|     console.log(`Fetching source: ${src.name}`);
  201| 
  202|     const checkedAt = new Date().toISOString();
  203|     try {
  204|       await supabase
  205|         .from("event_sources")
  206|         .update({ last_checked: checkedAt })
  207|         .eq("id", src.id);
  208|     } catch {
  209|       // Monitoring updates should never break ingestion.
  210|     }
  211| 
  212|     try {
  213|       await sleep(750);
  214|       const feed = await withTimeout(parser.parseURL(src.rss_url), 10000);
  215|       const sourceLabel =
  216|         src.name?.trim() || feed.title?.trim() || new URL(src.rss_url).host;
  217|       const category = (src.category ?? "unknown").toString();
  218| 
  219|       const rows: MacroEventRow[] = [];
  220|       const seenUrls = new Set<string>();
  221| 
  222|       const rawItems =
  223|         feed.items ?? (feed as any).entries ?? (feed as any).entry ?? [];
  224|       const items = Array.isArray(rawItems) ? rawItems : [];
  225| 
  226|       if (!items.length) {
  227|         console.warn("Feed returned no items", {
  228|           source: src.name,
  229|           url: src.rss_url,
  230|         });
  231|         continue;
  232|       }
  233| 
  234|       console.log("Feed structure:", Object.keys(feed));
  235|       console.log("Items found:", items.length);
  236|       console.log("First item:", items[0]);
  237| 
  238|       for (const item of items) {
  239|         const normalized = normalizeFeedItem(item, sourceLabel);
  240|         if (!normalized) continue;
  241| 
  242|         const url = normalized.url;
  243|         if (!url) continue;
  244|         if (seenUrls.has(url)) {
  245|           continue;
  246|         }
  247|         seenUrls.add(url);
  248| 
  249|         const fullContent = await extractArticleContent(url);
  250|         await sleep(500);
  251| 
  252|         const title = normalized.title;
  253|         const description = fullContent ?? normalized.description;
  254|         const link = normalized.url;
  255| 
  256|         const timestamp = toEpochMs(normalized.publishedAt);
  257| 
  258|         rows.push({
  259|           title,
  260|           description,
  261|           source: sourceLabel,
  262|           url,
  263|           published_at: new Date(timestamp).toISOString(),
  264|           processed: false,
  265|           category,
  266|           geography: null,
  267|           industries: null,
  268|         });
  269|       }
  270| 
  271|       if (rows.length === 0) {
  272|         continue;
  273|       }
  274| 
  275|       const existingUrls = await getExistingUrls(
  276|         supabase,
  277|         rows.map((r) => r.url),
  278|       );
  279|       const rowsToInsert = rows.filter((r) => !existingUrls.has(r.url));
  280| 
  281|       for (const row of rowsToInsert) {
  282|         batchBuffer.push(row);
  283| 
  284|         if (batchBuffer.length >= BATCH_SIZE) {
  285|           await flushBatch(supabase);
  286|         }
  287|       }
  288| 
  289|       articlesInserted += rowsToInsert.length;
  290| 
  291|       try {
  292|         await supabase
  293|           .from("event_sources")
  294|           .update({ last_success: new Date().toISOString() })
  295|           .eq("id", src.id);
  296|       } catch {
  297|         // Monitoring updates should never break ingestion.
  298|       }
  299|     } catch (err: unknown) {
  300|       const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
  301|       console.error("Feed error", {
  302|         source: src.name,
  303|         url: src.rss_url,
  304|         error: message,
  305|       });
  306| 
  307|       try {
  308|         const nextErrorCount = (src.error_count ?? 0) + 1;
  309|         await supabase
  310|           .from("event_sources")
  311|           .update({ error_count: nextErrorCount })
  312|           .eq("id", src.id);
  313|       } catch {
  314|         // Monitoring updates should never break ingestion.
  315|       }
  316|       continue;
  317|     }
  318|   }
  319| 
  320|   await flushBatch(supabase);
  321| 
  322|   return { sourcesProcessed, articlesInserted };
  323| }

===== FILE: services\pipelineEventUtils.ts =====

    1| import type { SupabaseClient } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
    2| 
    3| export async function emitClusterEventOnce(params: {
    4|   supabase: SupabaseClient;
    5|   eventType: string;
    6|   clusterId: string;
    7| }): Promise<void> {
    8|   const clusterId = (params.clusterId ?? "").toString().trim();
    9|   const eventType = (params.eventType ?? "").toString().trim();
   10|   if (!clusterId || !eventType) return;
   11| 
   12|   const { data: existing, error: existingError } = await params.supabase
   13|     .from("pipeline_events")
   14|     .select("id")
   15|     .eq("event_type", eventType)
   16|     .eq("processed", false)
   17|     .eq("payload->>cluster_id", clusterId)
   18|     .limit(1);
   19| 
   20|   if (existingError) {
   21|     // Best-effort: if we can't check, still attempt to insert.
   22|     const { error } = await params.supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
   23|       event_type: eventType,
   24|       payload: { cluster_id: clusterId },
   25|     });
   26| 
   27|     if (error) {
   28|       throw new Error(`Failed to emit ${eventType} event: ${error.message}`);
   29|     }
   30| 
   31|     return;
   32|   }
   33| 
   34|   if ((existing ?? []).length > 0) return;
   35| 
   36|   const { error } = await params.supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
   37|     event_type: eventType,
   38|     payload: { cluster_id: clusterId },
   39|   });
   40| 
   41|   if (error) {
   42|     throw new Error(`Failed to emit ${eventType} event: ${error.message}`);
   43|   }
   44| }

   25|   return new Date().toISOString();

   27| 
   28| function toErrorMessage(err: unknown): { message: string; stack: string | null } {
   29|   if (err instanceof Error) {
   30|     return {
   31|       message: err.message || "Error",
   32|       stack: typeof err.stack === "string" ? err.stack : null,
   33|     };
   34|   }
   35| 
   36|   if (typeof err === "string") {
   37|     return { message: err, stack: null };
   38|   }
   39| 
   40|   try {
   41|     return { message: JSON.stringify(err), stack: null };
   42|   } catch {
   43|     return { message: "Unknown error", stack: null };
   44|   }
   45| }
   46| 
   47| export async function recordStageRuntime(
   48|   supabase: SupabaseClient,
   49|   row: StageRuntimeInsert,
   50| ): Promise<void> {
   51|   const { error } = await supabase.from("pipeline_stage_runtime").insert(row);
   52|   if (error) {
   53|     // Observability must never block the pipeline.
   54|     return;
   55|   }
   56| }

   58| export async function recordFailure(
   59|   supabase: SupabaseClient,
   60|   row: FailureInsert,
   61| ): Promise<void> {
   62|   const { error } = await supabase.from("pipeline_failures").insert(row);
   63|   if (error) {
   64|     return;
   65|   }
