   68| export async function withStageSpan<T>(params: {
   69|   supabase: SupabaseClient;
   70|   stageName: string;
   71|   clusterId?: string | null;
   72|   eventId?: string | null;
   73|   fn: () => Promise<T>;
   74|   statusOnSuccess?: StageStatus;
   75| }): Promise<T> {
   76|   const startMs = Date.now();
   77|   const startIso = nowIso();
   78| 
   79|   try {
   80|     const result = await params.fn();
   81| 
   82|     const endIso = nowIso();
   83|     await recordStageRuntime(params.supabase, {
   84|       stage_name: params.stageName,
   85|       event_id: params.eventId ?? null,
   86|       cluster_id: params.clusterId ?? null,
   87|       start_time: startIso,
   88|       end_time: endIso,
   89|       duration_ms: Math.max(0, Date.now() - startMs),
   90|       status: params.statusOnSuccess ?? "success",
   91|     });
   92| 
   93|     return result;
   94|   } catch (err) {
   95|     const endIso = nowIso();
   96|     const info = toErrorMessage(err);
   97| 
   98|     await recordStageRuntime(params.supabase, {
   99|       stage_name: params.stageName,
  100|       event_id: params.eventId ?? null,
  101|       cluster_id: params.clusterId ?? null,
  102|       start_time: startIso,
  103|       end_time: endIso,
  104|       duration_ms: Math.max(0, Date.now() - startMs),
  105|       status: "failure",
  106|     });
  107| 
  108|     await recordFailure(params.supabase, {
  109|       stage_name: params.stageName,
  110|       event_id: params.eventId ?? null,
  111|       cluster_id: params.clusterId ?? null,
  112|       error_message: info.message,
  113|       error_stack: info.stack,
  114|       occurred_at: endIso,
  115|     });
  116| 
  117|     throw err;
  118|   }
  119| }

===== FILE: services\pipelineInvariantMonitor.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| 
    3| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
    4|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
    5| }
    6| 
    7| type CountResult = { ok: true; count: number } | { ok: false; error: string };
    8| 
    9| async function countExact(table: string, filters?: (q: any) => any): Promise<CountResult> {
   10|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   11| 
   12|   let query = supabase.from(table).select("id", { head: true, count: "exact" });
   13|   if (filters) query = filters(query);
   14| 
   15|   const { count, error } = await query;
   16| 
   17|   if (error) return { ok: false, error: error.message };
   18|   return { ok: true, count: count ?? 0 };
   19| }
   20| 
   21| async function tick(): Promise<void> {
   22|   // If any critical count fails, skip this tick to avoid false positives.
   23|   const events = await countExact("macro_events_raw");
   24|   const clusters = await countExact("event_clusters");
   25|   const canon = await countExact("canonical_events");
   26|   const validated = await countExact("event_clusters", (q) => q.eq("validated", true));
   27| 
   28|   const failed = [events, clusters, canon, validated].find((r) => !r.ok) as
   29|     | { ok: false; error: string }
   30|     | undefined;
   31| 
   32|   if (failed) {
   33|     console.warn(`[pipelineInvariantMonitor] count failed; skipping tick (${failed.error})`);
   34|     return;
   35|   }
   36| 
   37|   const eventCount = (events as { ok: true; count: number }).count;
   38|   const clusterCount = (clusters as { ok: true; count: number }).count;
   39|   const canonicalCount = (canon as { ok: true; count: number }).count;
   40|   const validatedClusterCount = (validated as { ok: true; count: number }).count;
   41| 
   42|   if (eventCount > 100 && clusterCount === 0) {
   43|     console.error(
   44|       "Pipeline invariant violated: events exist but clustering produced zero clusters.",
   45|     );
   46|   }
   47| 
   48|   if (clusterCount > 0 && canonicalCount === 0) {
   49|     console.warn("Pipeline stalled after clustering.");
   50|   }
   51| 
   52|   if (canonicalCount > 0 && validatedClusterCount === 0) {
   53|     console.warn("Pipeline stalled before validation.");
   54|   }
   55| }
   56| 
   57| /**
   58|  * Periodically checks simple pipeline invariants and logs warnings.
   59|  *
   60|  * This monitor is read-only and must never mutate pipeline state.
   61|  */
   62| export async function runPipelineInvariantMonitor(): Promise<void> {
   63|   console.log("[pipelineInvariantMonitor] starting");
   64| 
   65|   while (true) {
   66|     try {
   67|       await tick();
   68|     } catch (err) {
   69|       console.error("[pipelineInvariantMonitor] tick failed", err);
   70|     }
   71| 
   72|     await sleep(60_000);
   73|   }
   74| }

===== FILE: services\pipelineListener.ts =====

    1| import { Client, type Notification } from "pg";
    2| import { fileURLToPath } from "url";
    3| import path from "path";
    4| 
    5| import { handlePipelineEventById } from "./pipelineOrchestrator";
    6| 
    7| type ListenerOptions = {
    8|   connectionString: string;
    9|   channel?: string;
   10|   reconnectDelayMs?: number;
   11| };
   12| 
   13| type PipelineEventCreatedNotification = {
   14|   event_id?: string;
   15|   event_type?: string;
   16|   cluster_id?: string | null;
   17| };
   18| 
   19| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
   20|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   21| }
   22| 
   23| function parseNotificationPayload(
   24|   payload: string | null | undefined,
   25| ): PipelineEventCreatedNotification | null {
   26|   if (!payload) return null;
   27|   try {
   28|     const parsed = JSON.parse(payload) as unknown;
   29|     if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== "object") return null;
   30| 
   31|     const obj = parsed as Record<string, unknown>;
   32|     const eventId = obj.event_id;
   33|     const eventType = obj.event_type;
   34|     const clusterId = obj.cluster_id;
   35| 
   36|     return {
   37|       event_id: typeof eventId === "string" ? eventId : undefined,
   38|       event_type: typeof eventType === "string" ? eventType : undefined,
   39|       cluster_id:
   40|         typeof clusterId === "string" ? clusterId : clusterId === null ? null : undefined,
   41|     };
   42|   } catch {
   43|     return null;
   44|   }
   45| }
   46| 
   47| async function connectAndListen(options: ListenerOptions): Promise<never> {
   48|   const channel = options.channel ?? "pipeline_event_created";
   49| 
   50|   // Dedicated connection for LISTEN/NOTIFY.
   51|   const client = new Client({
   52|     connectionString: options.connectionString,
   53|     application_name: "trajectos_pipeline_listener",
   54|     keepAlive: true,
   55|   });
   56| 
   57|   client.on("error", (err) => {
   58|     // The outer loop will reconnect.
   59|     console.error("[pipelineListener] pg client error", err);
   60|   });
   61| 
   62|   await client.connect();
   63|   await client.query(`listen ${channel}`);
   64| 
   65|   console.log(`[pipelineListener] LISTEN ${channel} (connected)`);
   66| 
   67|   client.on("notification", async (msg: Notification) => {
   68|     if (msg.channel !== channel) return;
   69| 
   70|     const parsed = parseNotificationPayload(msg.payload);
   71|     if (!parsed?.event_id) return;
   72| 
   73|     try {
   74|       await handlePipelineEventById(parsed.event_id);
   75|     } catch (err) {
   76|       console.error("[pipelineListener] failed handling event", parsed, err);
   77|     }
   78|   });
   79| 
   80|   // Keep the promise pending forever. If the connection drops, 'error' triggers and
   81|   // pg will eventually cause queries to reject; we also keep a heartbeat loop.
   82|   while (true) {
   83|     try {
   84|       await client.query("select 1");
   85|     } catch {
   86|       try {
   87|         await client.end();
   88|       } catch {
   89|         // ignore
   90|       }
   91|       throw new Error("LISTEN connection lost");
   92|     }
   93| 
   94|     await sleep(30_000);
   95|   }
   96| }
   97| 
   98| /**
   99|  * Starts a real-time pipeline listener using PostgreSQL LISTEN/NOTIFY.
  100|  *
  101|  * Required env:
  102|  * - DATABASE_URL (direct Postgres connection string)
  103|  */
  104| export async function runPipelineListener(): Promise<void> {
  105|   const connectionString = process.env.DATABASE_URL;
  106|   if (!connectionString) {
  107|     throw new Error("Missing DATABASE_URL env var for Postgres LISTEN/NOTIFY");
  108|   }
  109| 
  110|   const reconnectDelayMs = 2_000;
  111| 
  112|   console.log("[pipelineListener] starting");
  113| 
  114|   while (true) {
  115|     try {
  116|       await connectAndListen({
  117|         connectionString,
  118|         reconnectDelayMs,
  119|       });
  120|     } catch (err) {
  121|       console.error("[pipelineListener] reconnecting after error", err);
  122|       await sleep(reconnectDelayMs);
  123|     }
  124|   }
  125| }
  126| 
  127| function isMainModule(): boolean {
  128|   try {
  129|     const current = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
  130|     const invoked = process.argv[1] ?? "";
  131|     const invokedAbs = path.resolve(process.cwd(), invoked);
  132|     return path.normalize(invokedAbs).toLowerCase() === path.normalize(current).toLowerCase();
  133|   } catch {
  134|     return false;
  135|   }
  136| }
  137| 
  138| // If executed directly via tsx/node.
  139| if (isMainModule()) {
  140|   runPipelineListener().catch((err) => {
  141|     console.error(err);
  142|     process.exit(1);
  143|   });
  144| }

===== FILE: services\pipelineMonitor.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { fileURLToPath } from "url";
    3| import path from "path";
    4| 
    5| type StageAggregate = {
    6|   stage: string;
    7|   processed: number;
    8|   failed: number;
    9|   skipped: number;
   10|   avgDurationMs: number;
   11| };
   12| 
   13| type RuntimeRow = {
   14|   stage_name: string | null;
   15|   duration_ms: number | null;
   16|   status: string | null;
   17| };
   18| 
   19| type FailureRow = {
   20|   stage_name: string | null;
   21| };
   22| 
   23| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
   24|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   25| }
   26| 
   27| function minuteBucketIso(date: Date): string {
   28|   const ms = date.getTime();
   29|   const bucketMs = Math.floor(ms / 60_000) * 60_000;
   30|   return new Date(bucketMs).toISOString();
   31| }
   32| 
   33| async function fetchRuntimeRows(sinceIso: string): Promise<RuntimeRow[]> {
   34|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   35|   const pageSize = 1000;
   36|   const maxRows = 5000;
   37| 
   38|   const out: RuntimeRow[] = [];
   39|   for (let offset = 0; offset < maxRows; offset += pageSize) {
   40|     const { data, error } = await supabase
   41|       .from("pipeline_stage_runtime")
   42|       .select("stage_name,duration_ms,status")
   43|       .gte("end_time", sinceIso)
   44|       .order("end_time", { ascending: true })
   45|       .range(offset, offset + pageSize - 1);
   46| 
   47|     if (error) throw new Error(`Failed to query pipeline_stage_runtime: ${error.message}`);
   48| 
   49|     const rows = (data as RuntimeRow[] | null) ?? [];
   50|     out.push(...rows);
   51|     if (rows.length < pageSize) break;
   52|   }
   53| 
   54|   return out;
   55| }
   56| 
   57| async function fetchFailureRows(sinceIso: string): Promise<FailureRow[]> {
   58|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   59|   const pageSize = 1000;
   60|   const maxRows = 5000;
   61| 
   62|   const out: FailureRow[] = [];
   63|   for (let offset = 0; offset < maxRows; offset += pageSize) {
   64|     const { data, error } = await supabase
   65|       .from("pipeline_failures")
   66|       .select("stage_name")
   67|       .gte("occurred_at", sinceIso)
   68|       .order("occurred_at", { ascending: true })
   69|       .range(offset, offset + pageSize - 1);
   70| 
   71|     if (error) throw new Error(`Failed to query pipeline_failures: ${error.message}`);
   72| 
   73|     const rows = (data as FailureRow[] | null) ?? [];
   74|     out.push(...rows);
   75|     if (rows.length < pageSize) break;
   76|   }
   77| 
   78|   return out;
   79| }
   80| 
   81| async function getBacklogSize(): Promise<number> {
   82|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   83|   const { count, error } = await supabase
   84|     .from("pipeline_events")
   85|     .select("id", { head: true, count: "exact" })
   86|     .eq("processed", false);
   87| 
   88|   if (error) {
   89|     // Observability should be best-effort.
   90|     return 0;
   91|   }
   92| 
   93|   return count ?? 0;
   94| }
   95| 
   96| function aggregateStages(runtimeRows: RuntimeRow[], failureRows: FailureRow[]): StageAggregate[] {
   97|   const byStage = new Map<
   98|     string,
   99|     { processed: number; failed: number; skipped: number; durationSum: number; durationCount: number; failureCount: number }
  100|   >();
  101| 
  102|   for (const row of runtimeRows) {
  103|     const stage = (row.stage_name ?? "").toString().trim() || "unknown";
  104|     const status = (row.status ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase();
  105|     const duration = Number(row.duration_ms);
  106| 
  107|     const entry =
  108|       byStage.get(stage) ??
  109|       {
  110|         processed: 0,
  111|         failed: 0,
  112|         skipped: 0,
  113|         durationSum: 0,
  114|         durationCount: 0,
  115|         failureCount: 0,
  116|       };
  117| 
  118|     if (status === "failure") entry.failed += 1;
  119|     else if (status === "skipped") entry.skipped += 1;
  120|     else entry.processed += 1;
  121| 
  122|     if (Number.isFinite(duration) && duration >= 0) {
  123|       entry.durationSum += duration;
  124|       entry.durationCount += 1;
  125|     }
  126| 
  127|     byStage.set(stage, entry);
  128|   }
  129| 
  130|   for (const row of failureRows) {
  131|     const stage = (row.stage_name ?? "").toString().trim() || "unknown";
  132|     const entry =
  133|       byStage.get(stage) ??
  134|       {
  135|         processed: 0,
  136|         failed: 0,
  137|         skipped: 0,
  138|         durationSum: 0,
  139|         durationCount: 0,
  140|         failureCount: 0,
  141|       };
  142| 
  143|     entry.failureCount += 1;
  144|     byStage.set(stage, entry);
  145|   }
  146| 
  147|   const aggregates: StageAggregate[] = [];
  148|   for (const [stage, v] of byStage.entries()) {
  149|     aggregates.push({
  150|       stage,
  151|       processed: v.processed,
  152|       failed: v.failed,
  153|       skipped: v.skipped,
  154|       avgDurationMs: v.durationCount ? v.durationSum / v.durationCount : 0,
  155|     });
  156|   }
  157| 
  158|   aggregates.sort((a, b) => {
  159|     const aTotal = a.processed + a.failed + a.skipped;
  160|     const bTotal = b.processed + b.failed + b.skipped;
  161|     return bTotal - aTotal;
  162|   });
  163| 
  164|   return aggregates;
  165| }
  166| 
  167| async function writeMetricsSnapshot(windowStartIso: string, backlogSize: number, stages: StageAggregate[]): Promise<void> {
  168|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  169| 
  170|   const rows = stages.length
  171|     ? stages.map((s) => ({
  172|         window_start: windowStartIso,
  173|         stage_name: s.stage,
  174|         processed_count: s.processed,
  175|         avg_duration_ms: Number.isFinite(s.avgDurationMs) ? s.avgDurationMs : null,
  176|         failure_count: s.failed,
  177|         backlog_size: backlogSize,
  178|       }))
  179|     : [
  180|         {
  181|           window_start: windowStartIso,
  182|           stage_name: "pipeline_overall",
  183|           processed_count: 0,
  184|           avg_duration_ms: null,
  185|           failure_count: 0,
  186|           backlog_size: backlogSize,
  187|         },
  188|       ];
  189| 
  190|   const { error } = await supabase.from("pipeline_metrics").upsert(rows, {
  191|     onConflict: "window_start,stage_name",
  192|   });
  193| 
  194|   if (error) {
  195|     return;
  196|   }
  197| }
  198| 
  199| function printHealthSummary(windowStartIso: string, backlogSize: number, stages: StageAggregate[]): void {
  200|   const totalProcessed = stages.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.processed, 0);
  201|   const totalFailed = stages.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.failed, 0);
  202|   const totalSkipped = stages.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.skipped, 0);
  203| 
  204|   console.log(
  205|     `[pipelineMonitor] ${windowStartIso} backlog=${backlogSize} processed=${totalProcessed} failed=${totalFailed} skipped=${totalSkipped}`,
  206|   );
  207| 
  208|   for (const s of stages.slice(0, 10)) {
  209|     console.log(
  210|       `  - ${s.stage}: processed=${s.processed} failed=${s.failed} skipped=${s.skipped} avg_ms=${Math.round(s.avgDurationMs)}`,
  211|     );
  212|   }
  213| }
  214| 
  215| async function tick(): Promise<void> {
  216|   const now = new Date();
  217|   const windowStartIso = minuteBucketIso(now);
  218|   const sinceIso = new Date(now.getTime() - 60_000).toISOString();
  219| 
  220|   const backlogSize = await getBacklogSize();
  221| 
  222|   const runtimeRows = await fetchRuntimeRows(sinceIso);
  223|   const failureRows = await fetchFailureRows(sinceIso);
  224| 
  225|   const stages = aggregateStages(runtimeRows, failureRows);
  226| 
  227|   await writeMetricsSnapshot(windowStartIso, backlogSize, stages);
  228|   printHealthSummary(windowStartIso, backlogSize, stages);
  229| }
  230| 
  231| /**
  232|  * Aggregates pipeline observability tables and prints a health summary every minute.
  233|  *
  234|  * This is additive: it does not affect pipeline execution.
  235|  */
  236| export async function runPipelineMonitor(): Promise<void> {
  237|   console.log("[pipelineMonitor] starting");
  238| 
  239|   while (true) {
  240|     try {
  241|       await tick();
  242|     } catch (err) {
  243|       console.error("[pipelineMonitor] tick failed", err);
  244|     }
  245| 
  246|     await sleep(60_000);
  247|   }
  248| }
  249| 
  250| function isMainModule(): boolean {
  251|   try {
  252|     const current = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
  253|     const invoked = process.argv[1] ?? "";
  254|     const invokedAbs = path.resolve(process.cwd(), invoked);
  255|     return path.normalize(invokedAbs).toLowerCase() === path.normalize(current).toLowerCase();
  256|   } catch {
  257|     return false;
  258|   }
  259| }
  260| 
  261| // If executed directly via tsx/node.
  262| if (isMainModule()) {
  263|   runPipelineMonitor().catch((err) => {
  264|     console.error(err);
  265|     process.exit(1);
  266|   });
  267| }

   15|

   23| function toErrorMessage(err: unknown): string {

   25|   if (typeof err === "string") return err;

   32| 
   33| async function deadLetterEvent(evt: PipelineEventRow, err: unknown): Promise<void> {
   34|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   35| 
   36|   // Best-effort: dead-letter should not crash the orchestrator.
   37|   const { error: dlqError } = await supabase
   38|     .from("pipeline_dead_letters")
   39|     .upsert(
   40|       {
   41|         id: evt.id,
   42|         event_type: evt.event_type,
   43|         payload: evt.payload,
   44|         error_message: toErrorMessage(err),
   45|       },
   46|       { onConflict: "id" },
   47|     );
   48| 
   49|   if (dlqError) {
   50|     console.error("[pipelineOrchestrator] failed to dead-letter event", {
   51|       eventId: evt.id,
   52|       eventType: evt.event_type,
   53|       error: dlqError.message,
   54|     });
   55|   }
   56| 
   57|   // Mark as processed so the pipeline won't get stuck on a poisoned event.
   58|   const { error: markError } = await supabase
   59|     .from("pipeline_events")
   60|     .update({ processed: true })
   61|     .eq("id", evt.id)
   62|     .eq("processed", false);
   63| 
   64|   if (markError) {
   65|     // If we can't mark processed, the event will keep retrying and continue to block.
   66|     throw new Error(`Failed to mark dead-lettered event processed: ${markError.message}`);
   67|   }
   68| }
   69| 
   70| function extractClusterIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   71|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   72|   const clusterId = (payload as { cluster_id?: unknown }).cluster_id;
   73|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   74|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   75|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   76| }
   77| 
   78| async function markEventProcessed(id: string): Promise<void> {
   79|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   80|   const { error } = await supabase
   81|     .from("pipeline_events")
   82|     .update({ processed: true })
   83|     .eq("id", id)
   84|     .eq("processed", false);
   85| 
   86|   if (error) {
   87|     throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${error.message}`);
   88|   }
   89| }
   90| 
   91| function extractClusterIdFromJsonObject(payload: JsonObject): string | null {
   92|   const clusterId = payload.cluster_id;
   93|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   94|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   95|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   96| }
   97| 
   98| async function ensureEvent(eventType: string, payload: JsonObject): Promise<void> {
   99|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  100| 
  101|   const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromJsonObject(payload);
  102| 
  103|   const existingQuery = supabase
  104|     .from("pipeline_events")
  105|     .select("id")
  106|     .eq("event_type", eventType)
  107|     .eq("processed", false)
  108|     .limit(1);
  109| 
  110|   const { data: existing, error: existingError } = clusterId
  111|     ? await existingQuery.eq("payload->>cluster_id", clusterId)
  112|     : await existingQuery;
  113| 
  114|   if (existingError) {
  115|     throw new Error(`Failed to check existing ${eventType} events: ${existingError.message}`);
  116|   }
  117| 
  118|   if ((existing ?? []).length > 0) return;
  119| 
  120|   const { error } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  121|     event_type: eventType,
  122|     payload,
  123|   });
  124| 
  125|   if (error) {
  126|     throw new Error(`Failed to emit ${eventType} event: ${error.message}`);
  127|   }
  128| }
  129| 
  130| async function hasEvent(eventType: string, payload: JsonObject): Promise<boolean> {
  131|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  132| 
  133|   const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromJsonObject(payload);
  134| 
  135|   const query = supabase.from("pipeline_events").select("id").eq("event_type", eventType).limit(1);
  136|   const { data, error } = clusterId
  137|     ? await query.eq("payload->>cluster_id", clusterId)
  138|     : await query;
  139| 
  140|   if (error) return false;
  141|   return (data ?? []).length > 0;
  142| }
  143| 
  144| async function isClusterValidated(clusterId: string): Promise<boolean> {
  145|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  146|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  147|     .from("event_clusters")
  148|     .select("validated")
  149|     .eq("id", clusterId)
  150|     .maybeSingle();
  151| 
  152|   if (error) {
  153|     throw new Error(`Failed to load cluster validated flag: ${error.message}`);
  154|   }
  155| 
  156|   return Boolean((data as { validated?: boolean } | null)?.validated);
  157| }
  158| 
  159| async function isClusterProcessed(clusterId: string): Promise<boolean> {
  160|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  161|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  162|     .from("event_clusters")
  163|     .select("processed")
  164|     .eq("id", clusterId)
  165|     .maybeSingle();
  166| 
  167|   if (error) {
  168|     throw new Error(`Failed to load cluster processed flag: ${error.message}`);
  169|   }
  170| 
  171|   return Boolean((data as { processed?: boolean } | null)?.processed);
  172| }
  173| 
  174| async function hasAllocations(clusterId: string): Promise<boolean> {
  175|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  176|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  177|     .from("portfolio_allocations")
  178|     .select("id")
  179|     .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  180|     .limit(1);
  181| 
  182|   if (error) return false;
  183|   return (data ?? []).length > 0;
  184| }
  185| 
  186| async function handleEvent(evt: PipelineEventRow): Promise<void> {
  187|   const type = (evt.event_type ?? "").toString().trim();
  188|   const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
  189| 
  190|   // Dependency graph (requested):
  191|   // CLUSTER_CREATED -> VALIDATION_REQUIRED
  192|   // VALIDATION_COMPLETED -> FACTOR_REQUIRED
  193|   // FACTOR_CREATED -> IMPACT_REQUIRED
  194|   // IMPACT_CREATED -> SIGNAL_REQUIRED
  195|   // SIGNAL_CREATED -> INSIGHT_REQUIRED
  196|   // INSIGHT_CREATED -> ALLOCATION_REQUIRED
  197|   switch (type) {
  198|     case "CLUSTER_CREATED": {
  199|       if (!clusterId) {
  200|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  201|         return;
  202|       }
  203| 
  204|       // Create the dependency edge event (orchestrator-owned) and proactively run validation.
  205|       await ensureEvent("VALIDATION_REQUIRED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  206|       await runEventValidationEngine();
  207| 
  208|       if (await isClusterValidated(clusterId)) {
  209|         await ensureEvent("VALIDATION_COMPLETED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  210|       }
  211| 
  212|       return;
  213|     }
  214| 
  215|     case "VALIDATION_REQUIRED": {
  216|       if (!clusterId) {
  217|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  218|         return;
  219|       }
  220| 
  221|       await runEventValidationEngine();
  222| 
  223|       if (await isClusterValidated(clusterId)) {
  224|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  225|         await ensureEvent("VALIDATION_COMPLETED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  226|       }
  227| 
  228|       return;
  229|     }
  230| 
  231|     case "VALIDATION_COMPLETED": {
  232|       if (!clusterId) {
  233|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  234|         return;
  235|       }
  236| 
  237|       await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  238|       await ensureEvent("FACTOR_REQUIRED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  239| 
  240|       // Kick the next engine; it consumes CLUSTER_CREATED events and gates on validation.
  241|       await runFactorEngine();
  242| 
  243|       return;
  244|     }
  245| 
  246|     case "FACTOR_REQUIRED": {
  247|       if (!clusterId) {
  248|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  249|         return;
  250|       }
  251| 
  252|       await runFactorEngine();
  253| 
  254|       if (await isClusterProcessed(clusterId)) {
  255|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  256|       }
  257| 
  258|       return;
  259|     }
  260| 
  261|     case "FACTOR_CREATED": {
  262|       if (!clusterId) {
  263|         // Safe to mark malformed events; impact engine will ignore them anyway.
  264|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  265|         return;
  266|       }
  267| 
  268|       // Do NOT mark FACTOR_CREATED processed here; impact engine consumes it.
  269|       await ensureEvent("IMPACT_REQUIRED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  270|       return;
  271|     }
  272| 
  273|     case "IMPACT_REQUIRED": {
  274|       if (!clusterId) {
  275|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  276|         return;
  277|       }
  278| 
  279|       await runImpactEngine();
  280| 
  281|       // If impact produced downstream work, emit IMPACT_CREATED to advance DAG.
  282|       const producedSignal = await hasEvent("SIGNAL_CREATED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  283|       if (producedSignal) {
  284|         await ensureEvent("IMPACT_CREATED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  285|       }
  286| 
  287|       // Mark required event processed once the upstream FACTOR_CREATED is likely handled.
  288|       // (Impact engine marks FACTOR_CREATED events processed, even when it no-ops.)
  289|       await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  290|       return;
  291|     }
  292| 
  293|     case "IMPACT_CREATED": {
  294|       if (!clusterId) {
  295|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  296|         return;
  297|       }
  298| 
  299|       await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  300|       await ensureEvent("SIGNAL_REQUIRED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  301| 
  302|       // Kick the next engine; it consumes SIGNAL_CREATED events.
  303|       await runPortfolioSignalEngine();
  304| 
  305|       return;
  306|     }
  307| 
  308|     case "SIGNAL_REQUIRED": {
  309|       if (!clusterId) {
  310|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  311|         return;
  312|       }
  313| 
  314|       await runPortfolioSignalEngine();
  315| 
  316|       // Portfolio signal engine emits INSIGHT_REQUIRED when it processes SIGNAL_CREATED.
  317|       const producedInsightRequired = await hasEvent("INSIGHT_REQUIRED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  318|       if (producedInsightRequired) {
  319|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  320|       }
  321| 
  322|       // Kick insight engine opportunistically.
  323|       await runInsightEngine();
  324| 
  325|       return;
  326|     }
  327| 
  328|     case "INSIGHT_REQUIRED": {
  329|       await runInsightEngine();
  330|       return;
  331|     }
  332| 
  333|     case "SIGNAL_CREATED": {
  334|       // This event is consumed by portfolioSignalEngine.
  335|       await runPortfolioSignalEngine();
  336|       return;
  337|     }
  338| 
  339|     case "INSIGHT_CREATED": {
  340|       if (!clusterId) {
  341|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  342|         return;
  343|       }
  344| 
  345|       // Do NOT mark INSIGHT_CREATED processed here; allocation engine consumes it.
  346|       await ensureEvent("ALLOCATION_REQUIRED", { cluster_id: clusterId });
  347|       return;
  348|     }
  349| 
  350|     case "ALLOCATION_REQUIRED": {
  351|       if (!clusterId) {
  352|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  353|         return;
  354|       }
  355| 
  356|       await runAllocationEngine();
  357| 
  358|       if (await hasAllocations(clusterId)) {
  359|         await markEventProcessed(evt.id);
  360|       }
  361| 
  362|       return;
  363|     }
  364| 
  365|     default:
  366|       return;
  367|   }
  368| }
  369| 
  370| export async function runPipelineOrchestrator(options?: OrchestratorOptions): Promise<void> {
  371|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  372| 
  373|   const batchSize = options?.batchSize ?? 50;
  374|   const maxPasses = options?.maxPasses ?? 30;
  375| 
  376|   for (let pass = 0; pass < maxPasses; pass += 1) {
  377|     const { data: events, error } = await supabase
  378|       .from("pipeline_events")
  379|       .select("id,event_type,payload,created_at")
  380|       .eq("processed", false)
  381|       .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
  382|       .limit(batchSize);
  383| 
  384|     if (error) {
  385|       throw new Error(`Failed to poll pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
  386|     }
  387| 
  388|     const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
  389|     if (pending.length === 0) return;
  390| 
  391|     for (const evt of pending) {
  392|       try {
  393|         await handleEvent(evt);
  394|       } catch (err) {
  395|         console.error("[pipelineOrchestrator] unrecoverable event failure; dead-lettering", {
  396|           eventId: evt.id,
  397|           eventType: evt.event_type,
  398|           message: toErrorMessage(err),
  399|         });
  400|         await deadLetterEvent(evt, err);
  401|       }
  402|     }
  403|   }
  404| }
  405| 
  406| /**
  407|  * Event-driven entrypoint (used by the LISTEN/NOTIFY listener).
  408|  * Fetches a specific pipeline event by id and runs the orchestrator logic for it.
  409|  */
  410| export async function handlePipelineEventById(eventId: string): Promise<void> {
  411|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  412| 
  413|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  414|     .from("pipeline_events")
  415|     .select("id,event_type,payload,created_at,processed")
  416|     .eq("id", eventId)
  417|     .maybeSingle();
  418| 
  419|   if (error) {
  420|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline event ${eventId}: ${error.message}`);
  421|   }
  422| 
  423|   if (!data) return;
  424|   const processed = Boolean((data as { processed?: boolean } | null)?.processed);
  425|   if (processed) return;
  426| 
  427|   const row: PipelineEventRow = {
  428|     id: (data as { id: string }).id,
  429|     event_type: (data as { event_type: string }).event_type,
  430|     payload: (data as { payload: unknown }).payload,
  431|     created_at: (data as { created_at?: string }).created_at,
  432|   };
  433| 
  434|   try {
  435|     await handleEvent(row);
  436|   } catch (err) {
  437|     console.error("[pipelineOrchestrator] unrecoverable event failure; dead-lettering", {
  438|       eventId: row.id,
  439|       eventType: row.event_type,
  440|       message: toErrorMessage(err),
  441|     });
  442|     await deadLetterEvent(row, err);
  443|   }
  444| }

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";
    3| 
    4| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
    5|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
    6| }
    7| 
    8| function minutesAgoIso(minutes: number): string {
    9|   return new Date(Date.now() - minutes * 60_000).toISOString();
   10| }
   11| 
   12| type ClusterRow = {
   13|   id: string;
   14|   created_at?: string | null;
   15| };
   16| 
   17| async function getPipelineBacklogSize(): Promise<number> {
   18|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   19|   const { count, error } = await supabase
   20|     .from("pipeline_events")
   21|     .select("id", { head: true, count: "exact" })
   22|     .eq("processed", false);
   23| 
   24|   if (error) return 0;
   25|   return count ?? 0;
   26| }
   27| 
   28| async function listStuckUnvalidatedClusters(cutoffIso: string, limit = 100): Promise<string[]> {
   29|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   30|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   31|     .from("event_clusters")
   32|     .select("id")
   33|     .eq("validated", false)
   34|     .lt("created_at", cutoffIso)
   35|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   36|     .limit(limit);
   37| 
   38|   if (error) return [];
   39|   const rows = (data as ClusterRow[] | null) ?? [];
   40|   return rows.map((r) => (r.id ?? "").toString().trim()).filter(Boolean);
   41| }
   42| 
   43| async function listValidatedClustersMissingFactors(cutoffIso: string, limit = 100): Promise<string[]> {
   44|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   45| 
   46|   // Validated clusters that still have no factor exposures.
   47|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   48|     .from("event_clusters")
   49|     .select("id,event_factor_exposures!left(id)")
   50|     .eq("validated", true)
   51|     .lt("created_at", cutoffIso)
   52|     .is("event_factor_exposures.id", null)
   53|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   54|     .limit(limit);
   55| 
   56|   if (error) return [];
   57|   const rows = (data as Array<ClusterRow & { event_factor_exposures?: unknown }> | null) ?? [];
   58|   return rows.map((r) => (r.id ?? "").toString().trim()).filter(Boolean);
   59| }
   60| 
   61| async function listValidatedClustersMissingImpacts(cutoffIso: string, limit = 100): Promise<string[]> {
   62|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   63| 
   64|   // Validated clusters that still have no impact scores.
   65|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   66|     .from("event_clusters")
   67|     .select("id,event_impact_scores!left(id)")
   68|     .eq("validated", true)
   69|     .lt("created_at", cutoffIso)
   70|     .is("event_impact_scores.id", null)
   71|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
   72|     .limit(limit);
   73| 
   74|   if (error) return [];
   75|   const rows = (data as Array<ClusterRow & { event_impact_scores?: unknown }> | null) ?? [];
   76|   return rows.map((r) => (r.id ?? "").toString().trim()).filter(Boolean);
   77| }
   78| 
   79| async function tick(): Promise<void> {
   80|   const backlog = await getPipelineBacklogSize();
   81| 
   82|   const cutoffIso = minutesAgoIso(10);
   83|   const stuckUnvalidated = await listStuckUnvalidatedClusters(cutoffIso, 200);
   84| 
   85|   // "Stuck after factor/impact" is interpreted as: validated clusters that have not produced
   86|   // factor exposures and/or impact scores after enough time has passed.
   87|   const missingFactors = await listValidatedClustersMissingFactors(cutoffIso, 200);
   88|   const missingImpacts = await listValidatedClustersMissingImpacts(cutoffIso, 200);
   89| 
   90|   const hasBacklogWarning = backlog > 1000;
   91|   const hasStuckWarning =
   92|     stuckUnvalidated.length > 0 || missingFactors.length > 0 || missingImpacts.length > 0;
   93| 
   94|   if (hasBacklogWarning || hasStuckWarning) {
   95|     console.warn(
   96|       `[pipelineWatchdog] WARNING: backlog=${backlog} stuck_unvalidated=${stuckUnvalidated.length} missing_factors=${missingFactors.length} missing_impacts=${missingImpacts.length}`,
   97|     );
   98|   } else {
   99|     console.log(`[pipelineWatchdog] ok backlog=${backlog}`);
  100|   }
  101| 
  102|   // Recovery strategy:
  103|   // - Unvalidated > 10m: re-emit CLUSTER_CREATED (kicks validation/orchestration)
  104|   // - Validated but missing factor/impact: re-emit CLUSTER_VALIDATED
  105|   // This service must not mutate other tables.
  106|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  107| 
  108|   for (const clusterId of stuckUnvalidated.slice(0, 100)) {
  109|     await emitClusterEventOnce({
  110|       supabase,
  111|       eventType: "CLUSTER_CREATED",
  112|       clusterId,
  113|     });
  114|   }
  115| 
  116|   const validatedRecoveryTargets = new Set<string>([...missingFactors, ...missingImpacts]);
  117|   for (const clusterId of Array.from(validatedRecoveryTargets).slice(0, 100)) {
  118|     await emitClusterEventOnce({
  119|       supabase,
  120|       eventType: "CLUSTER_VALIDATED",
  121|       clusterId,
  122|     });
  123|   }
  124| }
  125| 
  126| /**
  127|  * Watches pipeline health and attempts self-healing by re-emitting pipeline events.
  128|  *
  129|  * - Runs every 60 seconds
  130|  * - Never modifies data directly other than emitting recovery events to pipeline_events
  131|  */
  132| export async function runPipelineWatchdog(): Promise<void> {
  133|   console.log("[pipelineWatchdog] starting");
  134| 
  135|   while (true) {
  136|     try {
  137|       await tick();
  138|     } catch (err) {
  139|       console.error("[pipelineWatchdog] tick failed", err);
  140|     }
  141| 
  142|     await sleep(60_000);
  143|   }
  144| }
  145| 
  146| // Exposed for tests/scripts.
  147| export async function runPipelineWatchdogOnce(): Promise<void> {
  148|   await tick();
  149| }

===== FILE: services\portfolioSignalEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| import { factorSignalMap } from "@/lib/factorSignalMap";
    3| import { withStageSpan } from "./pipelineInstrumentation";
    4| import { workerPoolForEach } from "./workerPool";
    5| import { emitClusterEventOnce } from "./pipelineEventUtils";

    7| type PipelineEventRow = {
    8|   id: string;
    9|   payload: unknown;
   10| };
   11| 
   12| function extractClusterIdFromPayload(payload: unknown): string | null {
   13|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") return null;
   14|   const clusterId = (payload as { cluster_id?: unknown }).cluster_id;
   15|   if (typeof clusterId !== "string" && typeof clusterId !== "number") return null;
   16|   const trimmed = clusterId.toString().trim();
   17|   return trimmed ? trimmed : null;
   18| }
   19| 
   20| type FactorExposureRow = {
   21|   cluster_id: string | null;
   22|   factor: string | null;
   23|   exposure: number | null;
   24| };
   25| 
   26| type PortfolioSignalRow = {
   27|   cluster_id: string;
   28|   asset: string;
   29|   signal: "BUY" | "SELL" | "NEUTRAL";
   30|   confidence: number;
   31| };
   32| 
   33| function clamp(min: number, value: number, max: number): number {
   34|   return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
   35| }
   36| 
   37| function scoreToSignal(score: number): "BUY" | "SELL" | "NEUTRAL" {
   38|   if (score > 0.5) return "BUY";
   39|   if (score < -0.5) return "SELL";
   40|   return "NEUTRAL";
   41| }
   42| 
   43| function scoreToConfidence(score: number): number {
   44|   const absScore = Math.abs(score);
   45|   // Keep it simple and monotonic: stronger score -> higher confidence.
   46|   // Floor slightly above 0.5 so BUY/SELL thresholded signals don't look low-confidence.
   47|   return clamp(0.55, absScore, 0.95);
   48| }
   49| 
   50| function computeSignalsForCluster(exposureByFactor: Map<string, number>): PortfolioSignalRow[] {
   51|   const assets = Object.keys(factorSignalMap) as Array<keyof typeof factorSignalMap>;
   52| 
   53|   const results: PortfolioSignalRow[] = [];
   54|   for (const asset of assets) {
   55|     let score = 0;
   56|     const weights = factorSignalMap[asset];
   57| 
   58|     for (const [factor, exposure] of exposureByFactor.entries()) {
   59|       const weight = (weights as Record<string, number>)[factor];
   60|       if (!Number.isFinite(weight)) continue;
   61|       score += exposure * weight;
   62|     }
   63| 
   64|     const signal = scoreToSignal(score);
   65|     const confidence = scoreToConfidence(score);
   66| 
   67|     results.push({
   68|       // cluster_id filled by caller
   69|       cluster_id: "",
   70|       asset: asset.toString(),
   71|       signal,
   72|       confidence,
   73|     });
   74|   }
   75| 
   76|   return results;
   77| }
   78| 
   79| async function loadFactorExposuresForClusters(
   80|   clusterIds: string[],
   81| ): Promise<FactorExposureRow[]> {
   82|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   83| 
   84|   const unique = Array.from(new Set(clusterIds.filter(Boolean)));
   85|   if (unique.length === 0) return [];
   86| 
   87|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   88|     .from("event_factor_exposures")
   89|     .select("cluster_id,factor,exposure")
   90|     .in("cluster_id", unique);
   91| 
   92|   if (error) {
   93|     throw new Error(`Failed to load factor exposures: ${error.message}`);
   94|   }
   95| 
   96|   return (data as FactorExposureRow[] | null) ?? [];
   97| }
   98| 
   99| export async function runPortfolioSignalEngine(): Promise<void> {
  100|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  101| 
  102|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
  103|     .from("pipeline_events")
  104|     .select("id,payload")
  105|     .eq("event_type", "SIGNAL_CREATED")
  106|     .eq("processed", false)
  107|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
  108|     .limit(20);
  109| 
  110|   if (error) {
  111|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
  112|   }
  113| 
  114|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
  115|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
  116| 
  117|   const seen = new Set<string>();
  118|   const unique: PipelineEventRow[] = [];
  119|   for (const evt of pending) {
  120|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
  121|     if (!clusterId) {
  122|       unique.push(evt);
  123|       continue;
  124|     }
  125|     if (seen.has(clusterId)) continue;
  126|     seen.add(clusterId);
  127|     unique.push(evt);
  128|   }
  129| 
  130|   await workerPoolForEach(
  131|     unique,
  132|     async (evt) => {
  133|     const clusterId = extractClusterIdFromPayload(evt.payload);
  134| 
  135|     await withStageSpan({
  136|       supabase,
  137|       stageName: "portfolio_signal",
  138|       clusterId,
  139|       eventId: evt.id,
  140|       statusOnSuccess: clusterId ? "success" : "skipped",
  141|       fn: async () => {
  142|         if (!clusterId) {
  143|           const { error: markError } = await supabase
  144|             .from("pipeline_events")
  145|             .update({ processed: true })
  146|             .eq("id", evt.id);
  147| 
  148|           if (markError) {
  149|             throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  150|           }
  151| 
  152|           return;
  153|         }
  154| 
  155|         const { data: existingSignals, error: existingError } = await supabase
  156|           .from("portfolio_signals")
  157|           .select("id")
  158|           .eq("cluster_id", clusterId)
  159|           .limit(1);
  160| 
  161|         if (existingError) {
  162|           throw new Error(`Failed to check existing signals: ${existingError.message}`);
  163|         }
  164| 
  165|         if ((existingSignals ?? []).length === 0) {
  166|           const exposures = await loadFactorExposuresForClusters([clusterId]);
  167| 
  168|           const factorSums = new Map<string, number>();
  169|           for (const row of exposures) {
  170|             const factor = (row.factor ?? "").toString().trim();
  171|             const exposure = Number(row.exposure);
  172|             if (!factor || !Number.isFinite(exposure)) continue;
  173|             factorSums.set(factor, (factorSums.get(factor) ?? 0) + exposure);
  174|           }
  175| 
  176|           const signals = computeSignalsForCluster(factorSums).map((s) => ({
  177|             ...s,
  178|             cluster_id: clusterId,
  179|           }));
  180| 
  181|           const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
  182|             .from("portfolio_signals")
  183|             .delete()
  184|             .eq("cluster_id", clusterId);
  185| 
  186|           if (deleteError) {
  187|             throw new Error(`Failed to clear existing signals: ${deleteError.message}`);
  188|           }
  189| 
  190|           if (signals.length > 0) {
  191|             const { error: insertError } = await supabase
  192|               .from("portfolio_signals")
  193|               .insert(signals);
  194| 
  195|             if (insertError) {
  196|               throw new Error(`Failed to insert portfolio signals: ${insertError.message}`);
  197|             }
  198|           }
  199|         }
  200| 
  201|         const { error: markEventError } = await supabase
  202|           .from("pipeline_events")
  203|           .update({ processed: true })
  204|           .eq("id", evt.id);
  205| 
  206|         if (markEventError) {
  207|           throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markEventError.message}`);
  208|         }
  209| 
  210|         await emitClusterEventOnce({
  211|           supabase,
  212|           eventType: "INSIGHT_REQUIRED",
  213|           clusterId,
  214|         });
  215|       },
  216|     });
  217|     },
  218|     { concurrency: Number(process.env.PIPELINE_CONCURRENCY ?? 5) || 5 },
  219|   );
  220| }

===== FILE: services\rankingEngine.ts =====

    1| export type RankingWeights = {
    2|   relevance: number;
    3|   recency: number;
    4|   impactStrength: number;
    5|   confidence: number;
    6|   factorExposureStrength: number;
    7| };
    8| 
    9| export type RankingConfig = {
   10|   weights: RankingWeights;
   11| 
   12|   /**
   13|    * Recency term decays with age using an exponential half-life.
   14|    * recency = exp(-ln(2) * ageDays / recencyHalfLifeDays)
   15|    */
   16|   recencyHalfLifeDays: number;
   17| 
   18|   /**
   19|    * Normalizes absolute impact score into [0,1] via: clamp(|impact| / impactScoreScale).
   20|    */
   21|   impactScoreScale: number;
   22| 
   23|   /**
   24|    * Normalizes factor exposure strength into [0,1] via: clamp(exposureStrength / factorExposureScale).
   25|    */
   26|   factorExposureScale: number;
   27| 
   28|   /**
   29|    * If true, confidence uses signal confidence first, otherwise insight confidence.
   30|    */
   31|   preferSignalConfidence: boolean;
   32| 
   33|   now?: () => Date;
   34| };
   35| 
   36| export const rankingConfig: RankingConfig = {
   37|   weights: {
   38|     relevance: 0.5,
   39|     recency: 0.2,
   40|     impactStrength: 0.2,
   41|     confidence: 0.1,
   42|     factorExposureStrength: 0.1,
   43|   },
   44|   recencyHalfLifeDays: 7,
   45|   impactScoreScale: 1,
   46|   factorExposureScale: 1,
   47|   preferSignalConfidence: true,
   48| };
   49| 
   50| function clamp01(value: number): number {
   51|   if (!Number.isFinite(value)) return 0;
   52|   return Math.min(1, Math.max(0, value));
   53| }
   54| 
   55| function safeNumber(value: unknown): number {
   56|   const n = typeof value === "number" ? value : Number(value);
   57|   return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : 0;
   58| }
   59| 
   60| export function computeRecencyWeight(createdAtIso: string | null | undefined, config: RankingConfig = rankingConfig): number {
   61|   if (!createdAtIso) return 0;
   62|   const createdMs = Date.parse(createdAtIso);
   63|   if (!Number.isFinite(createdMs)) return 0;
   64| 
   65|   const now = config.now ? config.now() : new Date();
   66|   const ageMs = Math.max(0, now.getTime() - createdMs);
   67|   const ageDays = ageMs / (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
   68| 
   69|   const halfLife = config.recencyHalfLifeDays;
   70|   if (!Number.isFinite(halfLife) || halfLife <= 0) return 0;
   71| 
   72|   const recency = Math.exp((-Math.LN2 * ageDays) / halfLife);
   73|   return clamp01(recency);
   74| }
   75| 
   76| export type RankingInputs = {
   77|   relevanceScore: number;
   78|   createdAt: string | null;
   79|   impactScore: number;
   80|   signalConfidence: number | null;
   81|   insightConfidence: number | null;
   82|   factorExposureStrength: number;
   83| };
   84| 
   85| export type RankingBreakdown = {
   86|   relevance: number;
   87|   recency: number;
   88|   impactStrength: number;
   89|   confidence: number;
   90|   factorExposureStrength: number;
   91|   score: number;
   92| };
   93| 
   94| export function computeInsightRanking(
   95|   inputs: RankingInputs,
   96|   config: RankingConfig = rankingConfig,
   97| ): RankingBreakdown {
   98|   const relevance = clamp01(safeNumber(inputs.relevanceScore));
   99|   const recency = computeRecencyWeight(inputs.createdAt, config);
  100| 
  101|   const rawImpact = safeNumber(inputs.impactScore);
  102|   const impactStrength = clamp01(Math.abs(rawImpact) / Math.max(1e-9, config.impactScoreScale));
  103| 
  104|   const rawExposure = safeNumber(inputs.factorExposureStrength);
  105|   const factorExposureStrength = clamp01(rawExposure / Math.max(1e-9, config.factorExposureScale));
  106| 
  107|   const signalConf = clamp01(safeNumber(inputs.signalConfidence));
  108|   const insightConf = clamp01(safeNumber(inputs.insightConfidence));
  109|   const hasSignal = inputs.signalConfidence !== null && inputs.signalConfidence !== undefined;
  110|   const hasInsight = inputs.insightConfidence !== null && inputs.insightConfidence !== undefined;
  111|   const confidence = config.preferSignalConfidence
  112|     ? (hasSignal ? signalConf : hasInsight ? insightConf : 0)
  113|     : (hasInsight ? insightConf : hasSignal ? signalConf : 0);
  114| 
  115|   const w = config.weights;
  116|   const score =
  117|     relevance * w.relevance +
  118|     recency * w.recency +
  119|     impactStrength * w.impactStrength +
  120|     confidence * w.confidence +
  121|     factorExposureStrength * w.factorExposureStrength;
  122| 
  123|   return {
  124|     relevance,
  125|     recency,
  126|     impactStrength,
  127|     confidence,
  128|     factorExposureStrength,
  129|     score,
  130|   };
  131| }
  132| 
  133| export function computeInsightRankingScore(inputs: RankingInputs, config: RankingConfig = rankingConfig): number {
  134|   return computeInsightRanking(inputs, config).score;
  135| }

===== FILE: services\relevanceEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| 
    3| type UserPortfolioRow = {
    4|   user_id: string | null;
    5|   asset: string | null;
    6| };
    7| 
    8| type AssetTagRow = {
    9|   tag: string | null;
   10| };
   11| 
   12| type InsightTagRow = {
   13|   insight_id: string | null;
   14|   tag: string | null;
   15| };
   16| 
   17| function clamp(min: number, value: number, max: number): number {
   18|   return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
   19| }
   20| 
   21| function uniq<T>(items: T[]): T[] {
   22|   return Array.from(new Set(items));
   23| }
   24| 
   25| export async function runRelevanceEngine(): Promise<void> {
   26|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   27| 
   28|   // 1) Load users and their assets.
   29|   const { data: portfolioRows, error: portfolioError } = await supabase
   30|     .from("user_portfolios")
   31|     .select("user_id,asset")
   32|     .limit(500);
   33| 
   34|   if (portfolioError) {
   35|     throw new Error(
   36|       `Failed to load user_portfolios (expected columns: user_id, asset): ${portfolioError.message}`,
   37|     );
   38|   }
   39| 
   40|   const rows = (portfolioRows as UserPortfolioRow[] | null) ?? [];
   41|   if (rows.length === 0) return;
   42| 
   43|   const assetsByUser = new Map<string, string[]>();
   44|   for (const row of rows) {
   45|     const userId = (row.user_id ?? "").toString().trim();
   46|     const asset = (row.asset ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase();
   47|     if (!userId || !asset) continue;
   48| 
   49|     const list = assetsByUser.get(userId) ?? [];
   50|     list.push(asset);
   51|     assetsByUser.set(userId, list);
   52|   }
   53| 
   54|   const userIds = Array.from(assetsByUser.keys()).slice(0, 20);
   55|   if (userIds.length === 0) return;
   56| 
   57|   for (const userId of userIds) {
   58|     const assets = uniq((assetsByUser.get(userId) ?? []).filter(Boolean));
   59|     if (assets.length === 0) continue;
   60| 
   61|     // 2) Fetch tags for user assets.
   62|     const { data: assetTags, error: assetTagsError } = await supabase
   63|       .from("asset_tags")
   64|       .select("tag")
   65|       .in("asset", assets);
   66| 
   67|     if (assetTagsError) {
   68|       throw new Error(`Failed to load asset tags: ${assetTagsError.message}`);
   69|     }
   70| 
   71|     const userTags = uniq(
   72|       ((assetTags as AssetTagRow[] | null) ?? [])
   73|         .map((r) => (r.tag ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase())
   74|         .filter(Boolean),
   75|     );
   76| 
   77|     if (userTags.length === 0) {
   78|       // Still emit an update event so downstream systems know this user was processed.
   79|       const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
   80|         event_type: "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED",
   81|         payload: { user_id: userId },
   82|       });
   83| 
   84|       if (emitError) {
   85|         throw new Error(
   86|           `Failed to emit USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED event: ${emitError.message}`,
   87|         );
   88|       }
   89| 
   90|       continue;
   91|     }
   92| 
   93|     // 3) Match insight tags.
   94|     const { data: matchingInsightTags, error: insightTagsError } = await supabase
   95|       .from("insight_tags")
   96|       .select("insight_id,tag")
   97|       .in("tag", userTags)
   98|       .limit(5000);
   99| 
  100|     if (insightTagsError) {
  101|       throw new Error(`Failed to load matching insight tags: ${insightTagsError.message}`);
  102|     }
  103| 
  104|     const matches = (matchingInsightTags as InsightTagRow[] | null) ?? [];
  105| 
  106|     // 4) Compute relevance score: match_count / total_user_tags
  107|     const matchCountByInsight = new Map<string, number>();
  108|     for (const row of matches) {
  109|       const insightId = (row.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  110|       if (!insightId) continue;
  111|       matchCountByInsight.set(insightId, (matchCountByInsight.get(insightId) ?? 0) + 1);
  112|     }
  113| 
  114|     // Keep the index bounded per user.
  115|     const scored = Array.from(matchCountByInsight.entries())
  116|       .map(([insightId, matchCount]) => ({
  117|         insight_id: insightId,
  118|         relevance_score: clamp(0, matchCount / userTags.length, 1),
  119|       }))
  120|       .sort((a, b) => b.relevance_score - a.relevance_score)
  121|       .slice(0, 200);
  122| 
  123|     // 5) Insert relevance index (idempotent per run).
  124|     const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
  125|       .from("user_relevance_index")
  126|       .delete()
  127|       .eq("user_id", userId);
  128| 
  129|     if (deleteError) {
  130|       throw new Error(`Failed to clear old relevance rows: ${deleteError.message}`);
  131|     }
  132| 
  133|     if (scored.length > 0) {
  134|       const inserts = scored.map((r) => ({
  135|         user_id: userId,
  136|         insight_id: r.insight_id,
  137|         relevance_score: r.relevance_score,
  138|       }));
  139| 
  140|       const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("user_relevance_index").insert(inserts);
  141|       if (insertError) {
  142|         throw new Error(`Failed to insert relevance index: ${insertError.message}`);
  143|       }
  144|     }
  145| 
  146|     // Emit update event
  147|     const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  148|       event_type: "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED",
  149|       payload: { user_id: userId },
  150|     });
  151| 
  152|     if (emitError) {
  153|       throw new Error(`Failed to emit USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED event: ${emitError.message}`);
  154|     }
  155|   }
  156| }

===== FILE: services\runtimeManager.ts =====

    1| import { spawn, type ChildProcessWithoutNullStreams } from "child_process";
    2| import { fileURLToPath } from "url";
    3| import path from "path";
    4| 
    5| import { validatePipelineSchemaOrThrow } from "./schemaValidator";
    6| 
    7| type ServiceKind = "daemon" | "scheduled";
    8| 
    9| type ManagedService = {
   10|   name: string;
   11|   kind: ServiceKind;
   12|   command: string;
   13|   args: string[];
   14|   restartOnCrash: boolean;
   15| };
   16| 
   17| type RuntimeOptions = {
   18|   ingestEveryMs?: number;
   19| };
   20| 
   21| type SupervisorState = {
   22|   shuttingDown: boolean;
   23|   children: Map<string, ChildProcessWithoutNullStreams>;
   24|   timers: Set<NodeJS.Timeout>;
   25|   ingestRunning: boolean;
   26| };
   27| 
   28| function sleep(ms: number): Promise<void> {
   29|   return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, ms));
   30| }
   31| 
   32| function npxCmd(): string {
   33|   return process.platform === "win32" ? "npx.cmd" : "npx";
   34| }
   35| 
   36| function timestamp(): string {
   37|   return new Date().toISOString();
   38| }
   39| 
   40| function log(name: string, message: string): void {
   41|   console.log(`[${timestamp()}] [runtime] [${name}] ${message}`);
   42| }
   43| 
   44| function wireOutput(name: string, child: ChildProcessWithoutNullStreams): void {
   45|   const prefix = `[${name}] `;
   46| 
   47|   child.stdout.on("data", (buf: Buffer) => {
   48|     const text = buf.toString("utf8");
   49|     for (const line of text.split(/\r?\n/)) {
   50|       if (!line) continue;
   51|       process.stdout.write(prefix + line + "\n");
   52|     }
   53|   });
   54| 
   55|   child.stderr.on("data", (buf: Buffer) => {
   56|     const text = buf.toString("utf8");
   57|     for (const line of text.split(/\r?\n/)) {
   58|       if (!line) continue;
   59|       process.stderr.write(prefix + line + "\n");
   60|     }
   61|   });
   62| }
   63| 
   64| function spawnService(proc: ManagedService): ChildProcessWithoutNullStreams {
   65|   const child = spawn(proc.command, proc.args, {
   66|     stdio: ["pipe", "pipe", "pipe"],
   67|     env: { ...process.env },
   68|   });
   69| 
   70|   wireOutput(proc.name, child);
   71|   return child;
   72| }
   73| 
   74| async function superviseDaemon(state: SupervisorState, service: ManagedService): Promise<void> {
   75|   let attempt = 0;
   76| 
   77|   while (!state.shuttingDown) {
   78|     attempt += 1;
   79|     log(service.name, `starting (attempt=${attempt})`);
   80| 
   81|     const child = spawnService(service);
   82|     state.children.set(service.name, child);
   83| 
   84|     const exitCode: number | null = await new Promise((resolve) => {
   85|       child.on("exit", (code) => resolve(code));
   86|     });
   87| 
   88|     state.children.delete(service.name);
   89| 
   90|     if (state.shuttingDown) {
   91|       log(service.name, `stopped (exit=${exitCode ?? "null"})`);
   92|       return;
   93|     }
   94| 
   95|     log(service.name, `crashed (exit=${exitCode ?? "null"})`);
   96| 
   97|     if (!service.restartOnCrash) return;
   98| 
   99|     const backoffMs = Math.min(30_000, 1_000 * Math.pow(2, Math.min(5, attempt)));
  100|     log(service.name, `restarting in ${backoffMs}ms`);
  101|     await sleep(backoffMs);
  102|   }
  103| }
  104| 
  105| async function runIngestOnce(state: SupervisorState, service: ManagedService): Promise<void> {
  106|   if (state.shuttingDown) return;
  107|   if (state.ingestRunning) {
  108|     log(service.name, "skipping (previous run still active)");
  109|     return;
  110|   }
  111| 
  112|   state.ingestRunning = true;
  113|   try {
  114|     log(service.name, "starting one-shot run");
  115|     const child = spawnService(service);
  116|     state.children.set(service.name, child);
  117| 
  118|     const exitCode: number | null = await new Promise((resolve) => {
  119|       child.on("exit", (code) => resolve(code));
  120|     });
  121| 
  122|     state.children.delete(service.name);
  123| 
  124|     if (exitCode === 0) {
  125|       log(service.name, "completed successfully");
  126|     } else {
  127|       log(service.name, `failed (exit=${exitCode ?? "null"})`);
  128|     }
  129|   } finally {
  130|     state.ingestRunning = false;
  131|   }
  132| }
  133| 
  134| function scheduleIngest(state: SupervisorState, service: ManagedService, everyMs: number): void {
  135|   const timer = setInterval(() => {
  136|     runIngestOnce(state, service).catch((err) => {
  137|       log(service.name, `ingest run error: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`);
  138|     });
  139|   }, everyMs);
  140| 
  141|   state.timers.add(timer);
  142| 
  143|   // Kick once immediately on startup.
  144|   runIngestOnce(state, service).catch((err) => {
  145|     log(service.name, `initial ingest error: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`);
  146|   });
  147| }
  148| 
  149| function shutdown(state: SupervisorState): void {
  150|   if (state.shuttingDown) return;
  151|   state.shuttingDown = true;
  152| 
  153|   log("manager", "shutting down");
  154| 
  155|   for (const t of state.timers) {
  156|     clearInterval(t);
  157|     clearTimeout(t);
  158|   }
  159|   state.timers.clear();
  160| 
  161|   for (const [name, child] of state.children.entries()) {
  162|     try {
  163|       log(name, "sending termination signal");
  164|       // On Windows, kill() ignores the signal string.
  165|       child.kill("SIGTERM");
  166|     } catch {
  167|       // ignore
  168|     }
  169|   }
  170| }
  171| 
  172| export async function startRuntime(options?: RuntimeOptions): Promise<void> {
  173|   const ingestEveryMs = options?.ingestEveryMs ?? 5 * 60_000;
  174| 
  175|   const state: SupervisorState = {
  176|     shuttingDown: false,
  177|     children: new Map(),
  178|     timers: new Set(),
  179|     ingestRunning: false,
  180|   };
  181| 
  182|   process.on("SIGINT", () => shutdown(state));
  183|   process.on("SIGTERM", () => shutdown(state));
  184| 
  185|   const services: ManagedService[] = [
  186|     {
  187|       name: "pipelineListener",
  188|       kind: "daemon",
  189|       command: npxCmd(),
  190|       args: ["tsx", "services/pipelineListener.ts"],
  191|       restartOnCrash: true,
  192|     },
  193|     {
  194|       name: "pipelineMonitor",
  195|       kind: "daemon",
  196|       command: npxCmd(),
  197|       args: ["tsx", "services/pipelineMonitor.ts"],
  198|       restartOnCrash: true,
  199|     },
  200|     {
  201|       name: "pipelineInvariantMonitor",
  202|       kind: "daemon",
  203|       command: npxCmd(),
  204|       args: ["tsx", "services/pipelineInvariantMonitor.ts"],
  205|       restartOnCrash: true,
  206|     },
  207|     {
  208|       name: "newsFetcher",
  209|       kind: "scheduled",
  210|       command: npxCmd(),
  211|       args: ["tsx", "services/newsFetcherRunner.ts"],
  212|       restartOnCrash: false,
  213|     },
  214|   ];
  215| 
  216|   log("schemaValidator", "validating required tables");
  217|   await validatePipelineSchemaOrThrow();
  218| 
  219|   log("manager", "starting runtime services");
  220| 
  221|   // Start daemons.
  222|   const daemonPromises = services
  223|     .filter((s) => s.kind === "daemon")
  224|     .map((s) => superviseDaemon(state, s));
  225| 
  226|   // Schedule ingestion.
  227|   const ingestService = services.find((s) => s.name === "newsFetcher");
  228|   if (ingestService) {
  229|     scheduleIngest(state, ingestService, ingestEveryMs);
  230|   }
  231| 
  232|   // Wait for daemons (this keeps the process alive).
  233|   await Promise.all(daemonPromises);
  234| }
  235| 
  236| function isMainModule(): boolean {
  237|   try {
  238|     const current = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
  239|     const invoked = process.argv[1] ?? "";
  240|     const invokedAbs = path.resolve(process.cwd(), invoked);
  241|     return path.normalize(invokedAbs).toLowerCase() === path.normalize(current).toLowerCase();
  242|   } catch {
  243|     return false;
  244|   }
  245| }
  246| 
  247| // Runnable via: npx tsx services/runtimeManager.ts
  248| if (isMainModule()) {
  249|   startRuntime().catch((err) => {
  250|     console.error(err);
  251|     process.exit(1);
  252|   });
  253| }

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
