    3| type RequiredTable = {
    4|   table: string;
    5|   probeColumn: string;
    6|   migration: string;
    7| };
    8| 
    9| const REQUIRED_TABLES: RequiredTable[] = [
   10|   { table: "event_clusters", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0008_event_clusters.sql" },
   11|   { table: "canonical_events", probeColumn: "cluster_id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0018_canonical_events.sql" },
   12|   { table: "event_factor_exposures", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0013_event_factor_exposures.sql" },
   13|   { table: "event_impact_scores", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0012_event_impact_scores.sql" },
   14|   { table: "portfolio_signals", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0017_portfolio_signals.sql" },
   15|   { table: "event_insights", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0020_event_insights.sql" },
   16|   { table: "portfolio_allocations", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0023_portfolio_allocations.sql" },
   17|   { table: "insight_tags", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0025_insight_tags.sql" },
   18|   { table: "asset_tags", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0026_asset_tags.sql" },
   19|   { table: "user_segments", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0028_user_segments.sql" },
   20|   { table: "user_relevance_index", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0027_user_relevance_index.sql" },
   21|   { table: "user_feed", probeColumn: "id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0031_user_feed.sql" },
   22|   { table: "user_feed_cache", probeColumn: "user_id", migration: "supabase/migrations/0032_user_feed_cache.sql" },
   23| ];
   24| 
   25| type ValidationFailure = {
   26|   table: string;
   27|   migration: string;
   28|   errorMessage: string;
   29| };
   30| 
   31| async function probeTable(table: RequiredTable): Promise<ValidationFailure | null> {
   32|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   33| 
   34|   const { error } = await supabase
   35|     .from(table.table)
   36|     .select(table.probeColumn)
   37|     .limit(1);
   38| 
   39|   if (!error) return null;
   40| 
   41|   return {
   42|     table: table.table,
   43|     migration: table.migration,
   44|     errorMessage: error.message,
   45|   };
   46| }
   47| 
   48| /**
   49|  * Verifies required pipeline tables exist.
   50|  *
   51|  * Throws if any table is missing/unreadable.
   52|  */
   53| export async function validatePipelineSchemaOrThrow(): Promise<void> {
   54|   const failures: ValidationFailure[] = [];
   55| 
   56|   for (const t of REQUIRED_TABLES) {
   57|     const failure = await probeTable(t);
   58|     if (failure) failures.push(failure);
   59|   }
   60| 
   61|   if (failures.length === 0) {
   62|     console.log("[schemaValidator] schema ok");
   63|     return;
   64|   }
   65| 
   66|   console.error("[schemaValidator] schema invalid; missing required tables:");
   67|   for (const f of failures) {
   68|     console.error(
   69|       `- ${f.table}: apply ${f.migration} (probe error: ${f.errorMessage})`,
   70|     );
   71|   }
   72| 
   73|   throw new Error(`Pipeline schema validation failed (missing=${failures.length})`);
   74| }

===== FILE: services\segmentRelevanceEngine.ts =====

    1| import { createSupabaseServerClient } from "./newsFetcher";
    2| 
    3| type SegmentRow = {
    4|   segment: string | null;
    5| };
    6| 
    7| type SegmentTagRow = {
    8|   tag: string | null;
    9| };
   10| 
   11| type InsightTagRow = {
   12|   insight_id: string | null;
   13|   tag: string | null;
   14| };
   15| 
   16| type UserPortfolioRow = {
   17|   user_id: string | null;
   18|   asset: string | null;
   19| };
   20| 
   21| function clamp(min: number, value: number, max: number): number {
   22|   return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
   23| }
   24| 
   25| function uniq<T>(items: T[]): T[] {
   26|   return Array.from(new Set(items));
   27| }
   28| 
   29| function inferSegmentsFromAssets(assets: string[]): string[] {
   30|   const segments = new Set<string>();
   31|   const lower = assets.map((a) => a.toLowerCase());
   32| 
   33|   // Spec examples
   34|   if (lower.some((a) => a.includes("equity") || a.includes("tech"))) {
   35|     segments.add("tech_investors");
   36|   }
   37| 
   38|   if (lower.some((a) => a.includes("bond") || a.includes("treasury"))) {
   39|     segments.add("bond_investors");
   40|   }
   41| 
   42|   if (lower.some((a) => a.includes("bitcoin") || a.includes("crypto"))) {
   43|     segments.add("crypto_investors");
   44|   }
   45| 
   46|   return Array.from(segments);
   47| }
   48| 
   49| async function computeSegmentInsightIndex(segment: string): Promise<void> {
   50|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   51| 
   52|   // 2) Fetch tags for each segment
   53|   const { data: segTagsData, error: segTagsError } = await supabase
   54|     .from("segment_tags")
   55|     .select("tag")
   56|     .eq("segment", segment)
   57|     .limit(200);
   58| 
   59|   if (segTagsError) {
   60|     throw new Error(`Failed to load segment tags: ${segTagsError.message}`);
   61|   }
   62| 
   63|   const segmentTags = uniq(
   64|     ((segTagsData as SegmentTagRow[] | null) ?? [])
   65|       .map((r) => (r.tag ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase())
   66|       .filter(Boolean),
   67|   );
   68| 
   69|   // Idempotent: clear prior rows even if tag set is empty.
   70|   const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
   71|     .from("segment_insight_index")
   72|     .delete()
   73|     .eq("segment", segment);
   74| 
   75|   if (deleteError) {
   76|     throw new Error(`Failed to clear old segment index: ${deleteError.message}`);
   77|   }
   78| 
   79|   if (segmentTags.length === 0) return;
   80| 
   81|   // 3) Match insights
   82|   const { data: matchesData, error: matchesError } = await supabase
   83|     .from("insight_tags")
   84|     .select("insight_id,tag")
   85|     .in("tag", segmentTags)
   86|     .limit(10000);
   87| 
   88|   if (matchesError) {
   89|     throw new Error(`Failed to load matching insight tags: ${matchesError.message}`);
   90|   }
   91| 
   92|   const matches = (matchesData as InsightTagRow[] | null) ?? [];
   93| 
   94|   // 4) Compute relevance score = matching_tags / total_segment_tags
   95|   const matchCountByInsight = new Map<string, number>();
   96|   for (const row of matches) {
   97|     const insightId = (row.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim();
   98|     if (!insightId) continue;
   99|     matchCountByInsight.set(
  100|       insightId,
  101|       (matchCountByInsight.get(insightId) ?? 0) + 1,
  102|     );
  103|   }
  104| 
  105|   const scored = Array.from(matchCountByInsight.entries())
  106|     .map(([insightId, matchCount]) => ({
  107|       segment,
  108|       insight_id: insightId,
  109|       relevance_score: clamp(0, matchCount / segmentTags.length, 1),
  110|     }))
  111|     .sort((a, b) => b.relevance_score - a.relevance_score)
  112|     .slice(0, 500);
  113| 
  114|   if (scored.length === 0) return;
  115| 
  116|   // 5) Insert segment insight relevance
  117|   const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("segment_insight_index").insert(scored);
  118| 
  119|   if (insertError) {
  120|     throw new Error(`Failed to insert segment insight index: ${insertError.message}`);
  121|   }
  122| }
  123| 
  124| async function mapUsersToSegments(): Promise<void> {
  125|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  126| 
  127|   // Load a bounded window of user portfolios.
  128|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  129|     .from("user_portfolios")
  130|     .select("user_id,asset")
  131|     .limit(1000);
  132| 
  133|   if (error) {
  134|     throw new Error(
  135|       `Failed to load user_portfolios (expected columns: user_id, asset): ${error.message}`,
  136|     );
  137|   }
  138| 
  139|   const rows = (data as UserPortfolioRow[] | null) ?? [];
  140|   if (rows.length === 0) return;
  141| 
  142|   const assetsByUser = new Map<string, string[]>();
  143|   for (const row of rows) {
  144|     const userId = (row.user_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  145|     const asset = (row.asset ?? "").toString().trim();
  146|     if (!userId || !asset) continue;
  147|     const list = assetsByUser.get(userId) ?? [];
  148|     list.push(asset);
  149|     assetsByUser.set(userId, list);
  150|   }
  151| 
  152|   const userIds = Array.from(assetsByUser.keys()).slice(0, 200);
  153| 
  154|   for (const userId of userIds) {
  155|     const assets = uniq((assetsByUser.get(userId) ?? []).filter(Boolean));
  156|     const segments = inferSegmentsFromAssets(assets);
  157| 
  158|     // Idempotent mapping.
  159|     const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
  160|       .from("user_segments")
  161|       .delete()
  162|       .eq("user_id", userId);
  163| 
  164|     if (deleteError) {
  165|       throw new Error(`Failed to clear user segments: ${deleteError.message}`);
  166|     }
  167| 
  168|     if (segments.length === 0) continue;
  169| 
  170|     const inserts = segments.map((segment) => ({
  171|       user_id: userId,
  172|       segment,
  173|     }));
  174| 
  175|     const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("user_segments").insert(inserts);
  176| 
  177|     if (insertError) {
  178|       throw new Error(`Failed to insert user segments: ${insertError.message}`);
  179|     }
  180|   }
  181| }
  182| 
  183| export async function runSegmentRelevanceEngine(): Promise<void> {
  184|   // Step 5: keep user->segment mapping fresh.
  185|   await mapUsersToSegments();
  186| 
  187|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  188| 
  189|   // 1) Load segments
  190|   const { data: segmentsData, error: segmentsError } = await supabase
  191|     .from("segment_tags")
  192|     .select("segment")
  193|     .limit(200);
  194| 
  195|   if (segmentsError) {
  196|     throw new Error(`Failed to load segments: ${segmentsError.message}`);
  197|   }
  198| 
  199|   const segments = uniq(
  200|     ((segmentsData as SegmentRow[] | null) ?? [])
  201|       .map((r) => (r.segment ?? "").toString().trim())
  202|       .filter(Boolean),
  203|   );
  204| 
  205|   if (segments.length === 0) return;
  206| 
  207|   for (const segment of segments) {
  208|     await computeSegmentInsightIndex(segment);
  209|   }
  210| }

===== FILE: services\trajectoryService.ts =====

    1| import { futureValue } from "@/lib/finance";
    2| import {
    3|   generateImprovements,
    4|   type ImprovementSuggestion,
    5| } from "@/engines/improvementEngine";
    6| import {
    7|   classifyTrajectory,
    8|   detectTrajectoryCause,
    9|   type TrajectoryCause,
   10|   type TrajectoryInsight,
   11| } from "@/engines/insightEngine";
   12| import { getReturnInsight, type ReturnInsight } from "@/engines/returnInsightEngine";
   13| import { marketScenarios } from "@/simulation/marketScenarios";
   14| import {
   15|   runScenarios,
   16|   type FinancialInputs,
   17|   type Scenario,
   18|   type ScenarioResult,
   19| } from "@/simulation/scenarioEngine";
   20| import { solveForN, solveForPMT } from "@/lib/solver";
   21| 
   22| export type TrajectoryAnalysis = {
   23|   projectedFutureValue: number;
   24|   nActual: number;
   25|   compression: number;
   26|   accelerationScore: number;
   27|   requiredMonthlySavings: number | null;
   28|   increaseMonthlySavings: number | null;
   29|   shock: {
   30|     rNew: number;
   31|     projectedFutureValue: number;
   32|     nActual: number;
   33|     monthsAdded: number;
   34|   };
   35|   returnInsight: ReturnInsight;
   36|   insight: TrajectoryInsight;
   37|   cause: TrajectoryCause;
   38|   improvements: ImprovementSuggestion[];
   39|   scenarios: ScenarioResult[];
   40|   marketScenarios: ScenarioResult[];
   41| };
   42| 
   43| const contributionScenarios: Scenario[] = [
   44|   {
   45|     label: "+₹500 per month",
   46|     modify: (inputs: FinancialInputs) => ({
   47|       ...inputs,
   48|       monthlySavings: inputs.monthlySavings + 500,
   49|     }),
   50|   },
   51|   {
   52|     label: "+₹1000 per month",
   53|     modify: (inputs: FinancialInputs) => ({
   54|       ...inputs,
   55|       monthlySavings: inputs.monthlySavings + 1000,
   56|     }),
   57|   },
   58|   {
   59|     label: "+₹2000 per month",
   60|     modify: (inputs: FinancialInputs) => ({
   61|       ...inputs,
   62|       monthlySavings: inputs.monthlySavings + 2000,
   63|     }),
   64|   },
   65| ];
   66| 
   67| export function analyzeTrajectory(inputs: FinancialInputs): TrajectoryAnalysis {
   68|   // 1) Projected future value at the user's time horizon.
   69|   const projectedFutureValue = futureValue(
   70|     inputs.currentSavings,
   71|     inputs.monthlySavings,
   72|     inputs.expectedReturn,
   73|     inputs.timeHorizon,
   74|   );
   75| 
   76|   // 2) Years to reach target.
   77|   const nActual = solveForN(
   78|     inputs.currentSavings,
   79|     inputs.monthlySavings,
   80|     inputs.expectedReturn,
   81|     inputs.targetAmount,
   82|   );
   83| 
   84|   const compression = inputs.timeHorizon - nActual;
   85| 
   86|   // Acceleration Score
   87|   if (inputs.timeHorizon <= 0) {
   88|     throw new RangeError("Time horizon must be > 0");
   89|   }
   90|   const requiredPace = inputs.targetAmount / inputs.timeHorizon;
   91|   const actualPace = projectedFutureValue / inputs.timeHorizon;
   92|   const accelerationScore =
   93|     requiredPace === 0
   94|       ? actualPace === 0
   95|         ? 1
   96|         : Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY
   97|       : actualPace / requiredPace;
   98| 
   99|   // Inflation shock simulation: r_new = r_old - 0.01
  100|   const rNew = inputs.expectedReturn - 0.01;
  101|   if (rNew < 0) {
  102|     throw new RangeError(
  103|       "Inflation shock results in r < 0; unable to run simulation",
  104|     );
  105|   }
  106| 
  107|   const projectedFutureValueShock = futureValue(
  108|     inputs.currentSavings,
  109|     inputs.monthlySavings,
  110|     rNew,
  111|     inputs.timeHorizon,
  112|   );
  113| 
  114|   const nActualShock = solveForN(
  115|     inputs.currentSavings,
  116|     inputs.monthlySavings,
  117|     rNew,
  118|     inputs.targetAmount,
  119|   );
  120| 
  121|   const monthsAdded = Math.max(0, Math.round((nActualShock - nActual) * 12));
  122| 
  123|   // Savings lever (only when behind)
  124|   const isBehind = compression < 0;
  125|   const requiredMonthlySavings = isBehind
  126|     ? solveForPMT(
  127|         inputs.currentSavings,
  128|         inputs.expectedReturn,
  129|         inputs.timeHorizon,
  130|         inputs.targetAmount,
  131|       )
  132|     : null;
  133| 
  134|   const increaseMonthlySavings =
  135|     isBehind && requiredMonthlySavings !== null
  136|       ? Math.max(0, requiredMonthlySavings - inputs.monthlySavings)
  137|       : null;
  138| 
  139|   // Layer-2 insights
  140|   const returnInsight = getReturnInsight(inputs.expectedReturn);
  141|   const insight = classifyTrajectory(compression, accelerationScore);
  142|   const cause = detectTrajectoryCause(
  143|     compression,
  144|     inputs.monthlySavings,
  145|     inputs.expectedReturn,
  146|     inputs.timeHorizon,
  147|     requiredMonthlySavings ?? undefined,
  148|   );
  149| 
  150|   // Improvement suggestions and scenarios
  151|   const improvements = isBehind ? generateImprovements(inputs, nActual) : [];
  152|   const scenarios = runScenarios(inputs, contributionScenarios)
  153|     .filter((s) => s.monthsImproved > 0)
  154|     .sort((a, b) => b.monthsImproved - a.monthsImproved);
  155| 
  156|   const marketScenarioResults = runScenarios(inputs, marketScenarios);
  157| 
  158|   return {
  159|     projectedFutureValue,
  160|     nActual,
  161|     compression,
  162|     accelerationScore,
  163|     requiredMonthlySavings,
  164|     increaseMonthlySavings,
  165|     shock: {
  166|       rNew,
  167|       projectedFutureValue: projectedFutureValueShock,
  168|       nActual: nActualShock,
  169|       monthsAdded,
  170|     },
  171|     returnInsight,
  172|     insight,
  173|     cause,
  174|     improvements,
  175|     scenarios,
  176|     marketScenarios: marketScenarioResults,
  177|   };
  178| }

   43| function extractPayload(payload: unknown): {
   44|   userId: string | null;
   45|   insightIds: string[];
   46| } {
   47|   if (!payload || typeof payload !== "object") {
   48|     return { userId: null, insightIds: [] };
   49|   }
   50| 
   51|   const rawUserId = (payload as { user_id?: unknown }).user_id;
   52|   const userId =
   53|     typeof rawUserId === "string" || typeof rawUserId === "number"
   54|       ? rawUserId.toString().trim() || null
   55|       : null;
   56| 
   57|   const rawInsightIds = (payload as { insight_ids?: unknown }).insight_ids;
   58|   const insightIds = Array.isArray(rawInsightIds)
   59|     ? rawInsightIds
   60|         .map((v) => (typeof v === "string" || typeof v === "number" ? v.toString().trim() : ""))
   61|         .filter(Boolean)
   62|     : [];
   63| 
   64|   return { userId, insightIds: uniq(insightIds) };
   65| }

   67| async function loadAffectedUsersByInsights(insightIds: string[]): Promise<string[]> {
   68|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   69|   const unique = uniq(insightIds.filter(Boolean));
   70|   if (unique.length === 0) return [];
   71| 
   72|   const { data, error } = await supabase
   73|     .from("insight_user_edges")
   74|     .select("user_id")
   75|     .in("insight_id", unique)
   76|     .limit(5000);
   77| 
   78|   if (error) {
   79|     throw new Error(`Failed to load affected users: ${error.message}`);
   80|   }
   81| 
   82|   const userIds = ((data as Array<{ user_id: string | null }> | null) ?? [])
   83|     .map((r) => (r.user_id ?? "").toString().trim())
   84|     .filter(Boolean);
   85| 
   86|   return uniq(userIds);
   87| }
   88| 
   89| async function rebuildUserFeed(userId: string): Promise<void> {
   90|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
   91| 
   92|   const { error: rankingProbeError } = await supabase
   93|     .from("user_feed")
   94|     .select("ranking_score")
   95|     .limit(1);
   96| 
   97|   const supportsRankingScore = !rankingProbeError;
   98| 
   99|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  100|     .from("user_relevance_index")
  101|     .select("user_id,insight_id,relevance_score")
  102|     .eq("user_id", userId)
  103|     .order("relevance_score", { ascending: false })
  104|     .limit(200);
  105| 
  106|   if (error) {
  107|     throw new Error(`Failed to load user relevance index: ${error.message}`);
  108|   }
  109| 
  110|   const rows = (data as RelevanceRow[] | null) ?? [];
  111| 
  112|   const insightIds = uniq(
  113|     rows
  114|       .map((row) => (row.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim())
  115|       .filter(Boolean),
  116|   );
  117| 
  118|   const insightById = new Map<string, InsightMetaRow>();
  119|   const clusterIds: string[] = [];
  120| 
  121|   if (insightIds.length > 0) {
  122|     const { data: insights, error: insightError } = await supabase
  123|       .from("event_insights")
  124|       .select("id,cluster_id,created_at,confidence")
  125|       .in("id", insightIds)
  126|       .limit(5000);
  127| 
  128|     if (insightError) {
  129|       throw new Error(`Failed to load event_insights metadata: ${insightError.message}`);
  130|     }
  131| 
  132|     for (const row of (insights as InsightMetaRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  133|       if (!row?.id) continue;
  134|       insightById.set(row.id, row);
  135|       const clusterId = (row.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  136|       if (clusterId) clusterIds.push(clusterId);
  137|     }
  138|   }
  139| 
  140|   const uniqueClusterIds = uniq(clusterIds);
  141| 
  142|   const impactStrengthByCluster = new Map<string, number>();
  143|   const confidenceByCluster = new Map<string, number>();
  144|   const exposureStrengthByCluster = new Map<string, number>();
  145| 
  146|   if (uniqueClusterIds.length > 0) {
  147|     const { data: impactRows, error: impactError } = await supabase
  148|       .from("event_impact_scores")
  149|       .select("cluster_id,impact_score,confidence")
  150|       .in("cluster_id", uniqueClusterIds)
  151|       .limit(5000);
  152| 
  153|     if (impactError) {
  154|       throw new Error(`Failed to load event_impact_scores: ${impactError.message}`);
  155|     }
  156| 
  157|     for (const row of (impactRows as ImpactScoreRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  158|       const clusterId = (row.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  159|       if (!clusterId) continue;
  160| 
  161|       const impact = Math.abs(Number(row.impact_score));
  162|       const conf = Number(row.confidence);
  163|       const adjusted =
  164|         Number.isFinite(impact) && Number.isFinite(conf)
  165|           ? impact * Math.max(0, Math.min(1, conf))
  166|           : Number.isFinite(impact)
  167|             ? impact
  168|             : 0;
  169| 
  170|       const prev = impactStrengthByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? 0;
  171|       if (adjusted > prev) impactStrengthByCluster.set(clusterId, adjusted);
  172|     }
  173| 
  174|     const { data: signalRows, error: signalError } = await supabase
  175|       .from("portfolio_signals")
  176|       .select("cluster_id,confidence")
  177|       .in("cluster_id", uniqueClusterIds)
  178|       .order("created_at", { ascending: false })
  179|       .limit(5000);
  180| 
  181|     if (signalError) {
  182|       throw new Error(`Failed to load portfolio_signals: ${signalError.message}`);
  183|     }
  184| 
  185|     for (const row of (signalRows as SignalConfidenceRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  186|       const clusterId = (row.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  187|       if (!clusterId) continue;
  188| 
  189|       const conf = Number(row.confidence);
  190|       if (!Number.isFinite(conf)) continue;
  191|       const clamped = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, conf));
  192| 
  193|       const prev = confidenceByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? 0;
  194|       if (clamped > prev) confidenceByCluster.set(clusterId, clamped);
  195|     }
  196| 
  197|     const { data: exposureRows, error: exposureError } = await supabase
  198|       .from("event_factor_exposures")
  199|       .select("cluster_id,exposure,confidence")
  200|       .in("cluster_id", uniqueClusterIds)
  201|       .order("created_at", { ascending: false })
  202|       .limit(10000);
  203| 
  204|     if (exposureError) {
  205|       throw new Error(`Failed to load event_factor_exposures: ${exposureError.message}`);
  206|     }
  207| 
  208|     for (const row of (exposureRows as FactorExposureRow[] | null) ?? []) {
  209|       const clusterId = (row.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  210|       if (!clusterId) continue;
  211| 
  212|       const exposure = Math.abs(Number(row.exposure));
  213|       const conf = Number(row.confidence);
  214|       const adjusted =
  215|         Number.isFinite(exposure) && Number.isFinite(conf)
  216|           ? exposure * Math.max(0, Math.min(1, conf))
  217|           : Number.isFinite(exposure)
  218|             ? exposure
  219|             : 0;
  220| 
  221|       const prev = exposureStrengthByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? 0;
  222|       if (adjusted > prev) exposureStrengthByCluster.set(clusterId, adjusted);
  223|     }
  224|   }
  225| 
  226|   const ranked = rows
  227|     .map((row) => {
  228|       const insightId = (row.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  229|       const relevanceScore = Number(row.relevance_score);
  230|       if (!insightId || !Number.isFinite(relevanceScore)) return null;
  231| 
  232|       const meta = insightById.get(insightId);
  233|       const createdAt = meta?.created_at ?? null;
  234|       const insightConfidence = meta?.confidence ?? null;
  235| 
  236|       const clusterId = (meta?.cluster_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  237|       const impactStrength = clusterId ? impactStrengthByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? 0 : 0;
  238|       const signalConfidence = clusterId ? confidenceByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? null : null;
  239|       const factorExposureStrength = clusterId ? exposureStrengthByCluster.get(clusterId) ?? 0 : 0;
  240| 
  241|       const rankingScore = computeInsightRankingScore(
  242|         {
  243|           relevanceScore,
  244|           createdAt,
  245|           impactScore: impactStrength,
  246|           signalConfidence,
  247|           insightConfidence,
  248|           factorExposureStrength,
  249|         },
  250|         rankingConfig,
  251|       );
  252| 
  253|       return {
  254|         user_id: userId,
  255|         insight_id: insightId,
  256|         relevance_score: relevanceScore,
  257|         ranking_score: rankingScore,
  258|       };
  259|     })
  260|     .filter(Boolean) as Array<{
  261|     user_id: string;
  262|     insight_id: string;
  263|     relevance_score: number;
  264|     ranking_score: number;
  265|   }>;
  266| 
  267|   const sorted = ranked
  268|     .sort((a, b) => b.ranking_score - a.ranking_score || b.relevance_score - a.relevance_score)
  269|     .slice(0, 100);
  270| 
  271|   const inserts = supportsRankingScore
  272|     ? sorted
  273|     : sorted.map((r) => ({
  274|         user_id: r.user_id,
  275|         insight_id: r.insight_id,
  276|         relevance_score: r.relevance_score,
  277|       }));
  278| 
  279|   const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
  280|     .from("user_feed")
  281|     .delete()
  282|     .eq("user_id", userId);
  283| 
  284|   if (deleteError) {
  285|     throw new Error(`Failed to clear user feed: ${deleteError.message}`);
  286|   }
  287| 
  288|   if (inserts.length > 0) {
  289|     const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("user_feed").insert(inserts);
  290| 
  291|     if (insertError) {
  292|       throw new Error(`Failed to insert user feed rows: ${insertError.message}`);
  293|     }
  294|   }
  295| 
  296|   const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  297|     event_type: "USER_FEED_DELTA",
  298|     payload: { user_id: userId },
  299|   });
  300| 
  301|   if (emitError) {
  302|     throw new Error(`Failed to emit USER_FEED_DELTA event: ${emitError.message}`);
  303|   }
  304| }
  305| 
  306| export async function runUserFeedEngine(): Promise<void> {
  307|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  308| 
  309|   const { data: events, error } = await supabase
  310|     .from("pipeline_events")
  311|     .select("id,payload")
  312|     .eq("event_type", "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED")
  313|     .eq("processed", false)
  314|     .order("created_at", { ascending: true })
  315|     .limit(25);
  316| 
  317|   if (error) {
  318|     throw new Error(`Failed to load pipeline events: ${error.message}`);
  319|   }
  320| 
  321|   const pending = (events as PipelineEventRow[] | null) ?? [];
  322|   if (pending.length === 0) return;
  323| 
  324|   for (const evt of pending) {
  325|     const { userId, insightIds } = extractPayload(evt.payload);
  326| 
  327|     let affectedUserIds: string[] = [];
  328|     if (insightIds.length > 0) {
  329|       affectedUserIds = await loadAffectedUsersByInsights(insightIds);
  330|     } else if (userId) {
  331|       affectedUserIds = [userId];
  332|     }
  333| 
  334|     affectedUserIds = uniq(affectedUserIds).slice(0, 500);
  335| 
  336|     for (const uid of affectedUserIds) {
  337|       await rebuildUserFeed(uid);
  338|     }
  339| 
  340|     const { error: markError } = await supabase
  341|       .from("pipeline_events")
  342|       .update({ processed: true })
  343|       .eq("id", evt.id);
  344| 
  345|     if (markError) {
  346|       throw new Error(`Failed to mark pipeline event processed: ${markError.message}`);
  347|     }
  348|   }
  349| }

   21| function clamp(min: number, value: number, max: number): number {
   22|   return Math.min(max, Math.max(min, value));
   23| }
   24| 
   25| function uniq<T>(items: T[]): T[] {
   26|   return Array.from(new Set(items));
   27| }
   28| 
   29| function inferSegmentsFromAssets(assets: string[]): string[] {
   30|   const segments = new Set<string>();
   31|   const lower = assets.map((a) => a.toLowerCase());
   32| 
   33|   if (lower.some((a) => a.includes("equity") || a.includes("tech"))) {
   34|     segments.add("tech_investors");
   35|   }
   36| 
   37|   if (lower.some((a) => a.includes("bond") || a.includes("treasury"))) {
   38|     segments.add("bond_investors");
   39|   }
   40| 
   41|   if (lower.some((a) => a.includes("bitcoin") || a.includes("crypto"))) {
   42|     segments.add("crypto_investors");
   43|   }
   44| 
   45|   return Array.from(segments);
   46| }

  138| async function computeMatchCounts(params: {
  139|   insightIds: string[];
  140|   userTags: string[];
  141| }): Promise<Map<string, number>> {
  142|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  143| 
  144|   const insightIds = uniq(params.insightIds.filter(Boolean));
  145|   const userTags = uniq(params.userTags.filter(Boolean));
  146| 
  147|   if (insightIds.length === 0 || userTags.length === 0) return new Map();
  148| 
  149|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  150|     .from("insight_tags")
  151|     .select("insight_id,tag")
  152|     .in("insight_id", insightIds)
  153|     .in("tag", userTags)
  154|     .limit(20000);
  155| 
  156|   if (error) {
  157|     throw new Error(`Failed to load insight tag matches: ${error.message}`);
  158|   }
  159| 
  160|   const rows = (data as InsightTagRow[] | null) ?? [];
  161|   const tagsByInsight = new Map<string, Set<string>>();
  162| 
  163|   for (const row of rows) {
  164|     const insightId = (row.insight_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  165|     const tag = (row.tag ?? "").toString().trim().toLowerCase();
  166|     if (!insightId || !tag) continue;
  167| 
  168|     let set = tagsByInsight.get(insightId);
  169|     if (!set) {
  170|       set = new Set<string>();
  171|       tagsByInsight.set(insightId, set);
  172|     }
  173| 
  174|     set.add(tag);
  175|   }
  176| 
  177|   const counts = new Map<string, number>();
  178|   for (const [insightId, set] of tagsByInsight.entries()) {
  179|     counts.set(insightId, set.size);
  180|   }
  181| 
  182|   return counts;
  183| }
  184| 
  185| async function filterExistingInsights(insightIds: string[]): Promise<Set<string>> {
  186|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  187| 
  188|   const unique = uniq(insightIds.filter(Boolean));
  189|   if (unique.length === 0) return new Set();
  190| 
  191|   const { data, error } = await supabase
  192|     .from("event_insights")
  193|     .select("id")
  194|     .in("id", unique)
  195|     .limit(5000);
  196| 
  197|   if (error) {
  198|     throw new Error(`Failed to load event_insights ids: ${error.message}`);
  199|   }
  200| 
  201|   const existing = new Set<string>();
  202|   for (const row of (data as Array<{ id: string }> | null) ?? []) {
  203|     if (row?.id) existing.add(row.id);
  204|   }
  205| 
  206|   return existing;
  207| }

  209| export async function runUserRelevanceEngine(): Promise<void> {
  210|   const supabase = createSupabaseServerClient();
  211| 
  212|   const portfolioRows = await loadUserPortfolios(2000);
  213|   if (portfolioRows.length === 0) return;
  214| 
  215|   const assetsByUser = new Map<string, string[]>();
  216|   for (const row of portfolioRows) {
  217|     const userId = (row.user_id ?? "").toString().trim();
  218|     const asset = (row.asset ?? "").toString().trim();
  219|     if (!userId || !asset) continue;
  220| 
  221|     const list = assetsByUser.get(userId) ?? [];
  222|     list.push(asset);
  223|     assetsByUser.set(userId, list);
  224|   }
  225| 
  226|   const userIds = Array.from(assetsByUser.keys()).slice(0, 50);
  227|   if (userIds.length === 0) return;
  228| 
  229|   for (const userId of userIds) {
  230|     const assets = uniq((assetsByUser.get(userId) ?? []).filter(Boolean));
  231| 
  232|     // 2) Fetch asset tags
  233|     const userTags = await loadTagsForAssets(assets);
  234| 
  235|     // Clear prior rows for idempotency.
  236|     const { error: deleteError } = await supabase
  237|       .from("user_relevance_index")
  238|       .delete()
  239|       .eq("user_id", userId);
  240| 
  241|     if (deleteError) {
  242|       throw new Error(`Failed to clear old relevance rows: ${deleteError.message}`);
  243|     }
  244| 
  245|     if (userTags.length === 0) {
  246|       const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  247|         event_type: "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED",
  248|         payload: { user_id: userId },
  249|       });
  250| 
  251|       if (emitError) {
  252|         throw new Error(
  253|           `Failed to emit USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED event: ${emitError.message}`,
  254|         );
  255|       }
  256| 
  257|       continue;
  258|     }
  259| 
  260|     // Clear prior edges for this user (delta propagation uses these edges).
  261|     const { error: deleteEdgesError } = await supabase
  262|       .from("insight_user_edges")
  263|       .delete()
  264|       .eq("user_id", userId);
  265| 
  266|     if (deleteEdgesError) {
  267|       throw new Error(
  268|         `Failed to clear old insight_user_edges rows: ${deleteEdgesError.message}`,
  269|       );
  270|     }
  271| 
  272|     // 3) Candidate insights
  273|     const tagCandidates = await loadCandidateInsightsFromTags(userTags);
  274| 
  275|     // Optional accelerator: union with segment-based candidates.
  276|     const segments = inferSegmentsFromAssets(assets);
  277|     const segmentCandidates = await loadCandidateInsightsFromSegments(segments);
  278| 
  279|     const candidateIds = uniq([...tagCandidates, ...segmentCandidates]).slice(0, 1000);
  280| 
  281|     if (candidateIds.length === 0) {
  282|       const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  283|         event_type: "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED",
  284|         payload: { user_id: userId, insight_ids: [] },
  285|       });
  286| 
  287|       if (emitError) {
  288|         throw new Error(
  289|           `Failed to emit USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED event: ${emitError.message}`,
  290|         );
  291|       }
  292| 
  293|       continue;
  294|     }
  295| 
  296|     // Ensure we only insert insights that actually exist.
  297|     const existing = await filterExistingInsights(candidateIds);
  298|     const existingCandidates = candidateIds.filter((id) => existing.has(id));
  299| 
  300|     if (existingCandidates.length === 0) {
  301|       const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  302|         event_type: "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED",
  303|         payload: { user_id: userId, insight_ids: [] },
  304|       });
  305| 
  306|       if (emitError) {
  307|         throw new Error(
  308|           `Failed to emit USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED event: ${emitError.message}`,
  309|         );
  310|       }
  311| 
  312|       continue;
  313|     }
  314| 
  315|     // 4) Compute relevance: matching_tags / total_asset_tags
  316|     const matchCounts = await computeMatchCounts({
  317|       insightIds: existingCandidates,
  318|       userTags,
  319|     });
  320| 
  321|     const scored = Array.from(matchCounts.entries())
  322|       .map(([insightId, matchCount]) => ({
  323|         insight_id: insightId,
  324|         relevance_score: clamp(0, matchCount / userTags.length, 1),
  325|       }))
  326|       .sort((a, b) => b.relevance_score - a.relevance_score)
  327|       .slice(0, 200);
  328| 
  329|     if (scored.length > 0) {
  330|       const inserts = scored.map((r) => ({
  331|         user_id: userId,
  332|         insight_id: r.insight_id,
  333|         relevance_score: r.relevance_score,
  334|       }));
  335| 
  336|       const { error: insertError } = await supabase
  337|         .from("user_relevance_index")
  338|         .insert(inserts);
  339| 
  340|       if (insertError) {
  341|         throw new Error(`Failed to insert relevance index: ${insertError.message}`);
  342|       }
  343| 
  344|       const { error: edgeInsertError } = await supabase
  345|         .from("insight_user_edges")
  346|         .insert(inserts);
  347| 
  348|       if (edgeInsertError) {
  349|         throw new Error(
  350|           `Failed to insert insight_user_edges rows: ${edgeInsertError.message}`,
  351|         );
  352|       }
  353|     }
  354| 
  355|     // 3) Emit update event to trigger feed engine
  356|     const changedInsightIds = scored.map((r) => r.insight_id);
  357|     const { error: emitError } = await supabase.from("pipeline_events").insert({
  358|       event_type: "USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED",
  359|       payload: { user_id: userId, insight_ids: changedInsightIds },
  360|     });
  361| 
  362|     if (emitError) {
  363|       throw new Error(`Failed to emit USER_RELEVANCE_UPDATED event: ${emitError.message}`);
  364|     }
  365|   }
  366| }

===== FILE: services\workerPool.ts =====

    1| export type WorkerPoolOptions = {
    2|   concurrency?: number;
    3| };
    4| 
    5| /**
    6|  * Runs async work with a fixed maximum concurrency.
    7|  *
    8|  * - Preserves input order for the returned results.
    9|  * - Rejects immediately on the first worker error.
   10|  */
   11| export async function workerPoolMap<T, R>(
   12|   items: T[],
   13|   worker: (item: T, index: number) => Promise<R>,
   14|   options?: WorkerPoolOptions,
   15| ): Promise<R[]> {
   16|   const concurrency = Math.max(1, Math.floor(options?.concurrency ?? 5));
   17|   if (items.length === 0) return [];
   18| 
   19|   const results: R[] = new Array(items.length);
   20|   let nextIndex = 0;
   21| 
   22|   const runners = new Array(Math.min(concurrency, items.length)).fill(null).map(async () => {
   23|     while (true) {
   24|       const index = nextIndex;
   25|       nextIndex += 1;
   26|       if (index >= items.length) return;
   27| 
   28|       results[index] = await worker(items[index], index);
   29|     }
   30|   });
   31| 
   32|   await Promise.all(runners);
   33|   return results;
   34| }
   35| 
   36| export async function workerPoolForEach<T>(
   37|   items: T[],
   38|   worker: (item: T, index: number) => Promise<void>,
   39|   options?: WorkerPoolOptions,
   40| ): Promise<void> {
   41|   await workerPoolMap(items, worker, options);
   42| }

===== FILE: simulation\scenarioEngine.ts =====

    1| import { solveForN } from "@/lib/solver";
    2| 
    3| export type FinancialInputs = {
    4|   currentSavings: number;
    5|   monthlySavings: number;
    6|   expectedReturn: number; // decimal (e.g. 0.10)
    7|   targetAmount: number;
    8|   timeHorizon: number;
    9| };
   10| 
   11| export type Scenario = {
   12|   label: string;
   13|   modify: (inputs: FinancialInputs) => FinancialInputs;
   14| };
   15| 
   16| export type ScenarioResult = {
   17|   label: string;
   18|   monthsImproved: number;
   19| };
   20| 
   21| /**
   22|  * Runs scenarios by applying small modifications to inputs and comparing
   23|  * the time-to-target vs the baseline inputs.
   24|  *
   25|  * Note: This returns raw deltas (can be negative or zero). Filtering/sorting is
   26|  * intentionally left to the caller, because some scenario UIs need to show
   27|  * worse-case environments (e.g. conservative markets).
   28|  */
   29| export function runScenarios(
   30|   inputs: FinancialInputs,
   31|   scenarios: Scenario[],
   32| ): ScenarioResult[] {
   33|   const baselineYears = solveForN(
   34|     inputs.currentSavings,
   35|     inputs.monthlySavings,
   36|     inputs.expectedReturn,
   37|     inputs.targetAmount,
   38|   );
   39| 
   40|   return scenarios.map((scenario) => {
   41|     const modified = scenario.modify(inputs);
   42| 
   43|     const newYears = solveForN(
   44|       modified.currentSavings,
   45|       modified.monthlySavings,
   46|       modified.expectedReturn,
   47|       modified.targetAmount,
   48|     );
   49| 
   50|     const monthsImproved = Math.round((baselineYears - newYears) * 12);
   51| 
   52|     return { label: scenario.label, monthsImproved };
   53|   });
   54| }

    1| -- Trajectos — Supabase setup (SQL)

===== FILE: supabase\migrations\0010_vector_search_function.sql =====

    1| CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION match_macro_events(
    2|   query_embedding vector(384),
    3|   match_threshold float,
    4|   match_count int
    5| )
    6| RETURNS TABLE (
    7|   id text,
    8|   title text,
    9|   similarity float
   10| )
   11| LANGUAGE sql STABLE
   12| AS $$
   13|   SELECT
   14|     id,
   15|     title,
   16|     1 - (embedding <=> query_embedding) AS similarity
   17|   FROM macro_events_raw
   18|   WHERE embedding IS NOT NULL
   19|   AND 1 - (embedding <=> query_embedding) > match_threshold
   20|   ORDER BY embedding <=> query_embedding
   21|   LIMIT match_count;
   22| $$;

===== FILE: supabase\migrations\0015_time_bucket.sql =====

    1| -- Temporal bucketing for macro events (10-minute buckets)
    2| 
    3| ALTER TABLE public.macro_events_raw
    4| ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS time_bucket timestamptz;
    5| 
    6| -- Backfill existing rows
    7| UPDATE public.macro_events_raw
    8| SET time_bucket = to_timestamp(floor(extract(epoch from published_at) / 600) * 600)
    9| WHERE time_bucket IS NULL;
   10| 
   11| CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION public.set_macro_events_raw_time_bucket()
   12| RETURNS trigger
   13| LANGUAGE plpgsql
   14| AS $$
   15| BEGIN
   16|   IF NEW.published_at IS NULL THEN
   17|     RETURN NEW;
   18|   END IF;
   19| 
   20|   NEW.time_bucket := to_timestamp(floor(extract(epoch from NEW.published_at) / 600) * 600);
   21|   RETURN NEW;
   22| END;
   23| $$;
   24| 
   25| DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS macro_events_raw_time_bucket_trg ON public.macro_events_raw;
   26| 
   27| CREATE TRIGGER macro_events_raw_time_bucket_trg
   28| BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE OF published_at
   29| ON public.macro_events_raw
   30| FOR EACH ROW
   31| EXECUTE FUNCTION public.set_macro_events_raw_time_bucket();

===== FILE: supabase\migrations\0016_vector_search_bucket_filter.sql =====

    1| -- Bucket-filtered vector search overload (keeps existing match_macro_events intact)
    2| 
    3| CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION match_macro_events(
    4|   query_embedding vector(384),
    5|   match_threshold float,
    6|   match_count int,
    7|   bucket_filter timestamptz
    8| )
    9| RETURNS TABLE (
   10|   id text,
   11|   title text,
   12|   similarity float
   13| )
   14| LANGUAGE sql STABLE
   15| AS $$
   16|   SELECT
   17|     id,
   18|     title,
   19|     1 - (embedding <=> query_embedding) AS similarity
   20|   FROM macro_events_raw
   21|   WHERE embedding IS NOT NULL
   22|     AND 1 - (embedding <=> query_embedding) > match_threshold
   23|     AND (bucket_filter IS NULL OR time_bucket = bucket_filter)
   24|   ORDER BY embedding <=> query_embedding
   25|   LIMIT match_count;
   26| $$;

===== FILE: supabase\migrations\0024_emit_insight_created.sql =====

    1| -- Emits a pipeline event whenever an insight row is created.
    2| -- This enables downstream streaming stages (e.g. allocation engine) without
    3| -- modifying the existing insight engine code.
    4| 
    5| CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION emit_insight_created_pipeline_event()
    6| RETURNS trigger
    7| LANGUAGE plpgsql
    8| AS $$
    9| BEGIN
   10|   INSERT INTO pipeline_events (event_type, payload, processed)
   11|   VALUES (
   12|     'INSIGHT_CREATED',
   13|     jsonb_build_object('cluster_id', NEW.cluster_id),
   14|     false
   15|   );
   16| 
   17|   RETURN NEW;
   18| END;
   19| $$;
   20| 
   21| DROP TRIGGER IF EXISTS trg_event_insights_emit_pipeline_event ON event_insights;
   22| 
   23| CREATE TRIGGER trg_event_insights_emit_pipeline_event
   24| AFTER INSERT ON event_insights
   25| FOR EACH ROW
   26| EXECUTE FUNCTION emit_insight_created_pipeline_event();

===== FILE: supabase\migrations\0034_pipeline_events_notify.sql =====

    1| -- Emits a real-time notification whenever a pipeline event is created.
    2| -- Channel: pipeline_event_created
    3| -- Payload: { event_id, event_type, cluster_id }
    4| 
    5| create or replace function public.notify_pipeline_event_created()
    6| returns trigger
    7| language plpgsql
    8| as $$
    9| declare
   10|   v_cluster_id text;
   11|   v_payload text;
   12| begin
   13|   -- cluster_id is carried in the JSON payload for most pipeline events.
   14|   v_cluster_id := nullif(trim(coalesce((new.payload ->> 'cluster_id')::text, '')), '');
   15| 
   16|   v_payload := json_build_object(
   17|     'event_id', new.id,
   18|     'event_type', new.event_type,
   19|     'cluster_id', v_cluster_id
   20|   )::text;
   21| 
   22|   perform pg_notify('pipeline_event_created', v_payload);
   23|   return new;
   24| end;
   25| $$;
   26| 
   27| -- Drop + recreate to be idempotent.
   28| drop trigger if exists trg_pipeline_event_created_notify on public.pipeline_events;
   29| 
   30| create trigger trg_pipeline_event_created_notify
   31| after insert on public.pipeline_events
   32| for each row
   33| execute function public.notify_pipeline_event_created();

===== FILE: supabase\migrations\0038_clustering_checkpoints.sql =====

    1| -- Ensures clustering_checkpoints exists with the expected schema.
    2| -- Safe to run on databases where the table (or some columns) already exist.
    3| 
    4| CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS public.clustering_checkpoints (
    5|   id uuid PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
    6|   last_processed_event timestamptz,
    7|   created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now()
    8| );
    9| 
   10| -- If an older migration created the table with a different schema, add missing columns.
   11| ALTER TABLE public.clustering_checkpoints
   12|   ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS last_processed_event timestamptz;
   13| 
   14| ALTER TABLE public.clustering_checkpoints
   15|   ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS created_at timestamptz DEFAULT now();
   16| 
   17| -- Backfill from legacy column name if present.
   18| DO $$
   19| BEGIN
   20|   IF EXISTS (
   21|     SELECT 1
   22|     FROM information_schema.columns
   23|     WHERE table_schema = 'public'
   24|       AND table_name = 'clustering_checkpoints'
   25|       AND column_name = 'last_processed_at'
   26|   ) THEN
   27|     UPDATE public.clustering_checkpoints
   28|       SET last_processed_event = last_processed_at
   29|       WHERE last_processed_event IS NULL
   30|         AND last_processed_at IS NOT NULL;
   31|   END IF;
   32| END $$;
   33| 
   34| CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_clustering_checkpoints_last_processed_event
   35|   ON public.clustering_checkpoints (last_processed_event);
